## Phật giáo Việt Nam

Tịnh pháp giới chân ngôn:  
Án lam. Án lam. Án lam.

Tịnh khẩu nghiệp chân ngôn:  
Tu rị tu rị, ma ha tu rị, tu tu rị, ta bà ha.

Tịnh tam nghiệp chân ngôn:  
Án ta phạ bà phạ, thuật đà ta phạ, đạt ma ta phạ, bà phạ thuật độ hám.

Nam mô Bổn Sư Thích Ca Mâu Ni Phật.  
Nam mô Bổn Sư Thích Ca Mâu Ni Phật.  
Nam mô Bổn Sư Thích Ca Mâu Ni Phật.

Đệ tử này chí tâm đảnh lễ:  
Nam mô tận hư không biến pháp giới quá, hiện, vị lai thập phương chư Phật.  
Nam mô tận hư không biến pháp giới quá, hiện, vị lai thập phương chư Tôn Pháp.  
Nam mô tận hư không biến pháp giới quá, hiện, vị lai thập phương Hiền Thánh Tăng.

Nguyện thử diệu hương vân,  
Biến mãn thập phương giới,  
Cúng dường nhất thiết Phật,  
Tôn Pháp chư Bồ Tát,  
Vô biên Thanh Văn chúng,  
Cập nhất thiết Thánh Hiền.

Phát nguyện:  
Đệ tử này chí tâm quy mạng Tam Bảo, phát nguyện cho việc cầu chức, tham dự phỏng vấn được thuận duyên theo chánh pháp; khi lâm trường tâm ý sáng suốt, lời nói hòa nhã tự nhiên, trình bày chân thật, gặp được sự hiểu biết và trân trọng đúng đắn, tìm được nhân duyên nghề nghiệp lành thiện, nuôi sống bằng chánh mạng, lợi mình lợi người.  
Nguyện việc thành tựu nếu đủ duyên là do phước đức, trí tuệ, sự chuẩn bị và thiện nghiệp hội tụ; không cầu cưỡng ép lòng người, không đoạt phước phần của ai, không làm tổn hại danh dự, cơ hội, tài sản hay đời sống của người khác.

Sám hối:  
Vãng tích sở tạo chư ác nghiệp,  
Giai do vô thỉ tham sân si,  
Tùng thân ngữ ý chi sở sanh,  
Nhất thiết ngã kim giai sám hối.

Tội tùng tâm khởi tương tâm sám,  
Tâm nhược diệt thời tội diệc vong,  
Tội vong tâm diệt lưỡng câu không,  
Thị tắc danh vi chân sám hối.

Tam quy:  
Tự quy y Phật, đương nguyện chúng sanh, thể giải đại đạo, phát vô thượng tâm.  
Tự quy y Pháp, đương nguyện chúng sanh, thâm nhập kinh tạng, trí tuệ như hải.  
Tự quy y Tăng, đương nguyện chúng sanh, thống lý đại chúng, nhất thiết vô ngại.

Chú Đại Bi:  
Nam mô hắc ra đát na đa ra dạ da.  
Nam mô a rị da bà lô yết đế thước bát ra da.  
Bồ đề tát đỏa bà da.  
Ma ha tát đỏa bà da.  
Ma ha ca lô ni ca da.  
Án.  
Tát bàn ra phạt duệ.  
Số đát na đát tỏa.  
Nam mô tất kiết lật đỏa y mông a rị da.  
Bà lô kiết đế thất Phật ra lăng đà bà.  
Nam mô na ra cẩn trì.  
Hê rị ma ha bàn đa sa mế.  
Tát bà a tha đậu du bằng.  
A thệ dựng.  
Tát bà tát đa na ma bà tát đa, na ma bà già.  
Ma phạt đạt đậu.  
Đát điệt tha.  
Án a bà lô hê.  
Lô ca đế.  
Ca ra đế.  
Di hê rị.  
Ma ha bồ đề tát đỏa.  
Tát bà tát bà.  
Ma ra ma ra.  
Ma hê ma hê rị đà dựng.  
Câu lô câu lô yết mông.  
Độ lô độ lô phạt xà da đế.  
Ma ha phạt xà da đế.  
Đà ra đà ra.  
Địa rị ni.  
Thất Phật ra da.  
Giá ra giá ra.  
Mạ mạ phạt ma ra.  
Mục đế lệ.  
Y hê y hê.  
Thất na thất na.  
A ra sâm Phật ra xá lợi.  
Phạt sa phạt sâm.  
Phật ra xá da.  
Hô lô hô lô ma ra.  
Hô lô hô lô hê rị.  
Ta ra ta ra.  
Tất rị tất rị.  
Tô rô tô rô.  
Bồ đề dạ bồ đề dạ.  
Bồ đà dạ bồ đà dạ.  
Di đế rị dạ.  
Na ra cẩn trì.  
Địa rị sắt ni na.  
Ba dạ ma na.  
Ta bà ha.  
Tất đà dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Ma ha tất đà dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Tất đà du nghệ.  
Thất bàn ra dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Na ra cẩn trì.  
Ta bà ha.  
Ma ra na ra.  
Ta bà ha.  
Tất ra tăng a mục khư da.  
Ta bà ha.  
Ta bà ma ha a tất đà dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Giả kiết ra a tất đà dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Ba đà ma yết tất đà dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Na ra cẩn trì bàn đà ra dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Ma bà lợi thắng yết ra dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Nam mô hắc ra đát na đa ra dạ da.  
Nam mô a rị da bà lô yết đế thước bàn ra dạ.  
Ta bà ha.  
Án tất điện đô.  
Mạn đa ra.  
Bạt đà dạ.  
Ta bà ha.

Bát Nhã Tâm Kinh:  
Quán Tự Tại Bồ Tát hành thâm Bát Nhã Ba La Mật Đa thời, chiếu kiến ngũ uẩn giai không, độ nhất thiết khổ ách.  
Xá Lợi Tử, sắc bất dị không, không bất dị sắc, sắc tức thị không, không tức thị sắc, thọ tưởng hành thức diệc phục như thị.  
Xá Lợi Tử, thị chư pháp không tướng, bất sanh bất diệt, bất cấu bất tịnh, bất tăng bất giảm.  
Thị cố không trung vô sắc, vô thọ tưởng hành thức, vô nhãn nhĩ tỷ thiệt thân ý, vô sắc thanh hương vị xúc pháp, vô nhãn giới nãi chí vô ý thức giới, vô vô minh diệc vô vô minh tận, nãi chí vô lão tử diệc vô lão tử tận, vô khổ tập diệt đạo, vô trí diệc vô đắc.  
Dĩ vô sở đắc cố, Bồ Đề Tát Đỏa y Bát Nhã Ba La Mật Đa cố, tâm vô quái ngại; vô quái ngại cố, vô hữu khủng bố, viễn ly điên đảo mộng tưởng, cứu cánh Niết Bàn.  
Tam thế chư Phật y Bát Nhã Ba La Mật Đa cố, đắc A Nậu Đa La Tam Miệu Tam Bồ Đề.  
Cố tri Bát Nhã Ba La Mật Đa thị đại thần chú, thị đại minh chú, thị vô thượng chú, thị vô đẳng đẳng chú, năng trừ nhất thiết khổ, chân thật bất hư.  
Cố thuyết Bát Nhã Ba La Mật Đa chú, tức thuyết chú viết:  
Yết đế yết đế, ba la yết đế, ba la tăng yết đế, bồ đề tát bà ha.

Niệm danh hiệu:  
Nam mô Đại Bi Quán Thế Âm Bồ Tát.  
Nam mô Đại Bi Quán Thế Âm Bồ Tát.  
Nam mô Đại Bi Quán Thế Âm Bồ Tát.

Nam mô Văn Thù Sư Lợi Bồ Tát.  
Nam mô Văn Thù Sư Lợi Bồ Tát.  
Nam mô Văn Thù Sư Lợi Bồ Tát.

Nam mô A Di Đà Phật.  
Nam mô A Di Đà Phật.  
Nam mô A Di Đà Phật.

Hồi hướng riêng:  
Nguyện đem công đức trì tụng này hồi hướng cho việc phỏng vấn cầu chức được an ổn, sáng suốt, đúng thời, đúng duyên; nguyện tâm không tán loạn, miệng nói lời chân thật hòa ái, ý không kiêu mạn cũng không tự ti; nguyện các chướng ngại do vô minh, sợ hãi, hấp tấp, vọng tưởng đều tiêu dung; nguyện gặp thiện tri thức, gặp người biết xét đúng năng lực và phẩm hạnh; nguyện chánh duyên nghề nghiệp thành tựu theo nhân quả lành, không trái giới, không trái pháp.

Nguyện tiêu tam chướng trừ phiền não,  
Nguyện đắc trí tuệ chân minh liễu,  
Phổ nguyện tội chướng tất tiêu trừ,  
Thế thế thường hành Bồ Tát đạo.

Nguyện sanh Tây Phương Tịnh Độ trung,  
Cửu phẩm liên hoa vi phụ mẫu,  
Hoa khai kiến Phật ngộ vô sanh,  
Bất thối Bồ Tát vi bạn lữ.

Nguyện đem công đức này,  
Hướng về khắp tất cả,  
Đệ tử và chúng sanh,  
Đều trọn thành Phật đạo.

Tam tự quy:  
Tự quy y Phật, nguyện cho chúng sanh, hiểu thấu đạo cả, phát tâm vô thượng.  
Tự quy y Pháp, nguyện cho chúng sanh, thâm nhập kinh tạng, trí tuệ như biển.  
Tự quy y Tăng, nguyện cho chúng sanh, quản lý đại chúng, hết thảy không ngại.

---

## 拜罗婆派（克什米尔湿婆派）

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ

śrī-gurubhyo namaḥ  
śrī-paramaśivāya bhairavāya namaḥ

ahaṃ śuddha-bhāvena āgāmi-sevā-nimitta-saṃvāda-parīkṣā-siddhyarthaṃ  
sphuṭa-smṛti-prasāda-pratyutpanna-buddhi-vāk-sauṣṭhava-anukūla-darśana-yogyakarma-lābhārthaṃ  
na parasya bhāgyāpahāreṇa, na parasya hānyā, na vaśīkaraṇa-doṣeṇa,  
kevalaṃ dharma-yogya-maṅgala-prāptyarthaṃ  
śrī-bhairava-paramaśiva-smaraṇaṃ karomi.

oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya

oṃ bhairavāya namaḥ  
oṃ bhairavāya namaḥ  
oṃ bhairavāya namaḥ

caitanyam ātmā

jñānaṃ bandhaḥ

udyamo bhairavaḥ

yataḥ karaṇavargo 'yaṃ vimūḍho 'mūḍhavat svayam |  
sahāntareṇa cakreṇa pravṛttas tiṣṭhate yataḥ ||

tasmāt sarvaprayatnena prabodhyo hṛdayeśvaraḥ |  
ekānenaiva yuktena spanda-tattvaṃ vivicyate ||

hṛdaye bhairava-prakāśaḥ prasīdatu |  
vāci śiva-śaktiḥ prasīdatu |  
manasi caitanya-prasādaḥ prasīdatu |  
saṃvāde spaṣṭatā, dhairyaṃ, mādhuryaṃ, satyaṃ ca bhavatu |  
yathā-yogyaṃ guṇa-darśanaṃ, sat-kārya-prāptiḥ, śubha-saṃbandhaḥ ca bhavatu ||

oṃ tryambakaṃ yajāmahe sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam |  
urvārukam iva bandhanān mṛtyor mukṣīya mā'mṛtāt ||

namaḥ śivāya ca śivatarāya ca

yat kiñcid atra mantra-varṇa-svara-bhaṅga-doṣaṃ jātaṃ  
tat sarvaṃ śrī-bhairava-paramaśiva-prasādena kṣamyatām.

idaṃ japa-stotra-smaraṇaṃ  
āgāmi-saṃvāda-parīkṣā-maṅgala-siddhaye  
citta-prasāda-vāk-sauṣṭhava-yogyakarma-lābhāya  
sarvabhūta-hita-śāntyai ca samarpayāmi.

oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ

---

## 毗湿奴派（Gaudiya / ISKCON 等）

oṁ ajñāna-timirāndhasya jñānāñjana-śalākayā  
cakṣur unmīlitaṁ yena tasmai śrī-gurave namaḥ

nama oṁ viṣṇu-pādāya kṛṣṇa-preṣṭhāya bhū-tale  
śrīmate bhaktivedānta-svāmin iti nāmine

vande śrī-kṛṣṇa-caitanya-nityānandau sahoditau  
gauḍodaye puṣpavantau citrau śandau tamo-nudau

śrī-kṛṣṇa-caitanya prabhu-nityānanda  
śrī-advaita gadādhara śrīvāsādi-gaura-bhakta-vṛnda

he śrī guru, he śrī gaura, he śrī śrī rādhā-kṛṣṇa,  
愿求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，谈吐自若，得遇赏识，觅得良缘；以不求伤害、不求操控、不凭圣名造罪之心，归依圣名。愿此成就不夺他人机缘福报，不损他人正当利益，唯愿依正法、依恩典而得相应之门开启。

Hare Kṛṣṇa Hare Kṛṣṇa  
Kṛṣṇa Kṛṣṇa Hare Hare  
Hare Rāma Hare Rāma  
Rāma Rāma Hare Hare

愿面试之时心念安住，言语清净，所学所能得以如实呈现；愿与面试者相见时互怀尊重，若此职位与正当生计、奉献生活相合，愿得善缘成就；若另有更适宜之路，亦愿蒙引导而不迷失、不执著。

tṛṇād api sunīcena taror iva sahiṣṇunā  
amāninā mānadena kīrtanīyaḥ sadā hariḥ

na dhanaṁ na janaṁ na sundarīṁ  
kavitāṁ vā jagad-īśa kāmaye  
mama janmani janmanīśvare  
bhavatād bhaktir ahaitukī tvayi

idaṁ kīrtanaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇārpaṇam astu  
sarveṣāṁ maṅgalaṁ bhavatu  
vaiṣṇava-aparādha-nāma-aparādha-kṣamā-prārthanāṁ karomi

Hare Kṛṣṇa Hare Kṛṣṇa  
Kṛṣṇa Kṛṣṇa Hare Hare  
Hare Rāma Hare Rāma  
Rāma Rāma Hare Hare

---

## कबीर पंथ

Sāhib Bandagī.

Satguru Kabīr Sāhib kī jai.  
Sāhib, Satnām.  
Rām, Rām.

He Satguru Kabīr Sāhib,  
man, vachan aur kāyā ko satya, dayā aur sahaj mẽ rakhkar vinay hai.  
Āj jo naukrī ke sākṣātkār kā kārya āge hai, usmẽ antar-man nirmal rahe, buddhi spaṣṭ rahe, vachan sahaj aur niḍar nikle.  
Jo yogya avasar ho, vah satya-mārg se mile; jo milan hitkārī ho, vah dayā, nyāy aur maryādā mẽ siddh ho.

Guru Govind dou khaṛe, kāke lāgū̃ pāy;  
balihārī guru āpane, Govind diyo batāy.

Pothī paṛh paṛh jag muā, paṇḍit bhayā na koy;  
ḍhāī ākhar prem kā, paṛhe so paṇḍit hoy.

Kal kare so āj kar, āj kare so ab;  
pal mẽ pralaya hoyegī, bahuri karegā kab.

Satguru Sāhib,  
is sākṣātkār ke kṣaṇ mẽ bhay, bhram, ahaṃkār, lobh aur asatya kā bandhan chhūṭe.  
Jo prashn āve, usmẽ vivek rahe; jo uttar nikle, vah satya, saṃyam aur sahaj prem se nikle.  
Dekhanewālõ ke hṛday mẽ nyāy aur prasannatā ho; yogya guṇ pahchāne jāẽ; uchit rojgār kā dvār khule.  
Kisī kā adhikār na chhine, kisī kī rojī na ṭūṭe, kisī ko hāni na ho; keval satya-yogya bhāg aur śubh sambandh mile.

Sāī̃ itnā dījiye, jāmẽ kuṭum samāy;  
maĩ bhī bhūkhā na rahū̃, sādhu na bhūkhā jāy.

Moko kahā̃ ḍhū̃ḍhe re bande, maĩ to tere pās mẽ;  
nā tīrath mẽ, nā mūrat mẽ, nā ekānt nivās mẽ.  
Nā mandir mẽ, nā masjid mẽ, nā Kābe Kailās mẽ;  
maĩ to tere pās mẽ bande, maĩ to tere pās mẽ.

Prem galī ati sā̃karī, tā mẽ do na samāy;  
jab maĩ thā tab Hari nahī̃, ab Hari hai maĩ nāy.

Dukh mẽ sumiran sab kare, sukh mẽ kare na koy;  
jo sukh mẽ sumiran kare, to dukh kāhe ko hoy.

Sāhib, Satnām.  
Rām, Rām.

Jo kuchh bhī śubh ho, vah sab jīv ke hit mẽ samarpit.  
Nirguṇ Sāhib ke nām mẽ, Satguru ke smaraṇ mẽ, satya-dayā-sahaj-vairāgya mẽ man ṭike.  
Na jāti kā garv, na rūp kā mān, na bāharī āḍambar kā bharam; keval Satnām, satya-vachan, dayā-bhāv aur guru-bhakti kā āśray rahe.

Satguru Kabīr Sāhib kī jai.  
Sāhib Bandagī.

---

## 耆那教 Pratikraman / Samayika

Namo Arihantāṇaṃ  
Namo Siddhāṇaṃ  
Namo Āyariyāṇaṃ  
Namo Uvajjhāyāṇaṃ  
Namo Loe Savva-Sāhūṇaṃ  
Eso Pañca Namokkāro  
Savva-Pāvappaṇāsaṇo  
Maṅgalāṇaṃ ca Savvesiṃ  
Paḍhamaṃ Havai Maṅgalaṃ  

Karemi bhante sāmāiyaṃ,  
savvaṃ sāvajjaṃ jogaṃ paccakkhāmi,  
jāva niyamaṃ pajjuvāsāmi,  
duvihaṃ tiviheṇaṃ,  
maṇeṇaṃ vāyāe kāeṇaṃ,  
na karemi na kārāvemi,  
tassa bhante paḍikkamāmi,  
nindāmi, garahāmi,  
appāṇaṃ vosirāmi.  

愿求职面试一切顺利；临场清明，谈吐自若；以真实、谦和、无害之心应对问答，得遇正当赏识，觅得相宜岗位因缘。不夺他人机会，不损他人福报，不以虚言欺取，不以贪著逼迫，唯愿善业成熟，正命成就。  

Icchāmi paḍikkamium iriyāvahiyāe virāhaṇāe.  
Gamanāgamane pāṇakkamaṇe,  
bīyakkamaṇe, hariyakkamaṇe,  
osā-uṭṭiṅga-paṇaga-daga-maṭṭi-makkadā-santāṇa-saṅkamaṇe.  
Je me jīvā virāhiyā,  
egindiyā, beindiyā, teindiyā, cauindiyā, pañcindiyā,  
abhihayā, vattiyā, lesiyā, saṅghāiyā, saṅghaṭṭiyā,  
pariyāviyā, kilāmiyā, uddaviyā,  
ṭhāṇāo ṭhāṇaṃ saṅkāmiyā,  
jīvitāo vavaroviyā,  
tassa micchā mi dukkaḍaṃ.  

Tassa uttarī-karaṇeṇaṃ,  
pāyacchitta-karaṇeṇaṃ,  
visohi-karaṇeṇaṃ,  
visallī-karaṇeṇaṃ,  
pāvāṇaṃ kammāṇaṃ nigghāyaṇaṭṭhāe,  
ṭhāmi kāussaggaṃ.  

Annattha usasieṇaṃ, nīsasieṇaṃ,  
khāsieṇaṃ, chīeṇaṃ, jambhāieṇaṃ,  
uḍḍueṇaṃ, vāya-nisaggeṇaṃ,  
bhamalieṇaṃ, pittamucchāe,  
suhumehiṃ aṅga-sañcālehiṃ,  
suhumehiṃ khela-sañcālehiṃ,  
suhumehiṃ diṭṭhi-sañcālehiṃ,  
evamāiehiṃ āgārehiṃ  
abhaggo avirāhio hujja me kāussaggo.  
Jāva arihaṃtāṇaṃ bhagavaṃtāṇaṃ namukkāreṇaṃ na pāremi,  
tāva kāyaṃ ṭhāṇeṇaṃ,  
moṇeṇaṃ, jhāṇeṇaṃ,  
appāṇaṃ vosirāmi.  

Namo Arihantāṇaṃ  
Namo Siddhāṇaṃ  
Namo Āyariyāṇaṃ  
Namo Uvajjhāyāṇaṃ  
Namo Loe Savva-Sāhūṇaṃ  

Logassa ujjoyagare,  
dhamma-titthayare jiṇe;  
arihaṃte kittaissami,  
cauvīsaṃ pi kevalī.  

Usabham Ajiaṃ ca vande,  
Sambhavam Abhinandanaṃ ca Sumaiṃ ca;  
Paumappahaṃ Supāsaṃ,  
Jiṇaṃ ca Candappahaṃ vande.  

Suvihiṃ ca Pupphadantaṃ,  
Sīala-Sijjaṃsa-Vāsupujjaṃ ca;  
Vimalaṃ Anantaṃ ca Jiṇaṃ,  
Dhammaṃ Santiṃ ca vandāmi.  

Kunthuṃ Araṃ ca Malliṃ,  
Munisuvvayaṃ Nami-Jiṇaṃ ca vandāmi;  
Ariṭṭhanemiṃ Pāsaṃ,  
Vaddhamāṇaṃ ca vandāmi.  

Evam mae abhithuā,  
vihuya-raya-malā pahīṇa-jara-maraṇā;  
cauvīsaṃ pi jiṇavarā,  
titthayarā me pasīyantu.  

Kittiya-vandiya-mahiyā,  
je e logassa uttamā siddhā;  
ārugga-bohi-lābhaṃ,  
samāhi-vara-muttamaṃ dentu.  

Candesu nimmalayarā,  
āiccesu ahiyaṃ payāsayarā;  
sāgara-vara-gambhīrā,  
siddhā siddhiṃ mama disantu.  

Maṇeṇaṃ vāyāe kāeṇaṃ,  
kayaṃ, kāritaṃ, anumodiyaṃ,  
rāga-dosa-moha-vasena,  
asacca-vayaṇeṇa vā,  
pariggaha-taṇhāe vā,  
para-hite virāhaṇāe vā,  
je me pāvā joga uppannā,  
tassa micchā mi dukkaḍaṃ.  

Khamemi savva-jīve,  
savve jīvā khamantu me;  
mittī me savva-bhūesu,  
veraṃ majjha na keṇai.  

Khamemi, khamāve-mi,  
micchā mi dukkaḍaṃ.  

Namo Arihantāṇaṃ  
Namo Siddhāṇaṃ  
Namo Āyariyāṇaṃ  
Namo Uvajjhāyāṇaṃ  
Namo Loe Savva-Sāhūṇaṃ  
Eso Pañca Namokkāro  
Savva-Pāvappaṇāsaṇo  
Maṅgalāṇaṃ ca Savvesiṃ  
Paḍhamaṃ Havai Maṅgalaṃ  

Savvaṃ sāvajjaṃ jogaṃ paccakkhāmi;  
maṇeṇaṃ vāyāe kāeṇaṃ,  
nindāmi, garahāmi,  
appāṇaṃ vosirāmi.  

Khamemi savva-jīve,  
savve jīvā khamantu me;  
mittī me savva-bhūesu,  
veraṃ majjha na keṇai.  

Micchāmi Dukkaḍaṃ.

---

## कौल

oṃ śrī-gurubhyo namaḥ ।  
oṃ gurave namaḥ ।  
gurur brahmā gurur viṣṇuḥ gurur devo maheśvaraḥ ।  
guruḥ sākṣāt parabrahma tasmai śrīgurave namaḥ ॥

oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ ।  
vakratuṇḍa mahākāya sūryakoṭisamaprabha ।  
nirvighnaṃ kuru me deva sarvakāryeṣu sarvadā ॥

mama upātta-samasta-durita-kṣaya-dvāra  
śrī-parādevī-prītyarthaṃ  
udyoga-sākṣātkāra-kārye  
tatkāla-prasanna-citta-siddhyarthaṃ  
svābhāvika-sphuṭa-vāk-pravṛttyarthaṃ  
guṇa-parijñātṛ-prasāda-prāptyarthaṃ  
śubha-yogyāvasara-lābhārthaṃ  
idaṃ prārthanā-japaṃ kariṣye ॥

oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ parādevyai namaḥ ।  
oṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ kulāyai namaḥ ।  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।  
oṃ śrī-mātṛkāyai namaḥ ॥

oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ parādevyai namaḥ ।  
oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ parādevyai namaḥ ।  
oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ parādevyai namaḥ ॥

he parādevī, he kula-mātṛke,  
asmin udyoga-sākṣātkāra-viṣaye  
anugrahaṃ kuru kuru ।  
śāntiṃ kuru kuru ।  
rakṣāṃ kuru kuru ।  
citta-prasādaṃ dehi ।  
vāk-sauṣṭhavaṃ dehi ।  
dhairyaṃ dehi ।  
samyag-buddhiṃ dehi ।  
ucita-kāle ucita-vākyaṃ dehi ।  
sajjana-dṛṣṭau mādhuryaṃ dehi ।  
śubha-saṃvādaṃ dehi ।  
yathārhaṃ śubha-yogaṃ dehi ॥

nānyasya bhāgya-hānyai,  
nānyasya sthāna-bhraṃśāya,  
nānyasya duḥkhāya vā;  
kevalaṃ dharmya-śubha-kārya-siddhyai,  
paraspara-hita-saṃpattaye,  
śivā-śiva-prasāda-lābhāya ॥

tryambakaṃ yajāmahe sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam ।  
urvārukam iva bandhanān mṛtyor mukṣīya mā'mṛtāt ॥

sarve bhavantu sukhinaḥ sarve santu nirāmayāḥ ।  
sarve bhadrāṇi paśyantu mā kaścid duḥkhabhāg bhavet ॥

yat kṛtaṃ tu mayā devi mantra-hīnaṃ kriyā-hīnam ।  
tat sarvaṃ pūrṇatāṃ yātu tvat-prasādāt parāmbike ॥

kāyena vācā manasendriyair vā  
buddhyātmanā vā prakṛteḥ svabhāvāt ।  
karomi yad yat sakalaṃ parasmai  
śrī-parādevyai samarpaṇam astu ॥

etat phalaṃ śānti-rakṣā-prāyaścitta-rūpeṇa  
sarva-bhūta-hitaṃ bhavatu ।  
kula-guru-devatā-prasādena  
sarva-vighnāḥ śāmyantu,  
sarve pāśāḥ śivāyaiva vimucyantām ॥

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ ॥

---

## ಲಿಂಗಾಯತ

ಓಂ ಶ್ರೀ ಗುರುಭ್ಯೋ ನಮಃ ।  
ಓಂ ಶ್ರೀ ಲಿಂಗಾಯ ನಮಃ ।  
ಓಂ ಶ್ರೀ ಜಂಗಮಾಯ ನಮಃ ।  

oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।  

ಇಂದು ಉದ್ಯೋಗ ಸಂದರ್ಶನವು ಶುಭವಾಗಿ ಸಾಗಲೆಂದು,  
ಕ್ಷಣದಲ್ಲಿ ಮನಸ್ಸು ನಿರ್ಮಲವಾಗಲೆಂದು, ಮಾತು ಸ್ವಚ್ಛವಾಗಿ ಹರಿಯಲೆಂದು,  
ಯೋಗ್ಯರಾದವರ ದೃಷ್ಟಿಯಲ್ಲಿ ಸತ್ಯಕಾಯಕದ ಮೌಲ್ಯ ಕಾಣಿಸಲೆಂದು,  
ಸದುಪಾಯದ ಉದ್ಯೋಗ-ಸಂಬಂಧ ದೊರಕಲೆಂದು,  
ಇಷ್ಟಲಿಂಗ ಸಾಕ್ಷಿಯಾಗಿ ಸಂಕಲ್ಪ ಮಾಡುತ್ತೇವೆ ।  

ಇದು ಯಾರ ಹಕ್ಕನ್ನೂ ಕಸಿದುಕೊಳ್ಳುವ ಆಶೆಯಲ್ಲ;  
ಯಾರ ಕಾಯಕವನ್ನೂ ಕುಗ್ಗಿಸುವ ಬೇಡಿಕೆಯಲ್ಲ;  
ಶಿವಸಂಕಲ್ಪಕ್ಕೆ ತಕ್ಕಂತೆ ಸತ್ಯ, ಸಮತೆ, ದಾಸೋಹದ ಮಾರ್ಗದಲ್ಲಿ  
ಯೋಗ್ಯವಾದ ದ್ವಾರ ತೆರೆಯಲಿ ।  

ಓಂ ನಮಃ ಶಿವಾಯ ।  
ಓಂ ನಮಃ ಶಿವಾಯ ।  
ಓಂ ನಮಃ ಶಿವಾಯ ।  

ಗುರು-ಲಿಂಗ-ಜಂಗಮ ಸ್ಮರಣೆ ।  
ಪಾದೋದಕ-ಪ್ರಸಾದ-ವಿಭೂತಿ-ರುದ್ರಾಕ್ಷ-ಮಂತ್ರ ಸ್ಮರಣೆ ।  
ಪಂಚಾಚಾರ ಸ್ಮರಣೆ ।  
ಲಿಂಗಾಂಗ ಸಾಮರಸ್ಯ ಧ್ಯಾನ ।  

ಉಳ್ಳವರು ಶಿವಾಲಯ ಮಾಡುವರು,  
ನಾನೇನು ಮಾಡಲಿ ಬಡವನಯ್ಯ?  
ಎನ್ನ ಕಾಲೇ ಕಂಬ, ದೇಹವೇ ದೇಗುಲ,  
ಶಿರವೇ ಹೊನ್ನ ಕಲಶವಯ್ಯ.  
ಕೂಡಲಸಂಗಮದೇವಾ, ಕೇಳಯ್ಯ,  
ಸ್ಥಾವರಕ್ಕಳಿವುಂಟು, ಜಂಗಮಕ್ಕಳಿವಿಲ್ಲ.  

oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।  

ಕೂಡಲಸಂಗಮದೇವಾ,  
ಸಂದರ್ಶನದ ಕ್ಷಣದಲ್ಲಿ ಭಯ ಕರಗಲಿ;  
ಬುದ್ಧಿ ಸ್ಪಷ್ಟವಾಗಲಿ, ವಾಣಿ ಸಮವಾಗಲಿ,  
ಹೃದಯದಲ್ಲಿ ವಿನಯ ಇರಲಿ, ಮುಖದಲ್ಲಿ ಧೈರ್ಯ ಇರಲಿ ।  

ಬಸವಣ್ಣನ “ಕಾಯಕವೇ ಕೈಲಾಸ” ಮಾರ್ಗ ನೆನಪಾಗಲಿ;  
ಕಾಯಕದಲ್ಲಿ ನಿಷ್ಠೆ, ಮಾತಿನಲ್ಲಿ ನೇರತೆ,  
ಪ್ರಶ್ನೆಗೆ ತಕ್ಕ ಉತ್ತರ, ಉತ್ತರಕ್ಕೆ ತಕ್ಕ ಮಿತಭಾಷೆ ದೊರಕಲಿ ।  

ಯೋಗ್ಯರು ಯೋಗ್ಯತೆಯನ್ನು ಗುರುತಿಸಲಿ;  
ಅನ್ಯಾಯವಿಲ್ಲದೆ, ಬಲಾತ್ಕಾರವಿಲ್ಲದೆ, ಅಹಂಕಾರವಿಲ್ಲದೆ,  
ಶಿವಾನುಗ್ರಹಕ್ಕೆ ತಕ್ಕ ಸದುದ್ಯೋಗದ ಸಂಬಂಧ ಕೂಡಿಬರಲಿ ।  

ಗುರು-ಲಿಂಗ-ಜಂಗಮ ಸಾಕ್ಷಿಯಾಗಿ,  
ಅಷ್ಟಾವರಣ ಕಾಪಾಡಲಿ, ಪಂಚಾಚಾರ ಸ್ಥಿರವಾಗಲಿ;  
ಕಾಯಕ ದಾಸೋಹ ಶರಣ ಮಾರ್ಗದಲ್ಲಿ ಈ ಫಲ ಶಿವಾರ್ಪಣವಾಗಲಿ ।  

sarvaṃ śivārpaṇam astu ।  
ಓಂ ನಮಃ ಶಿವಾಯ ।

---

## गाणपत्य

oṃ śrī-gaṇeśāya namaḥ

vakratuṇḍa mahākāya sūryakoṭisamaprabha |
nirvighnaṃ kuru me deva sarvakāryeṣu sarvadā ||

asmin upasthite karma-saṃbandhini sākṣātkāra-kārye,
citta-prasāda-vāk-sauṣṭhava-samaya-jñāna-saubhāgya-prāptyarthaṃ,
śrī-mahāgaṇapati-prītyarthaṃ,
ahaṃ gaṇapati-prārthanāṃ kariṣye ||

oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ ||
oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ ||
oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ ||

oṃ namaste gaṇapataye |
tvameva pratyakṣaṃ tattvamasi |
tvameva kevalaṃ kartā'si |
tvameva kevalaṃ dhartā'si |
tvameva kevalaṃ hartā'si |
tvameva sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahmāsi |
tvaṃ sākṣādātmā'si nityam ||

ṛtaṃ vacmi | satyaṃ vacmi ||

ava tvaṃ mām |
ava vaktāram |
ava śrotāram |
ava dātāram |
ava dhātāram |
avānūcānamava śiṣyam |
ava paścāttāt |
ava purastāt |
avottarāttāt |
ava dakṣiṇāttāt |
ava cordhvāttāt |
avādharāttāt |
sarvato māṃ pāhi pāhi samantāt ||

tvaṃ vāṅmayastvaṃ cinmayaḥ |
tvamānandamayastvaṃ brahmamayaḥ |
tvaṃ saccidānandādvitīyo'si |
tvaṃ pratyakṣaṃ brahmāsi |
tvaṃ jñānamayo vijñānamayo'si ||

ekadantāya vidmahe vakratuṇḍāya dhīmahi |
tanno dantiḥ pracodayāt ||

prathamaṃ vakratuṇḍaṃ ca ekadantaṃ dvitīyakam |
tṛtīyaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgākṣaṃ gajavaktraṃ caturthakam ||
lambodaraṃ pañcamaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhaṃ vikaṭameva ca |
saptamaṃ vighnarājaṃ ca dhūmravarṇaṃ tathāṣṭamam ||
navamaṃ bhālacandraṃ ca daśamaṃ tu vināyakam |
ekādaśaṃ gaṇapatiṃ dvādaśaṃ tu gajānanaṃ ||

oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ |

愿求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，谈吐自若，得遇赏识，觅得良缘；不夺他人福报，不损他人机缘，唯愿障碍消除、善缘成熟、正当成就。

sarva-vighna-vināśāya sarva-maṅgala-hetave |
śrī-gaṇeśāya namaḥ ||

anena gaṇapati-prārthanā-japa-stotra-pāṭhena
yat puṇyaṃ tat sarvaṃ
śrī-gaṇapati-prītyarthaṃ
samarpyāmi ||

yad-akṣara-pada-bhraṣṭaṃ mātrā-hīnaṃ tu yad bhavet |
tat sarvaṃ kṣamyatāṃ deva prasīda gaṇanāyaka ||

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ ||

---

## नाथ संप्रदाय

श्रीगुरवे नमः।  
अलख निरंजन।

ॐ आदिनाथाय नमः।  
ॐ श्रीमत्स्येन्द्रनाथाय नमः।  
ॐ श्रीगोरक्षनाथाय नमः।

सम्यग्-उपजीविका-प्राप्त्यर्थं,  
कर्म-साक्षात्कारस्य निर्विघ्न-सिद्ध्यर्थं,  
काले चित्त-प्रसादाय, वाक्-स्थैर्याय, धैर्याय,  
योग्य-गुण-दर्शनाय, सदवसर-लाभाय च,  
नाथ-गुरु-गोरक्ष-स्मरणं करिष्ये।

न परभाग्यापहाराय, न परहानये,  
न परजीविकाविघाताय, न कस्यचित् क्लेशाय;  
केवलं धर्म्येण मार्गेण स्वकर्म-सिद्धये,  
सर्वभूत-हिताय च।

ॐ शिव गोरक्ष योगी नमः।  
ॐ शिव गोरक्ष योगी नमः।  
ॐ शिव गोरक्ष योगी नमः।

ॐ श्री गोरक्षनाथाय नमः।  
ॐ श्री गोरक्षनाथाय नमः।  
ॐ श्री गोरक्षनाथाय नमः।

गुरोः प्रसादेन मे मनः निर्मलं भवतु।  
गोरक्षनाथस्य स्मरणेन मे वाणी स्वच्छा भवतु।  
आदिनाथस्य अनुग्रहेण उचितं कार्यं सिद्ध्यतु।  
सत्पुरुषैः सद्भावेन दर्शनं भवतु।  
योग्यं स्थानं, योग्यः समयः, योग्यः संयोगः प्राप्यताम्।

अलख निरंजन।  
सतगुरु गोरक्षनाथ महाराज की जय।

यदत्र पुण्यं तद्  
गुरु-परम्परा-प्रसाद-स्मरणपूर्वकं  
स्वचित्त-शुद्धये, धर्म्य-कर्म-सिद्धये,  
सर्वभूत-कल्याणाय, सर्वेषां शान्तये च समर्पयामि।

अलख निरंजन।  
ॐ शान्तिः शान्तिः शान्तिः।

---

## 尼泊尔 Newar Vajracharya

oṃ āḥ hūṃ

namo ratnatrayāya  
namo guru-vajrasattvāya

buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi  
dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi  
saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi

dvitīyam api buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi  
dvitīyam api dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi  
dvitīyam api saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi

tṛtīyam api buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi  
tṛtīyam api dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi  
tṛtīyam api saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi

bodhicittaṃ utpādayāmi  
sarvasattvānāṃ hitāya sukhāya

oṃ vajrasattva samayam anupālaya  
vajrasattva tvenopatiṣṭha  
dṛḍho me bhava  
sutoṣyo me bhava  
supoṣyo me bhava  
anurakto me bhava  
sarvasiddhiṃ me prayaccha  
sarvakarmasu ca me cittaṃ śreyaḥ kuru hūṃ  
ha ha ha ha hoḥ  
bhagavan sarvatathāgata-vajra mā me muñca  
vajrī bhava mahāsamayasattva āḥ hūṃ phaṭ

为此求职面试之吉祥成办而立愿：愿临场身语意清净，心识明澈，谈吐安稳自若；愿所具才能、诚意与善业得以如实呈现，得遇赏识，觅得相应良缘与正当职位。此愿不夺他人福报，不损他人机会，不以强迫、迷惑、伤害成就，只愿以智慧、福德、因缘和合而成。

asya kārya-siddhyarthaṃ  
sarvavighna-praśamanārthaṃ  
sarva-maṅgala-saṃpatti-siddhyarthaṃ  
sarvapuṇya-jñāna-saṃbhāra-paripūraṇārthaṃ

puṣpaṃ samarpayāmi  
dhūpaṃ samarpayāmi  
dīpaṃ samarpayāmi  
gandhaṃ samarpayāmi  
naivedyaṃ samarpayāmi  
sarvaṃ ratnatrayāya samarpayāmi

oṃ vajrasattva āḥ hūṃ svāhā  
oṃ vajrasattva āḥ hūṃ svāhā  
oṃ vajrasattva āḥ hūṃ svāhā

oṃ a ra pa ca na dhīḥ  
oṃ a ra pa ca na dhīḥ  
oṃ a ra pa ca na dhīḥ

oṃ āḥ hūṃ  
oṃ vajrasattva āḥ hūṃ svāhā

sarvakarmasu cittaṃ prasannaṃ bhavatu  
vāk śuddhā bhavatu  
smṛtiḥ prajñā ca vardhatām  
maṅgalaṃ bhavatu  
svasti bhavatu  
śubhaṃ bhavatu

idaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ bhavatu  
anuttara-samyak-saṃbodhi-prāptaye

yad atra puṇyaṃ tad bhavatu  
mātā-pitṛ-pūrvāṅgama-sarvasattvānām  
anuttara-jñāna-phala-prāptaye

yat kiñcid aparādhaṃ kāyena vācā manasā vā kṛtaṃ  
tat sarvaṃ vajrasattva-prasādena śuddhyatu  
ratnatraya-prasādena śāntir bhavatu  
guru-vajrasattva-prasādena maṅgalaṃ bhavatu

sarve sattvāḥ sukhino bhavantu  
sarve sattvā nirāmayāḥ  
sarve sattvā bhadrāṇi paśyantu  
mā kaścid duḥkhabhāg bhavet

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ

---

## Sant Mat / Radha Soami

Rādhāsoāmī.  
Rādhāsoāmī.  
Rādhāsoāmī.

Satgurū Dayāl, Rādhāsoāmī Dayāl,  
is naukarī-sākṣātkār ke avasar meṅ yah man Satgurū kī dayā aur hukam kī or jhukā rahe;  
man nirmal ho, buddhi spaṣṭ ho, vachan sahaj ho, aur vyavahār satya, vinamratā, dayā aur santosh se bharā rahe.

Rādhāsoāmī Dayāl,  
jo yogya avasar ho, vah dayā se mile;  
jo uttam sambandh aur sat-saṅgati jaisā kārya-saṃbandh ho, vah binā kisī par dabāv, binā kisī kā adhikār chhīne, dayā se prakaṭ ho.  
Kisī kā haq na chhine, kisī kī roṭī na kaṭe, kisī kā bhāgya na ghaṭe;  
sirf satya, mehnat, vivek aur hukam ke anusār śubh phal ho.

Rādhāsoāmī Nām Simran:  
Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī

Yadi Satgurū kī maryādā se Nāmdān prāpt ho, to antar meṅ, chup-cāp, apne prāpt Simran ko smaraṇ kiyā jāe;  
anyathā keval sarvajanik Nām se prem-pūrvak simran ho:

Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī

Satgurū Dayāl, man ko simran meṅ sthir karo.  
Rādhāsoāmī Dayāl, surat ko śabd kī or pher do.

Is sākṣātkār ke liye:  
hukam, satya, dhairya, vivek.  
Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī  
Rādhāsoāmī

Antar dhyān:  
Satgurū  
Satgurū  
Satgurū

Bhajan / Surat-Śabd Yoga:  
śabd  
śabd  
śabd

Rādhāsoāmī Dayāl,  
jo kuchh hai, terā hai;  
jo phal ho, hukam meṅ ho;  
bhakti, sevā, dayā sab jīvāṅ ke liye ho.

Sarvajanik Rādhāsoāmī Nām meṅ śaraṇ rahe;  
gupt Nām gupt rahe, maryādā akhaṇḍ rahe, man lābh-lobh aur ahaṅkār se bache.  
Jīvan meṅ ahiṃsā, satya, śuddh āhār, nirmal ācaran, nasha-tyāg, sevā aur Satgurū-bhakti sthir rahe.  
Sab kā kalyāṇ ho, sab ko śānti mile, sab par dayā ho.

Rādhāsoāmī.  
Rādhāsoāmī.  
Rādhāsoāmī.

---

## 湿婆悉檀派

oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  

śrī-parameśvara-parāśakti-gurubhyo namaḥ |  
pati-paśu-pāśa-viveka-prakāśāya śivāya namaḥ ||

śrī-parameśvara-prītyarthaṃ  
udyoga-sākṣātkāra-sarva-maṅgala-siddhyarthaṃ  
samaye nirmala-citta-prasāda-siddhyarthaṃ  
vāg-viśāradya-dhairya-saukumārya-siddhyarthaṃ  
satkāra-sammāna-anukūla-darśana-prāptyarthaṃ  
śubha-yogyatā-lābha-siddhyarthaṃ  
śiva-smaraṇaṃ pañcākṣara-japaṃ ca kariṣye ||

oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  

namaḥ śivāya ca śivatarāya ca ||

oṃ tryambakaṃ yajāmahe sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam |  
urvārukam iva bandhanān mṛtyor mukṣīya mā'mṛtāt ||

tirucciṟṟampalam  

நமச்சிவாய வாழ்க! நாதன் தாள் வாழ்க!  
இமைப்பொழுதும் என் நெஞ்சில் நீங்காதான் தாள் வாழ்க!  

tirucciṟṟampalam  

oṃ namaḥ śivāya ||

śambho mahādeva śiva śaṅkara |  
āgāmini udyoga-sākṣātkāre sarvaṃ maṅgalaṃ kuru |  
antaḥkaraṇaṃ prasādaya, smṛtiṃ medhāṃ ca dīpaya |  
vācaṃ spaṣṭāṃ saumyaṃ ca kuru, manaḥ-sthairyaṃ dehi |  
guṇāḥ yathārthena dṛśyantāṃ, satpuruṣaiḥ sammānaṃ labhyatām |  
ucitaṃ karma-sthānaṃ śubha-sambandhaṃ ca prasādaya ||

na parabhāgyāpahāraṃ yāce |  
na parāyurhāniṃ yāce |  
sarveṣāṃ hitena, dharmeṇa, śiva-anugraheṇa eva siddhir astu ||

yat kṛtaṃ tu mayā deva paripūrṇaṃ tad astu te |  
aparādha-sahasrāṇi kṣamasva parameśvara ||

kāyena vācā manasendriyair vā  
buddhyātmanā vā prakṛteḥ svabhāvāt |  
karomi yad yat sakalaṃ parasmai  
śrī-parameśvarāya samarpayāmi ||

oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  
oṃ namaḥ śivāya  

sarve bhavantu śivamayāḥ |  
śiva-jñāna-prakāśena pāśa-kṣayaḥ, anugrahaḥ, śāntiś ca astu ||

śivārpaṇam astu ||

---

## पुष्टिमार्ग

श्रीकृष्णः शरणं मम ।  
श्रीकृष्णः शरणं मम ।  
श्रीकृष्णः शरणं मम ।

श्रीवल्लभाधीशाय नमः ।  
श्रीगोकुलेश्वराय नमः ।  
श्रीगिरिराजधराय श्रीनाथजी प्रभवे नमः ।

नमामि यमुनामहं सकलसिद्धिहेतुं मुदा  
मुरारिपदपङ्कजस्फुरदमन्दरेणूत्कटाम् ।  
तटस्थनवकाननप्रकटमोदपुष्पाम्बुना  
सुरासुरसुपूजितस्मरपितुः श्रियं बिभ्रतीम् ॥१॥

अस्मिन् कर्मावसरे मम मनः, वाक्, कायः, बुद्धिः, धैर्यं च  
श्रीकृष्णाय समर्पितम् ।  
कार्योपवेशने सर्वं मङ्गलं भवतु;  
प्रत्युत्पन्नबुद्धिः, निर्मलं मनः, सुशोभना वाणी,  
स्वाभाविकं धैर्यं, योग्यगुणदर्शनं, अनुकूलः सत्सम्बन्धश्च  
श्रीनाथजीकृपया सिध्यतु ।  
नान्यस्य भाग्यहरणं, नान्यस्य हानिः,  
केवलं स्वधर्मानुकूलं शुभफलम् इति सङ्कल्पः;  
न मम, श्रीकृष्णस्यैव ।

अधरं मधुरं वदनं मधुरं  
नयनं मधुरं हसितं मधुरम् ।  
हृदयं मधुरं गमनं मधुरं  
मधुराधिपतेरखिलं मधुरम् ॥१॥

वचनं मधुरं चरितं मधुरं  
वसनं मधुरं वलितं मधुरम् ।  
चलितं मधुरं भ्रमितं मधुरं  
मधुराधिपतेरखिलं मधुरम् ॥२॥

श्रीकृष्णः शरणं मम ।  
श्रीकृष्णः शरणं मम ।  
श्रीकृष्णः शरणं मम ।

हे श्रीनाथजी प्रभो,  
इदं हृदयभावसमर्पणम् ।  
अयं अवसरः श्रीकृष्णचरणे न्यस्तः ।  
मम अहङ्कारः, ममत्वं, भयम्, संशयः, फलाकाङ्क्षा च  
श्रीकृष्णचरणयोः समर्पितम् ।  
वाणी मधुरा भवतु, बुद्धिः प्रसन्ना भवतु,  
चित्तं तव स्मरणे स्थितं भवतु ।

यत्करोषि यदश्नासि यज्जुहोषि ददासि यत् ।  
यत्तपस्यसि कौन्तेय तत्कुरुष्व मदर्पणम् ॥

कायेन वाचा मनसेन्द्रियैर्वा  
बुद्ध्यात्मना वा प्रकृतेः स्वभावात् ।  
करोमि यद्यत्सकलं परस्मै  
नारायणायेति समर्पयामि ॥

श्रीकृष्णः शरणं मम ।  
सेवाभावेन स्मरामि, कीर्तनभावेन नमामि,  
शरणागतभावेन सर्वं समर्पयामि ।  
श्रीवल्लभाधीशाय नमः ।  
श्रीयमुनामहाराण्यै नमः ।  
श्रीनाथजी प्रभवे नमः ।

---

## 沙克塔派

oṃ apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthāṃ gato 'pi vā |  
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ ||

oṃ śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ ||

gurur brahmā gurur viṣṇuḥ gurur devo maheśvaraḥ |  
guruḥ sākṣāt parabrahma tasmai śrīgurave namaḥ ||

mama udyoga-sākṣātkāra-kārye  
sarva-maṅgala-siddhyarthaṃ,  
pratyutpanna-buddhi-prasādārthaṃ,  
vāg-viśāradya-sthairya-lābhārthaṃ,  
satkāra-dṛṣṭi-prāptyarthaṃ,  
śubha-yogya-sthāna-lābhārthaṃ,  
na parānāṃ bhāgya-haraṇāya,  
na parānām āyur-hānaye,  
śrī-durgā-prītyarthaṃ  
etat prārthanā-japaṃ kariṣye ||

oṃ duṃ durgāyai namaḥ ||

oṃ kātyāyanāya vidmahe  
kanyakumāri dhīmahi  
tanno durgiḥ pracodayāt ||

dhyāyāmi śrī-durgāṃ devīṃ  
siṃha-vāhinīṃ śubha-pradām |  
abhaya-varadāṃ mātaraṃ  
sarva-vighna-vināśinīm ||

āvāhayāmi śrī-durgāṃ  
śaraṇāgata-vatsalām |  
mama cittaṃ prasādaya  
mama vācaṃ śobhayā ||

yā devī sarvabhūteṣu śakti-rūpeṇa saṃsthitā |  
namastasyai namastasyai namastasyai namo namaḥ ||

yā devī sarvabhūteṣu mātr̥-rūpeṇa saṃsthitā |  
namastasyai namastasyai namastasyai namo namaḥ ||

yā devī sarvabhūteṣu buddhi-rūpeṇa saṃsthitā |  
namastasyai namastasyai namastasyai namo namaḥ ||

yā devī sarvabhūteṣu kṣānti-rūpeṇa saṃsthitā |  
namastasyai namastasyai namastasyai namo namaḥ ||

yā devī sarvabhūteṣu vāk-rūpeṇa saṃsthitā |  
namastasyai namastasyai namastasyai namo namaḥ ||

yā devī sarvabhūteṣu śraddhā-rūpeṇa saṃsthitā |  
namastasyai namastasyai namastasyai namo namaḥ ||

sarva-maṅgala-māṅgalye śive sarvārtha-sādhike |  
śaraṇye tryambake gauri nārāyaṇi namo 'stu te ||

śaraṇāgata-dīnārta-paritrāṇa-parāyaṇe |  
sarvasyārti-hare devi nārāyaṇi namo 'stu te ||

sarva-svarūpe sarveśe sarva-śakti-samanvite |  
bhayebhyas trāhi no devi durge devi namo 'stu te ||

rogān aśeṣān apahaṃsi tuṣṭā  
ruṣṭā tu kāmān sakalān abhīṣṭān |  
tvām āśritānāṃ na vipannarāṇāṃ  
tvām āśritā hy āśrayatāṃ prayānti ||

he mātar durge,  
sākṣātkāra-kāle me manaḥ prasannaṃ bhavatu |  
buddhiḥ nirmalā bhavatu |  
vāk svacchā madhurā ca bhavatu |  
bhayaṃ dūraṃ gacchatu |  
dhairyaṃ hṛdaye tiṣṭhatu |  
yogyāḥ janāḥ guṇān paśyantu |  
yathā-dharmaṃ yathā-maṅgalaṃ  
śubha-saṃyogaḥ sampadyatām ||

oṃ duṃ durgāyai namaḥ |  
oṃ duṃ durgāyai namaḥ |  
oṃ duṃ durgāyai namaḥ ||

aparādha-sahasrāṇi kriyante 'harniśaṃ mayā |  
dāso 'yam iti māṃ matvā kṣamasva parameśvari ||

mantra-hīnaṃ kriyā-hīnaṃ bhakti-hīnaṃ sureśvari |  
yat pūjitaṃ mayā devi paripūrṇaṃ tad astu me ||

oṃ sarve bhavantu sukhinaḥ  
sarve santu nirāmayāḥ |  
sarve bhadrāṇi paśyantu  
mā kaścid duḥkha-bhāg bhavet ||

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ ||

etat phalaṃ śrī-durgā-devyai samarpyāmi |  
sarva-bhūta-hita-siddhyarthaṃ samarpayāmi ||

---

## සිංහල පිරිත්

Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa.  
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa.  
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa.

Buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dhammaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Saṅghaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.

Dutiyampi Buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dutiyampi Dhammaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dutiyampi Saṅghaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.

Tatiyampi Buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Tatiyampi Dhammaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Tatiyampi Saṅghaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.

Pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Adinnādānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Kāmesu micchācārā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Musāvādā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.

Iti pi so bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho,  
vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū,  
anuttaro purisadammasārathi,  
satthā devamanussānaṃ buddho bhagavā.

Svākkhāto bhagavatā dhammo,  
sandiṭṭhiko akāliko ehipassiko,  
opanayiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī.

Supaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho,  
ujuppaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho,  
ñāyappaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho,  
sāmīcippaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho,  
yadidaṃ cattāri purisayugāni aṭṭha purisapuggalā,  
esa bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho,  
āhuneyyo pāhuneyyo dakkhiṇeyyo añjalikaraṇīyo,  
anuttaraṃ puññakkhettaṃ lokassa.

රැකියා සම්මුඛ පරීක්ෂණයේදී සිත පැහැදිලි වේවා;  
වචනය සුවච, සත්‍ය, මෘදු, යථාකාලික වේවා;  
භය හා අවුල් සිතින් දුරුවේවා;  
ගුණය දකින සුදුසු සම්මුඛකාරයන් හමුවේවා;  
ධර්මයට එකඟ යහපත් කාර්ය-සම්බන්ධයක් ලැබේවා.  
අන්‍යයන්ගේ පුඤ්ඤය නොහරමින්, අන්‍යයන්ගේ ආයුෂ නොහීන කරමින්,  
සියල්ලන්ට අවිරෝධව සුභ මඟ විවෘත වේවා.

Asevanā ca bālānaṃ,  
paṇḍitānañ ca sevanā;  
pūjā ca pūjanīyānaṃ,  
etaṃ maṅgalam uttamaṃ.

Bāhusaccañ ca sippañ ca,  
vinayo ca susikkhito;  
subhāsitā ca yā vācā,  
etaṃ maṅgalam uttamaṃ.

Khantī ca sovacassatā,  
samaṇānañ ca dassanaṃ;  
kālena dhammasākacchā,  
etaṃ maṅgalam uttamaṃ.

Phuṭṭhassa lokadhammehi,  
cittaṃ yassa na kampati;  
asokaṃ virajaṃ khemaṃ,  
etaṃ maṅgalam uttamaṃ.

Yaṃ kiñci vittaṃ idha vā huraṃ vā,  
saggesu vā yaṃ ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ,  
na no samaṃ atthi tathāgatena;  
idampi buddhe ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ,  
etena saccena suvatthi hotu.

Khayaṃ virāgaṃ amataṃ paṇītaṃ,  
yadajjhagā sakyamunī samāhito,  
na tena dhammena samatthi kiñci;  
idampi dhamme ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ,  
etena saccena suvatthi hotu.

Ye puggalā aṭṭha sataṃ pasatthā,  
cattāri etāni yugāni honti,  
te dakkhiṇeyyā sugatassa sāvakā;  
idampi saṅghe ratanaṃ paṇītaṃ,  
etena saccena suvatthi hotu.

Karaṇīyam atthakusalena,  
yantaṃ santaṃ padaṃ abhisamecca:  
sakko ujū ca suhujū ca,  
suvaco cassa mudu anatimānī.

Na ca khuddaṃ samācare kiñci,  
yena viññū pare upavadeyyuṃ.  
Sukhino vā khemino hontu,  
sabbe sattā bhavantu sukhitattā.

Mettañ ca sabbalokasmiṃ,  
mānasaṃ bhāvaye aparimāṇaṃ,  
uddhaṃ adho ca tiriyañ ca,  
asambādhaṃ averaṃ asapattaṃ.

Etena saccavajjena, sotthi hotu sabbadā.  
Buddhānubhāvena cittaṃ pasīdatu.  
Dhammānubhāvena paññā pakāsatu.  
Saṅghānubhāvena vacanaṃ suṭṭhu pavattatu.

Bhavatu sabbamaṅgalaṃ,  
rakkhantu sabbadevatā,  
sabbabuddhānubhāvena,  
sadā sotthī bhavantu te.

Bhavatu sabbamaṅgalaṃ,  
rakkhantu sabbadevatā,  
sabbadhammānubhāvena,  
sadā sotthī bhavantu te.

Bhavatu sabbamaṅgalaṃ,  
rakkhantu sabbadevatā,  
sabbasaṅghānubhāvena,  
sadā sotthī bhavantu te.

Sabbe sattā sukhitā hontu.  
Sabbe sattā averā hontu.  
Sabbe sattā abyāpajjhā hontu.  
Sabbe sattā anīghā hontu.  
Sabbe sattā sukhī attānaṃ pariharantu.

Idaṃ puññaṃ āsavakkhayāvahaṃ hotu.  
Idaṃ puññaṃ sabbasattānaṃ hotu.  
Sabbe sattā anumodantu.  
Iminā puññakammena, mā me bālasamāgamo;  
sataṃ samāgamo hotu, yāva nibbānapattiyā.

Buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dhammaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Saṅghaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Sabbe sattā bhavantu sukhitattā.

---

## 斯里兰卡 Thovil / Sanni Yakuma

Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā-sambuddhassa.  
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā-sambuddhassa.  
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā-sambuddhassa.

Buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dhammaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Saṅghaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dutiyampi Buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dutiyampi Dhammaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Dutiyampi Saṅghaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Tatiyampi Buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Tatiyampi Dhammaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.  
Tatiyampi Saṅghaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi.

Pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Adinnādānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Kāmesu micchācārā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Musāvādā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.  
Surāmeraya-majja-pamādaṭṭhānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṃ samādiyāmi.

Yānīdha bhūtāni samāgatāni,  
bhummāni vā yāni va antalikkhe;  
sabbeva bhūtā sumanā bhavantu,  
athopi sakkacca suṇantu bhāsitaṃ.

Tasmā hi bhūtā nisāmetha sabbe,  
mettaṃ karotha mānusiyā pajāya;  
divā ca ratto ca haranti ye baliṃ,  
tasmā hi ne rakkhatha appamattā.

Karaṇīyam atthakusalena,  
yaṃ taṃ santaṃ padaṃ abhisamecca;  
sakko ujū ca suhujū ca,  
suvaco cassa mudu anatimānī.

Me rækīyā sammuḵa-parīkṣaṇayaṭa yana kāryayē, hita pæhædili vēvā, vacana samādhāna vēvā, baya sæka duru vēvā, guṇa dakina aya hamu vēvā, yōgya rækīyā magak ære vēvā.  
Aññesaṃ puññaṃ ahāpetvā, aññesaṃ āyuṃ ahāpetvā, aññesaṃ lābhaṃ ahāpetvā, dhammena suvatthi hotu.

Budu guṇayen, Dhamma guṇayen, Saṅgha guṇayen ārakṣā vēvā.  
Graha-dosa, yak-dosa, sanni-dosa, vas-dosa me kāryayen duru vēvā.  
Avahira duru vēvā.  
Andhakāra duru vēvā.  
Hita kalabala duru vēvā.  
Vāca bādhā duru vēvā.  
Sammukha parīkṣaṇayē sukhuma-nuwana pæhædili vēvā.

Mahā Kōla Sanni Yakā, daha ata sanni yakku:  
Amukku Sanniya, Golu Sanniya, Kana Sanniya, Bihiri Sanniya,  
Vāta Sanniya, Pitta Sanniya, Slesma Sanniya, Gini-jala Sanniya,  
Kora Sanniya, Pissu Sanniya, Deva Sanniya, Nāga Sanniya,  
Maru Sanniya, Gulma Sanniya, Jala Sanniya, Kōla Sanniya,  
Būta Sanniya, Kapāla Sanniya —  
sakkacca suṇantu, mettaṃ karontu, appamattā rakkhantu.

Me kāryayē æti dosa duru karanna.  
Me hitaṭa æti baya duru karanna.  
Me vacanayē æti bandhana duru karanna.  
Me gamanē æti avahira duru karanna.  
Me sammuḵa-parīkṣaṇayē æti kalabala duru karanna.  
Āturayāge dosa duru vēvā.  
Baya duru vēvā.  
Yak-dosa duru vēvā.  
Sanni-dosa duru vēvā.  
Graha-dosa duru vēvā.

Mahā Kōla Sanni Yakā samaga daha ata sanni yakku, niyama lesa yanna, niyama lesa hærī yanna.  
Ata pā ata hærala yanna.  
Hita allanna epa.  
Vācā bandanna epa.  
Gaman baḍa karanna epa.  
Dhamma guṇayen, Saṅgha guṇayen, niyama lesa samayaṭa hærī yanna.

Iti pi so bhagavā arahaṃ sammā-sambuddho,  
vijjācaraṇa-sampanno sugato lokavidū,  
anuttaro purisadammasārathi,  
satthā devamanussānaṃ buddho bhagavā.

Etena saccena suvatthi hotu.  
Etena saccena suvatthi hotu.  
Etena saccena suvatthi hotu.

Sabbe sattā bhavantu sukhitattā.  
Sabbe sattā averā hontu.  
Sabbe sattā abyāpajjhā hontu.  
Sabbe sattā anīghā hontu.  
Sabbe sattā sukhī attānaṃ pariharantu.

Idaṃ me puññaṃ āsavakkhayāvahaṃ hotu.  
Idaṃ me puññaṃ nibbānassa paccayo hotu.  
Idaṃ puññaṃ sabba-bhūtānaṃ hotu.  
Sabbe sattā bhavantu sukhitattā.

---

## स्मार्त

oṃ apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthāṃ gato 'pi vā |  
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ ||

oṃ keśavāya svāhā |  
oṃ nārāyaṇāya svāhā |  
oṃ mādhavāya svāhā ||

oṃ bhūḥ | oṃ bhuvaḥ | oṃ suvaḥ | oṃ mahaḥ | oṃ janaḥ | oṃ tapaḥ | oṃ satyam |  
oṃ tat savitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt |  
oṃ āpo jyotī raso 'mṛtaṃ brahma bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar oṃ ||

mama upātta-samasta-duritakṣayadvārā śrī-parameśvara-prītyarthaṃ  
udyoga-sākṣātkāra-kārye sarva-maṅgala-prāptyarthaṃ,  
samaya-prāpte prasanna-buddhi-vāk-sauṣṭhava-svābhāvika-saṃvāda-prāptyarthaṃ,  
sat-sammāna-anukūla-avasara-śubha-yogyatā-sambandha-lābhārthaṃ,  
na parabhāgyāpahāreṇa na parahānyā kintu dharmya-siddhyarthaṃ,  
śrī-sarasvatī-devī-pūjāṃ kariṣye ||

oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ |  
vakratuṇḍa mahākāya sūryakoṭisamaprabha |  
nirvighnaṃ kuru me deva sarvakāryeṣu sarvadā ||

oṃ kalaśasya mukhe viṣṇuḥ kaṇṭhe rudraḥ samāśritaḥ |  
mūle tatra sthito brahmā madhye mātṛgaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
kukṣau tu sāgarāḥ sarve sapta-dvīpā vasundharā |  
ṛgvedo 'tha yajurvedaḥ sāmavedo hy atharvaṇaḥ |  
aṅgaiś ca sahitāḥ sarve kalaśāmbu samāśritāḥ ||

yā kundendu-tuṣārahāra-dhavalā yā śubhra-vastrāvṛtā |  
yā vīṇā-vara-daṇḍa-maṇḍita-karā yā śveta-padmāsanā |  
yā brahmācyuta-śaṅkara-prabhṛtibhir devaiḥ sadā vanditā |  
sā māṃ pātu sarasvatī bhagavatī niḥśeṣa-jāḍyāpahā ||

oṃ śrī-sarasvati devi āvāhayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai āsanaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai pādyaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai arghyaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai ācamanīyaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai snānaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai vastraṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai yajñopavītaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai gandhaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai akṣatān samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai puṣpāṇi samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai dhūpam āghrāpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai dīpaṃ darśayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai naivedyaṃ nivedayāmi |  
oṃ prāṇāya svāhā |  
oṃ apānāya svāhā |  
oṃ vyānāya svāhā |  
oṃ udānāya svāhā |  
oṃ samānāya svāhā |  
oṃ brahmaṇe svāhā |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai tāmbūlaṃ samarpayāmi |  
oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai nīrājanaṃ samarpayāmi ||

oṃ śrīṃ hrīṃ sarasvatyai namaḥ |  
oṃ aiṃ sarasvatyai namaḥ |  
oṃ vāgdevyai namaḥ ||

sarasvati namas tubhyaṃ varade kāmarūpiṇi |  
vidyārambhaṃ kariṣyāmi siddhir bhavatu me sadā ||

śuklāṃ brahmavicāra-sāra-paramām ādyāṃ jagad-vyāpinīṃ |  
vīṇā-pustaka-dhāriṇīm abhaya-dāṃ jāḍyāndhakārāpahām |  
haste sphāṭika-mālikāṃ vidadhatīṃ padmāsane saṃsthitām |  
vande tāṃ parameśvarīṃ bhagavatīṃ buddhi-pradāṃ śāradām ||

oṃ śrī-sarasvatyai devyai namaḥ |  
namaste astu bhagavati śrī-sarasvati devi |  
anena pūjā-japa-stotra-pāṭhena  
udyoga-sākṣātkāra-kārye prasanna-buddhiḥ, śuddhā vāk, dhairyaṃ, smṛtiḥ,  
samyag-uttara-dāna-śaktiḥ, sat-sammānaṃ, śubha-avasara-lābhaś ca astu ||

mantra-hīnaṃ kriyā-hīnaṃ bhakti-hīnaṃ sureśvari |  
yat pūjitaṃ mayā devi paripūrṇaṃ tad astu me ||

aparādha-sahasrāṇi kriyante 'harniśaṃ mayā |  
dāso 'yam iti māṃ matvā kṣamasva parameśvari ||

yāntu devagaṇāḥ sarve pūjām ādāya māmakīm |  
iṣṭakāma-prasiddhyarthaṃ punarāgamanāya ca ||

sarve bhavantu sukhinaḥ sarve santu nirāmayāḥ |  
sarve bhadrāṇi paśyantu mā kaścid duḥkhabhāg bhavet ||

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ ||

sarvaṃ śrī-parameśvarārpaṇam astu ||

---

## ஶ்ரீவைணவம்

**[Ācārya-vandanam]**

śrīḥ

śrīśailēśa dayāpātraṃ dhībhaktyādi guṇārṇavam |  
yatīndra-pravaṇaṃ vande ramya-jāmātaraṃ munim ||

lakṣmī-nātha-samārambhāṃ nātha-yāmuna-madhyamām |  
asmad-ācārya-paryantāṃ vande guru-paramparām ||

śrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥ |  
śrīmate nigamānta-mahādeśikāya namaḥ |  
śrīmate varavara-munaye namaḥ ||

**[Śrīman Nārāyaṇa śaraṇāgati]**

oṃ śrīmannārāyaṇāya namaḥ |  
oṃ śrīyai namaḥ |  
oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya ||

śāntākāraṃ bhujaga-śayanaṃ padmanābhaṃ sureśaṃ  
viśvādhāraṃ gagana-sadṛśaṃ meghavarṇaṃ śubhāṅgam |  
lakṣmīkāntaṃ kamala-nayanaṃ yogi-hṛd-dhyāna-gamyaṃ  
vande viṣṇuṃ bhava-bhaya-haraṃ sarva-lokaika-nātham ||

**[saṅkalpa / 发愿]**

愿求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，谈吐自若，得遇赏识，觅得良缘；不夺他人福报，不损他人前程，不以胜负伤人，但愿障碍自息，因缘端正，所遇皆合乎 dharma 与 Śrīman Nārāyaṇa 之慈悲。

asya kārya-samaye,  
udyoga-sākṣātkāra-siddhyarthaṃ,  
citta-prasāda-vāk-sāmarthya-smṛti-dhairya-lābhārthaṃ,  
anukūla-sambandha-prāptyarthaṃ,  
śrī-bhagavad-ājñā-kaiṅkarya-rūpeṇa,  
śrīman-nārāyaṇa-prītyarthaṃ,  
idaṃ prārthanā-pāṭhaṃ kariṣye ||

na parānāṃ bhāgya-hānyai,  
na parānāṃ vṛtti-vighātāya,  
kintu svānta-śuddhyai, yogyatā-prakāśāya,  
śubha-sambandha-siddhyai ca ||

**[公开 pāśuram、stotra、nāma 正行]**

yasya dvirada-vaktrādyāḥ pāriṣadyāḥ paraḥ śatam |  
vighnaṃ nighnanti satataṃ viśvaksenaṃ tam āśraye ||

jñānānanda-mayaṃ devaṃ nirmala-sphaṭikākṛtim |  
ādhāraṃ sarva-vidyānāṃ hayagrīvam upāsmahe ||

viśvaṃ viṣṇur vaṣaṭkāro bhūta-bhavya-bhavat-prabhuḥ |  
bhūta-kṛd bhūta-bhṛd bhāvo bhūtātmā bhūta-bhāvanaḥ ||

மார்கழித் திங்கள் மதி நிறைந்த நன்னாளால்  
நீராடப் போதுவீர் போதுமினோ நேரிழையீர்  
சீர் மல்கும் ஆய்ப்பாடிச் செல்வச் சிறுமீர்காள்  
கூர்வேல் கொடுந்தொழிலன் நந்தகோபன் குமரன்  
ஏரார்ந்த கண்ணி யசோதை இளஞ்சிங்கம்  
கார்மேனிச் செங்கண் கதிர்மதியம் போல்முகத்தான்  
நாராயணனே நமக்கே பறை தருவான்  
பாரோர் புகழப் படிந்தேலோர் எம்பாவாய்.

agalakillēn iṟaiyum enru alarmēl maṅgai uṟai mārba |  
nigaril pugazhāy ulagam mūnṟu uḍaiyāy ennai āḷvānē |  
nigaril amarar munikkaṇaṅgaḷ virumbum tiruvēṅkaṭattānē |  
pugal onṟillā aḍiyēn un aḍikkīḻ amarndu pugundēnē ||

**[prārthanā / 祈请]**

śrīman-nārāyaṇa, śrī-mahālakṣmī-sameta,  
ācārya-paramparā-anugraheṇa,  
asmin udyoga-sākṣātkāra-kāle  
mano me prasīdatām, buddhiḥ prasīdatu,  
smṛtiḥ sthirā bhavatu, vāk śuddhā bhavatu,  
dhairyaṃ vinaya-sahitaṃ vardhatām ||

hayagrīva-dayayā jñānaṃ smṛtiṃ ca dehi |  
śrī-dayayā sauśīlyaṃ mādhuryaṃ ca dehi |  
nārāyaṇa-kṛpayā bhayaṃ śāmyatu,  
vighnāḥ svayam apayāntu,  
yathārhaṃ mama guṇāḥ prakāśantām ||

samyag-praśnān avagantuṃ śaktiṃ dehi |  
samyag-uttarāṇi dātuṃ śaktiṃ dehi |  
satyam, vinayam, prasādaṃ, saukaryaṃ ca dehi |  
anukūlāḥ draṣṭāraḥ santu,  
dhārmikaḥ sambandhaḥ sidhyatu,  
śreyase yogyā vṛttiḥ labhyatām ||

**[ātma-nikṣepa / samarpana]**

kāyena vācā manasendriyair vā  
buddhyātmanā vā prakṛteḥ svabhāvāt |  
karomi yad yat sakalaṃ parasmai  
nārāyaṇāyeti samarpayāmi ||

yat phalaṃ bhavatu, tat tava prasādāt |  
yat na bhavatu, tat api tava hitānugrahaḥ |  
ahaṃ śrīman-nārāyaṇa-caraṇayoḥ  
śrī-sahitaṃ śaraṇam āśritaḥ ||

**[kṣamāpaṇa]**

aparādha-sahasrāṇi kriyante aharniśaṃ mayā |  
dāso’yam iti māṃ matvā kṣamasva puruṣottama ||

ajñānāt vismṛteḥ bhayāt vā  
yad vacanaṃ duṣṭaṃ, yad manaḥ calitam,  
yad ahaṅkāraḥ jātaḥ, tat sarvaṃ kṣamasva |  
śuddha-bhaktiṃ, śānta-cittaṃ, sevā-bhāvaṃ ca dehi ||

**[maṅgalam / 回向]**

sarvaṃ śrī-kṛṣṇārpaṇam astu |  
sarvaṃ śrīman-nārāyaṇa-caraṇāravindayoḥ samarpayāmi ||

pallāṇḍu pallāṇḍu pallāyirattāṇḍu  
palakōḍi nūṟāyiram  
mallāṇḍa tiṇḍōḷ maṇivaṇṇā  
un sēvaḍi sevvi tirukkāppu ||

śrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥ |  
śrīmate nigamānta-mahādeśikāya namaḥ |  
śrīmate varavara-munaye namaḥ |  
śrī-śrīman-nārāyaṇa-divya-dampatī-prītyarthaṃ  
idaṃ sarvaṃ samarpitam astu ||

---

## 室利韦迪亚（Śrī Vidyā）

oṃ apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthāṃ gato 'pi vā |  
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ ||

oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ ||

gurur brahmā gurur viṣṇuḥ gurur devo maheśvaraḥ |  
guruḥ sākṣāt paraṃ brahma tasmai śrī-gurave namaḥ ||

oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ śrī-gurubhyo namaḥ |  
oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ śrī-lalitā-tripurasundaryai namaḥ |

udyoga-sākṣātkāra-sarva-maṅgala-pravṛttyarthaṃ,  
tat-kāla-citta-prasāda-smṛti-prakāśa-vāk-sauṣṭhava-dhairya-siddhyarthaṃ,  
sat-puruṣaiḥ guṇa-parijñāna-prāptyarthaṃ,  
yogya-udyoga-lābha-siddhyarthaṃ,  
aparānāṃ bhāgya-hāniṃ vinā, aparānām āyuḥ-kṣayaṃ vinā,  
anṛta-vañcana-parapīḍā-varjita-śubha-saṅkalpa-siddhyarthaṃ,  
śrī-lalitā-tripurasundarī-prītyarthaṃ,  
ayaṃ saṅkalpaḥ ||

aruṇāṃ karuṇā-taraṅgitākṣīṃ  
dhṛta-pāśāṅkuśa-puṣpa-bāṇa-cāpām |  
aṇimādibhirāvṛtāṃ mayūkhair  
ahamityeva vibhāvaye bhavānīm ||

oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ śrī-lalitā-tripurasundaryai namaḥ ||  
oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ śrī-mātre namaḥ ||  
oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ śrī-mahārājñyai namaḥ ||  
oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ śrīmat-siṃhāsaneśvaryai namaḥ ||

śrīmātā śrīmahārājñī śrīmat-siṃhāsaneśvarī |  
cidagni-kuṇḍa-sambhūtā devakārya-samudyatā ||  
udyad-bhānu-sahasrābhā caturbāhu-samanvitā |  
rāga-svarūpa-pāśāḍhyā krodhākārāṅkuśojjvalā ||  
manorūpekṣu-kodaṇḍā pañca-tanmātra-sāyakā |  
nijāruṇa-prabhāpūra-majjad-brahmāṇḍa-maṇḍalā ||

oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ śrī-lalitā-tripurasundaryai namaḥ |  
nāma-japaṃ samarpayāmi ||

he śrī-mātaḥ, he tripurasundari,  
sākṣātkāra-kāle me manaḥ prasannaṃ bhavatu,  
buddhiḥ sphuṭā bhavatu, vāk śuddhā madhurā ca bhavatu,  
bhayaṃ śāmyatu, saṃśayaḥ praśāmyatu,  
satyaṃ hitaṃ priyaṃ ca vacanaṃ pravartatām |  
yogyatā mama prakāśatām,  
śubha-dṛṣṭiḥ śubha-saṃvādaś ca bhavatu,  
yad yogyaṃ śreyaskaraṃ dhārmikaṃ ca, tad eva prasīdatām ||

aparādha-sahasrāṇi kriyante 'harniśaṃ mayā |  
dāso 'yam iti māṃ matvā kṣamasva parameśvari ||

yadakṣara-pada-bhraṣṭaṃ mātrā-hīnaṃ ca yad bhavet |  
tat sarvaṃ kṣamyatāṃ devi prasīda parameśvari ||

sarve bhavantu sukhinaḥ sarve santu nirāmayāḥ |  
sarve bhadrāṇi paśyantu mā kaścid duḥkha-bhāg bhavet ||

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ ||

anena śrī-lalitā-tripurasundarī-nāma-stotra-mantra-japena  
udyoga-sākṣātkāra-saṅkalpasya śuddhi-siddhir astu |  
etat phalaṃ śrī-lalitā-tripurasundaryai samarpyate |  
guru-paramparā-prasādena sarvaṃ śubham astu |  
oṃ tat sat ||

---

## સ્વામિનારાયણ સંપ્રદાય

Śrī Svāminārāyaṇāya namaḥ।

He Bhagavān Svāminārāyaṇa, he Sahajānand Svāmī Mahārāj,  
huṁ āje nokarīnā interview māṭe,  
śuddha bhāve prārthanā karuṁ chuṁ।  
Mārā man, vachan ane kāyānā aparādh kṣamā karajo।  
Mane dharma, jñān, vairāgya ane bhakti māṁ sthir karajo।  
Mārī buddhi nirmal, man sthir, ane vānī maryādāpūrṇa karajo।

Svāminārāyaṇa, Svāminārāyaṇa,  
Svāminārāyaṇa, Svāminārāyaṇa,  
Svāminārāyaṇa, Svāminārāyaṇa,  
Svāminārāyaṇa, Svāminārāyaṇa।

Oṁ Śrī Svāminārāyaṇāya namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Sahajānandāya namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Harikṛṣṇāya namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Nārāyaṇamunaye namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Ghanshyāmāya namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Haraye namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Puruṣottamāya namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Akṣaradhāmanivāsine namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Bhaktavatsalāya namaḥ।  
Oṁ Śrī Dayānidhaye namaḥ।

Jaya Sadguru Svāmī, Prabhu jaya Sadguru Svāmī,  
Sahajānand dayāḷu, balavant bahunāmī।  
Jaya Sadguru Svāmī।

Caraṇakamal tava vandu, kar joḍī Prabhu,  
Caraṇe śīś dharyāthī, dukh nākhyā toḍī।  
Jaya Sadguru Svāmī।

Nārāyaṇ Muni trātā, dvijakuḷ tanu dhārī,  
Pāmar patit uddhāryā, agaṇit nar-nārī।  
Jaya Sadguru Svāmī।

Nitya nitya nautam līlā, kartā avināśī,  
Aḍasaṭh tīrath caraṇe, koṭi Gayā Kāśī।  
Jaya Sadguru Svāmī।

Puruṣottam pragaṭnuṁ, je darśan karaśe,  
Kāḷ karma thī chhūṭī, kuṭumb sahit taraśe।  
Jaya Sadguru Svāmī।

Ā avasar karuṇānidhi, karuṇā bahu kīdhī,  
Muktānand kahe mukti, sugam karī sīdhī।  
Jaya Sadguru Svāmī।

He Sahajānand Svāmī Mahārāj,  
interview samaye mane antar-śānti, smṛti, vivek ane spaṣṭatā āpajo।  
Mārī vānī svabhāvik, namra, satya ane prabhāvī rahe tevuṁ karajo।  
Bhaya, ghabarāṭ, aspaṣṭatā, ahaṁkār ane avivek dūr karajo।  
Je loko interview le, temnā man māṁ nyāy, samaj, sadbhāv ane yogya mūlyāṅkan rahe tevuṁ āśīrvād karajo।  
Mane dharma-yukta rojgār, sadācārne anukūḷ kāryasthān, ane yogya avasar-rūp śubh sambandh prāpt thāy tevuṁ karajo।  
Ā safaltā koī bījānā adhikār, bhāgya, ājīvikā ke sukha-ne haraṇ karīne na hoy; sarve māṭe nyāy ane kalyāṇ rahe।  
Mane satsang, niyam, sadācār ane bhakti māṁ dṛḍh karajo।  
Mārā sarva karma tamārā caraṇe samarpit che।

Svāminārāyaṇa, Svāminārāyaṇa,  
Svāminārāyaṇa, Svāminārāyaṇa।

He Prabhu, mārā man māṁ koīne vaś karavānī, hāni karavānī, adharmathī lābh levānī ke anyāy karavānī vṛtti na rahe।  
Huṁ mārā mandir, āchārya-guru-paramparānī maryādā pramāṇe dhun, mālā, ārti ane smaraṇ śuddha bhāve karuṁ; mane niyam, pavitratā, vinay ane Bhagavad-bhakti māṁ sthir rākho।  
Kṣamā karajo Mahārāj।  
Sarvaṁ Śrī Svāminārāyaṇārpaṇam astu।

---

## श्रौत / कर्मकाण्ड

oṃ

śuddhy-ācamanānantaram ।

asya yajamānasya karma-prāpti-saṃvāda-saṃbandhena  
saṃvāde sarvaṃ śubhaṃ bhavatu, antaḥkaraṇaṃ prasannaṃ bhavatu,  
smṛtiḥ medhā ca susthirā bhavatu, vāk svayam āyatā bhavatu,  
guṇāḥ yathārhaṃ prakāśantām, sat-puruṣaiḥ saṃmānaḥ labhyatām,  
anukūlaṃ karma-sthānaṃ ca śubhaḥ sambandhaḥ ca prāpyatām iti saṅkalpaḥ ।

na parasya śriyam āditsāmahe, na parasya āyuḥ kṣiṇīmahi;  
sarveṣāṃ bhadraṃ bhavatu, sarveṣāṃ ṛtam anuvartatām ।

agnim īḷe purohitaṃ yajñasya devaṃ ṛtvijam ।  
hotāraṃ ratnadhātamam ॥

agne naya supathā rāye asmān  
viśvāni deva vayunāni vidvān ।  
yuyodhy asmaj juhurāṇam eno  
bhūyiṣṭhāṃ te nama-uktiṃ vidhema ॥

oṃ bhūr agnaye svāhā ।  
idam agnaye na mama ।

oṃ bhuvaḥ vāyave svāhā ।  
idam vāyave na mama ।

oṃ svaḥ sūryāya svāhā ।  
idam sūryāya na mama ।

savitṛ-prārthanā:

tat savitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi ।  
dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt ॥

tryambakaṃ yajāmahe sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam ।  
urvārukam iva bandhanān mṛtyor mukṣīya mā'mṛtāt ॥

vāci me śāntiḥ, manasi me śāntiḥ, prāṇeṣu me śāntiḥ ।  
satyaṃ vadāni, ṛtaṃ vadāni, hitaṃ vadāni, anṛtaṃ mā vadāni ।  
savitā dhiyo me pracodayatu, agniḥ panthānaṃ nayatu,  
bṛhaspatiḥ vācaṃ dadhātu, indraḥ dhairyaṃ dadhātu ।

agnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā ।  
idam agnaye sviṣṭakṛte na mama ।

svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ ।  
svasti naḥ pūṣā viśvavedāḥ ।  
svasti nas tārkṣyo ariṣṭanemiḥ ।  
svasti no bṛhaspatir dadhātu ॥

dyauḥ śāntir antarikṣaṃ śāntiḥ  
pṛthivī śāntir āpaḥ śāntir oṣadhayaḥ śāntiḥ ।  
vanaspatayaḥ śāntir viśve devāḥ śāntir brahma śāntiḥ  
sarvaṃ śāntiḥ śāntir eva śāntiḥ  
sā mā śāntir edhi ॥

oṃ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ ॥

yat kṛtaṃ yad akṛtaṃ yad duṣkṛtaṃ yad vikṛtaṃ  
tat sarvaṃ agnaye sviṣṭakṛte samarpayāmi ।  
devebhyo namaḥ, ṛṣibhyo namaḥ, brahmaṇe namaḥ ।  
idam na mama ।

---

## वारकरी

॥ श्री विठ्ठलाय नमः ॥

जय जय राम कृष्ण हरी ।  
जय जय राम कृष्ण हरी ।  
जय जय राम कृष्ण हरी ॥

पुंडलिक वरदा हरी विठ्ठल ।  
श्री ज्ञानदेव तुकाराम ।  
पंढरीनाथ महाराज की जय ॥

हे पंढरीनाथा विठ्ठला,  
तुझ्या चरणी नमस्कार करितो/करिते।  
ही नोकरीची मुलाखत शांततेने, स्पष्ट बुद्धीने आणि सत्य व नम्र वाणीने पार पडो,  
मन प्रसन्न राहो, भीती दूर होवो, बोलणे सहज आणि योग्य होवो,  
योग्य परीक्षकांची कृपा व समज लाभो,  
धर्म, प्रामाणिकता आणि परिश्रमास अनुरूप चांगली संधी प्राप्त होवो।  
दुसऱ्याचे हक्क, भाग्य किंवा उपजीविका न हिरावता,  
सर्वांच्या मंगलात हे कार्य सिद्ध होवो।

माझ्या मनातील अहंकार, द्वेष, भीती आणि असत्य दूर होवो।  
नाम, भक्ती, दया आणि सत्य यांत माझे चित्त स्थिर होवो।

देवाचिये द्वारी उभा क्षणभरी ।  
तेणे मुक्ती चारी साधियेल्या ॥  
हरि मुखे म्हणा हरि मुखे म्हणा ।  
पुण्याची गणना कोण करी ॥

सुंदर ते ध्यान उभे विटेवरी ।  
कर कटावरी ठेवूनिया ॥  
तुळसीहार गळा कासे पितांबर ।  
आवडे निरंतर हेचि ध्यान ॥  
मकरकुंडले तळपती श्रवणी ।  
कंठी कौस्तुभमणी विराजित ॥  
तुका म्हणे माझे हेचि सर्व सुख ।  
पाहीन श्रीमुख आवडीने ॥

राम कृष्ण हरी ।  
राम कृष्ण हरी ।  
राम कृष्ण हरी ।  
विठ्ठल विठ्ठल जय हरी विठ्ठल ।  
विठ्ठल विठ्ठल जय हरी विठ्ठल ॥

हे विठ्ठला, नोकरीच्या मुलाखतीतील यश, प्रसन्नता, स्पष्टता आणि योग्य संधी हे तुझ्या चरणी अर्पण।  
जे काही कर्म, वचन, स्मरण, नाम आणि भक्ती येथे झाले,  
ते सर्व तुझ्याच चरणी समर्पित।

कायेन वाचा मनसेंद्रियैर्वा ।  
बुद्ध्यात्मना वा प्रकृतेः स्वभावात् ।  
करोमि यद्यत् सकलं परस्मै ।  
नारायणायेति समर्पयामि ॥

अवघे जन सुखी होवोत।  
जय जय राम कृष्ण हरी ।  
पुंडलिक वरदा हरी विठ्ठल ।  
श्री ज्ञानदेव तुकाराम ।  
पंढरीनाथ महाराज की जय ॥

---

## 格鲁派

**[皈依]**

sang gye chö dang tsog kyi chog nam la  
jang chub bar du dag ni kyab su chi  
dag gi jin sog gyi pe sö nam kyi  
dro la phän chir sang gye drub par shog  

**[发菩提心]**

dag dang ma nam kha nyam sem chen tam che  
la ma sang gye rin po che la kyab su chi  
jang chub sem chog rin po che kye war gyur chig  
dro kun phän de’i gyu ru gyur chig  

**[四无量心]**

sem chen tam che de wa dang de we gyu dang den par gyur chig  
dug ngal dang dug ngal gyi gyu dang dral war gyur chig  
dug ngal me pe de wa dang mi dral war gyur chig  
nye ring chag dang nyi dang dral we tang nyom la ne par gyur chig  

**[正行：宗喀巴祈请与文殊心咒]**

mig me tse wai ter chen chen re zig  
dri me khyen pai wang po jam pal yang  
du pung ma lu jom dze sang wai dag  
gang chen khe pai tsug gyen tsong kha pa  
lo zang drag pai zhab la sol wa deb  

oṃ āḥ guru vajradhara sumati kīrti siddhi hūṃ  

oṃ a ra pa ca na dhīḥ  
oṃ a ra pa ca na dhīḥ  
oṃ a ra pa ca na dhīḥ  

**[所愿陈白]**

愿此求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，心意安定，谈吐自若；  
愿所言真实、合宜、具智慧，所问所答皆能明白无碍；  
愿得遇赏识，觅得良缘，于正当事业中成就利己利他之因缘；  
不以此愿夺他人福报，不损他人机会，不逼迫他人心意；  
唯愿障碍净除，善缘成熟，所成一切悉为众生安乐与菩提资粮。  

**[回向]**

ge wa di yi nyur du dag  
la ma sang gye drub gyur ne  
dro wa chig kyang ma lu pa  
de yi sa la gö par shog  

jang chub sem chog rin po che  
ma kye pa nam kye gyur chig  
kye pa nyam pa me pa yang  
gong ne gong du phel war shog

---

## 不丹 Drukpa

sangs rgyas chos dang tshogs kyi mchog rnams la  
byang chub bar du bdag cag skyabs su mchi  
bdag cag gis sbyin sogs bgyis pa’i bsod nams kyis  
’gro la phan phyir sangs rgyas ’grub par shog  

bdag cag la sogs pa’i don du  
sems can thams cad bde ba dang bde ba’i rgyu dang ldan par gyur cig  
sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal gyi rgyu dang bral bar gyur cig  
sdug bsngal med pa’i bde ba dam pa dang mi ’bral bar gyur cig  
nye ring chags sdang gnyis dang bral ba’i btang snyoms la gnas par gyur cig  

dpal ldan ’brug pa’i bla ma brgyud pa dang  
dkon mchog gsum la dad pas gsol ba ’debs  
gu ru padma ’byung gnas kyis bar chad lam sel bar byin gyis rlobs  
thugs rje chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis bdag cag la thugs rjes gzigs  

oṃ maṇi padme hūṃ  
oṃ maṇi padme hūṃ  
oṃ maṇi padme hūṃ  

thugs rje chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug  
bdag cag la thugs rjes gzigs  
las don gyi ’dri rtsad thams cad legs par ’grub par byin gyis rlobs  
glo bur gnas skabs su blo gsal zhing dran pa mi nyams par byin gyis rlobs  
ngag ’jam zhing tshig gsal la brjod pa rang bzhin du ’byung bar byin gyis rlobs  
drang po’i bsam pa dang yon tan mthong ba’i skal ldan dang ’phrad par byin gyis rlobs  
rten ’brel bzang po dang chos dang mthun pa’i las skabs rnyed par byin gyis rlobs  
gzhan gyi bsod nams mi ’phrog  
gzhan gyi go skabs mi bcad  
su la’ang gnod pa mi ’gyur ba’i tshul du  
rang gzhan gnyis kyi don legs par ’grub par shog  

ge wa di yi nyur du bdag  
spyan ras gzigs dbang grub gyur nas  
’gro ba gcig kyang ma lus pa  
de yi sa la ’god par shog  

byang chub sems mchog rin po che  
ma skyes pa rnams skye gyur cig  
skyes pa nyams pa med pa yang  
gong nas gong du ’phel bar shog  

sangs rgyas chos dang tshogs kyi mchog rnams la  
byang chub bar du bdag cag skyabs su mchi  
byang chub sems mchog rin po che  
ma skyes pa rnams skye gyur cig  

oṃ maṇi padme hūṃ  
oṃ maṇi padme hūṃ  
oṃ maṇi padme hūṃ  

dge ba ’di yis skye bo kun  
bsod nams ye shes tshogs rdzogs shing  
bsod nams ye shes las byung ba’i  
dam pa sku gnyis thob par shog
