benedicta tu in mulieribus,  
et benedictus fructus ventris tui, Iesus.  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei,  
ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Ave Maria, gratia plena, Dominus tecum;  
benedicta tu in mulieribus,  
et benedictus fructus ventris tui, Iesus.  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei,  
ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

O mi Iesu, dimitte nobis peccata nostra,  
libera nos ab igne inferni,  
perduc in caelum omnes animas,  
praesertim eas, quae misericordiae tuae maxime indigent.

Salve, Regina, mater misericordiae;  
vita, dulcedo, et spes nostra, salve.  
Ad te clamamus, exsules filii Evae.  
Ad te suspiramus, gementes et flentes  
in hac lacrimarum valle.  
Eia ergo, advocata nostra,  
illos tuos misericordes oculos ad nos converte.  
Et Iesum, benedictum fructum ventris tui,  
nobis post hoc exsilium ostende.  
O clemens, O pia, O dulcis Virgo Maria.

Ora pro nobis, sancta Dei Genitrix.  
Ut digni efficiamur promissionibus Christi.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus,  
sancta Dei Genitrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

Kyrie, eleison.  
Christe, eleison.  
Kyrie, eleison.  
Christe, audi nos.  
Christe, exaudi nos.

Sancta Maria, ora pro nobis.  
Sancta Dei Genitrix, ora pro nobis.  
Sancta Virgo virginum, ora pro nobis.  
Mater Christi, ora pro nobis.  
Mater Ecclesiae, ora pro nobis.  
Mater misericordiae, ora pro nobis.  
Sedes Sapientiae, ora pro nobis.  
Causa nostrae laetitiae, ora pro nobis.  
Refugium peccatorum, ora pro nobis.  
Consolatrix afflictorum, ora pro nobis.  
Auxilium Christianorum, ora pro nobis.  
Regina sacratissimi Rosarii, ora pro nobis.  
Regina pacis, ora pro nobis.

Agnus Dei, qui tollis peccata mundi, parce nobis, Domine.  
Agnus Dei, qui tollis peccata mundi, exaudi nos, Domine.  
Agnus Dei, qui tollis peccata mundi, miserere nobis.

Ora pro nobis, sancta Dei Genitrix.  
Ut digni efficiamur promissionibus Christi.

Domine Deus, cuius Unigenitus per vitam, mortem et resurrectionem suam  
nobis salutis aeternae praemia comparavit:  
concede, quaesumus, ut haec mysteria sacratissimo beatae Mariae Virginis Rosario recolentes,  
et imitemur quod continent, et quod promittunt assequamur.  
Per eundem Christum Dominum nostrum. Amen.

Notre-Dame de Lourdes, priez pour nous.  
Sainte Bernadette, priez pour nous.

Maria, sine labe concepta, ora pro nobis qui ad te confugimus.

Pro hac intentione et pro colloquio laboris instanti,  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei, ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
ut cor sit quietum, mens vigilans, memoria ordinata,  
sermo verax, modestus et perspicuus,  
et ut ii qui audiunt recte discernant dona, laborem et voluntatem bonam.  
Si haec via utilis est ad maiorem Dei gloriam et ad bonum honestum,  
aperiat Dominus ianuam opportunam;  
sin autem, dirigat nos ad meliorem viam in pace.

Fiat voluntas tua.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Per Christum Dominum nostrum. Amen.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

## Հայ Առաքելական Եկեղեցի

Յանուն Հօր եւ Որդւոյ եւ Հոգւոյն Սրբոյ. Ամէն.

Ամենասուրբ Երրորդութիւն, Հայր եւ Որդի եւ Հոգի Սուրբ, լոյս անմատչելի եւ աղբիւր ամենայն բարեաց, յիշեա զծառայս քո եւ զամենայն որք կապեալ են այս խնդրուածով՝ զյաջողութիւն հարցման գործոյ, զպայծառութիւն մտաց, զխաղաղութիւն սրտի, զազատութիւն խօսից, զարդար ճանաչումն եւ զդուռ պատշաճաւոր աշխատանքի։

Ողորմեա ինձ, Աստուած, ըստ մեծի ողորմութեան քում.
եւ ըստ բազում գթութեան քում քաւեա զանօրէնութիւնս իմ.
Առաւել եւս լուա զիս յանօրէնութենէ իմմէ,
եւ ի մեղաց իմոց սրբեա զիս.

Ամբարձի զաչս իմ ի լերինս, ուստի եկեսցէ ինձ օգնութիւն.
Օգնութիւն իմ ի Տեառնէ, որ արար զերկինս եւ զերկիր.
Տէր պահեսցէ զմուտս քո եւ զելս քո,
այժմ եւ յաւիտեանս։

Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.
Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.
Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.

Հայր մեր, որ յերկինս ես,
սուրբ եղիցի անուն քո.
եկեսցէ արքայութիւն քո.
եղիցին կամք քո որպէս յերկինս եւ յերկրի.
զհաց մեր հանապազորդ տուր մեզ այսօր.
եւ թող մեզ զպարտիս մեր,
որպէս եւ մեք թողումք մերոց պարտապանաց.
եւ մի տանիր զմեզ ի փորձութիւն,
այլ փրկեա զմեզ ի չարէն.
զի քո է արքայութիւն եւ զօրութիւն եւ փառք յաւիտեանս. Ամէն.

Հաւատով խոստովանիմ եւ երկիր պագանեմ Քեզ,
Հայր եւ Որդի եւ Հոգի Սուրբ,
անեղ եւ անմահ բնութիւն.
արարիչ հրեշտակաց եւ մարդկան եւ ամենայն եղելոց.
ողորմեա քո արարածոց եւ ինձ բազմամեղիս.

Տէր Յիսուս Քրիստոս, Որդի Աստուծոյ կենդանւոյ,
լուր աղաչանաց ծառայի քո,
եւ ուղղեա զխնդրուածս այս՝ զի յաւուր հարցման գործոյ միտքն լինիցին պարզք, սիրտն՝ խաղաղ, լեզուն՝ հեզ եւ ճշմարիտ, երեսն՝ աներկիւղ, եւ գործն՝ ըստ քո սուրբ եւ փրկարար կամաց։

Բաց զդուռ արդար եւ օգտակար աշխատանքի, եթէ կամիս, Տէր, եւ տուր գտանել բարեհաճութիւն առանց հպարտութեան, պատիւ առանց զրկելոյ զայլս, եւ յաջողութիւն առանց վնասելոյ կամ խափանելոյ զճանապարհս եղբարց եւ քերց։ Ոչ խնդրեմք ի զրկումն այլոց, ոչ ի վնաս ումեք, այլ խաղաղութեամբ, արդարութեամբ եւ գոհութեամբ ընդունել զայն, զոր դու պատրաստես ի բարիս։

Բարեխօսութեամբ Սրբուհւոյ Աստուածածնին եւ միշտ Կուսին Մարիամու,
սրբոց առաքելոցն, սրբոց հայրապետացն,
սրբոյ Գրիգորի Լուսաւորչին,
սրբոյ Ներսէսի Շնորհալւոյ,
եւ ամենայն սրբոց քոց,
Տէր, ողորմեա.

Ընդունեա, Տէր, զայս խոնարհ աղօթս հաւատացելոց, ոչ իբրեւ առեւտուր եւ ոչ իբրեւ բռնութիւն կամ գուշակութիւն, այլ իբրեւ աղաչանք առ քո ողորմութիւն։ Պահեա զմեզ ի սուրբ հաւատս Եկեղեցւոյ, եւ զխորհուրդս, զօրհնութիւնս եւ զսրբազան պաշտօնս պահեա ի ձեռս կարգաւորեալ քահանայից քոց, իսկ մեզ շնորհեա ապաշխարութիւն, զգաստութիւն, աշխատանք արդար եւ խաղաղութիւն։

Փառք Հօր եւ Որդւոյ եւ Հոգւոյն Սրբոյ,
այժմ եւ միշտ եւ յաւիտեանս յաւիտենից. Ամէն.

---

## 灵恩派（Charismatic Movement）

天父，我奉主耶稣基督的名来到你面前，敬拜你、归向你；你是赐智慧、开道路、赐平安的主。为即将来到的求职面试，我把心思、言语、时间与结果都交托在你手中。

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

主耶稣基督，我承认你是主；我承认自己里面一切骄傲、惧怕、急躁、比较、虚假与不信，求你赦免我、洁净我。凡我在求职过程中亏欠人的地方，求你光照我，使我谦卑、诚实、尽责；我也饶恕一切曾使我受挫、被拒绝或被误解的人，把结果交在你公义与怜悯的手中。

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ· ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ, καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν· ἐγγίσατε τῷ θεῷ, καὶ ἐγγιεῖ ὑμῖν.

奉耶稣基督的名，我弃绝惧怕、混乱、自卑、夸大、谎言、讨好人的辖制与不义的依附；我断开一切使我失去清明、平安、诚实与节制的捆绑。凡不属于耶稣基督的搅扰，不得藉这次面试控制、欺骗、压迫或混乱我的心思意念。

σημεῖα δὲ τοῖς πιστεύσασιν ταῦτα παρακολουθήσει· ἐν τῷ ὀνόματί μου δαιμόνια ἐκβαλοῦσιν.

奉拿撒勒人耶稣基督的名，我抵挡一切惧怕、控告、混乱、灰心与谎言的黑暗权势；命令一切不洁、欺骗、压迫与搅扰离开，不得伤害、不得转移、不得返回，只按主耶稣基督的权柄退去。主啊，愿你的平安在我心中掌权。

圣灵，求你充满我；以真理、平安、圣洁、爱、信心与节制充满我的心。求你更新我的思想，使我临场清明；坚固我的心志，使我谈吐自若；赐我合宜的智慧，使我能真实表达能力、经验与品格。若有需要学习、预备、修正之处，求你光照我，使我殷勤而不焦虑，谦卑而不退缩。

κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ἐλέησον.

我为这次求职面试祈求：求你引导整个过程顺利，赐下合宜的时间、清楚的问题、准确的回应与彼此真实的认识。愿我得遇公正、明辨、愿意赏识合适人才的人；若这岗位是你所预备的良缘，求你开门，使我被看见、被理解、被接纳；若不是，求你温柔关闭，并引我进入更合宜的道路。

主啊，我不求操控任何人的意志，也不求夺取他人正当的机会；不愿因我的成功使别人受亏损、受羞辱或受伤害。愿你以公义安排道路，使每个人得着合宜的位置；愿我的求职不是出于贪婪或争竞，而是为忠心工作、供应生活、荣耀你的名。

天父，求你赐我面试前的安稳睡眠、清楚预备、准时到达与端正仪容；赐我倾听的耳、诚实的口、清醒的头脑与平稳的呼吸。愿我说当说的话，不夸口、不惧怕、不混乱；愿我的恩赐、经验与态度被合宜地呈现，也愿我能分辨这岗位是否与我的呼召、责任和品格相称。

主耶稣，我把面试官、招聘流程、沟通结果与未来去向都交托给你。愿你的旨意成就，愿你的国临到我的工作道路；凡需要修复的信心、秩序、责任与方向，求你按你的怜悯显明。

圣灵，求你保守这祷告在爱、温柔、清醒与圣经的秩序中；凡心中的感动、提醒与安慰，愿都被你的真理察验。求你使我不把压力、拒绝或人际难处轻易归咎黑暗，也不以属灵话语逃避预备、学习、沟通与应尽责任；愿我在平安中行动，在谦卑中等候，在感恩中领受。

感谢天父，感谢主耶稣基督，感谢圣灵。愿荣耀归给父、子、圣灵，从今时直到永远。

Ἀμήν.

---

## 科普特正教

Khen efran em-Phiot nem Pshiri nem Pi-epnevma Ethouab, Ounouti en-ouot. Amen.

Maren-shep-hmot entotk, O Peniot ethoteb, je ak-er-skepein ejon, ak-arithmeetin ejon, ak-areh eron, ak-shopten erok, ak-ti aso eron, ak-er-nosfin ejen nai nem nai.  
Etoi enhot, ari-vethin eron, ari-vethin em-pek-laos, ari-vethin en-tek-ekklisia ethmouab.

Eleison imas, O Theos, kata to mega eleos sou.  
Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison.

Nai nan, Vnouți, kata pek-nishti ennai; nem kata ep-ashai ente nek-met-shehnhēt ek-e-forg nem-moyi enna-novi.  
Pek-pnevma ethmouab em-per-olf evol haroi; moi nakhlom enou-pnevma ensouti.

Je Peniot et khen ni-fee-ou-ee,  
maref-touvo nje pekran,  
mares-i nje tekmetouro,  
petehnak maref-shopi emvriti khen etfe nem hijen pikahi.  
Pen-oik ente rastif moi nan emvoou.  
Ouoh ka ni-eteron nan evol,  
emvriti hon entenko evol ennet eouon entan erou.  
Ouoh mperenten ehoun epirasmoc,  
alla nahmen evol ha pipethoo-ou.  
Khen Pi-ekhristos Isos Penchois.  
Je thok te ti-metouro nem ti-gom nem pi-oo-ou sha eneh. Amen.

Agios O Theos,  
Agios Ischyros,  
Agios Athanatos,  
Eleison imas.

Doza Patri ke Yio ke Agio Pnevmati,  
ke nin ke aei ke is tous eonas ton eonon. Amen.

Agi’a Trias eleison imas.  
Kyrie, ilasthi tais amartiais imon.  
Despota, syngchorison tas anomias imon.  
Agie, episkepsai kai iasai tas astheneias imon, eneken tou onomatos sou.

主啊，圣三一上帝，求你以慈爱眷顾此求职面试：赐临场清明、心神安定、谈吐自若，使所言合乎真实、谦卑与智慧；若合乎你的圣意，求你开道路，使人得遇正当赏识，觅得良善合宜的机会。此求不夺他人机会，不损他人益处，不操控人的意志，只愿一切成于你的怜悯、公义与平安。

O Peniot ethoteb, through Isos Pikhristos Penchois, khen ti-metshenhēt ente Pi-epnevma Ethouab,  
ari-vethin em-pek-bok nem em-tek-boki.  
Shopi nemon khen pai-hwb, khen nai nem hirenē.  
Ari-vethin e-nen-tiho kata pek-ouōsh ethmouab,  
ouoh em-pi-ouōsh ente pirōmi.

Ten-tiho nem ten-tōbh evol hiten ni-eshlyl ente Ti-theotokos ethmouab Maria,  
nem pi-archangelos Mikhaēl,  
nem pi-archangelos Gabriēl,  
nem abba Markos pi-evangelistes,  
nem ni-apoctolos, ni-martyros, ni-agioc tēr-ou:  
Pchois ari-hmot nan em-pi-ko evol ente nen-novi.

Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison.

Je thok pe pi-oo-ou nem pi-tai-o nem ti-proskynesis,  
nem Pekiot en-agathos,  
nem Pi-epnevma Ethouab enreftanḫo,  
isjen ti-nou nem sha eneh ente ni-eneh tēr-ou. Amen.

---

## 菲律宾 El Shaddai

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

El Shaddai, El Shaddai, El Elyon na Adonai,  
we praise You, we worship You, we thank You, and we glorify Your holy name.

Lord Jesus Christ, have mercy on us.  
Panginoon, maawa ka.  
Kristo, maawa ka.  
Panginoon, maawa ka.

Our Father, who art in heaven,  
hallowed be thy name;  
thy kingdom come;  
thy will be done on earth as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread;  
and forgive us our trespasses,  
as we forgive those who trespass against us;  
and lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil. Amen.

You who dwell in the shelter of the Most High,  
who abide in the shade of the Almighty,  
say to the LORD, “My refuge and fortress,  
my God in whom I trust.”  
He will rescue you from the fowler’s snare,  
from the destroying plague,  
He will shelter you with his pinions,  
and under his wings you may take refuge;  
his faithfulness is a protecting shield.

Lord Jesus Christ,  
we bring before You this intention:  
May the job interview be peaceful and well ordered; grant a clear mind in the moment, calm speech, honest confidence, and the grace to be understood and appreciated. Open the right door to fitting work, good discernment, and a worthy opportunity according to Your will.

If we entrust an event to You, order our time, words, travel, labor, and decisions according to Your will.  
Guide every answer with truth and humility.  
Remove confusion, fear, and unnecessary obstacles without harm to anyone.  
Let this success dispossess no one, diminish no one, and manipulate no one’s will; may it come only through justice, merit, mercy, and peace.

Therefore I tell you, all that you ask for in prayer,  
believe that you will receive it and it shall be yours.

Lord, not as a bargain and not by our power,  
but according to Your mercy and holy will,  
we ask this in the name of Jesus Christ. Amen.

Hail Mary, full of grace, the Lord is with thee;  
blessed art thou among women,  
and blessed is the fruit of thy womb, Jesus.  
Holy Mary, Mother of God,  
pray for us sinners,  
now and at the hour of our death. Amen.

Glory be to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit,  
as it was in the beginning, is now, and ever shall be,  
world without end. Amen.

May the Lord bless us, protect us from all evil,  
keep us faithful in prayer, honest in work, generous in heart,  
and bring us to everlasting life. Amen.

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

---

## 耶和华见证人

耶和华我们的天父，יהוה，

愿你的名被尊为圣；愿你的王国和旨意在我们心里居首位。我们承认你是听祷告的上帝，也愿意在凡事上先寻求你的认可。

我们为这次求职面试到你面前祷告。求你帮助我们在面试前后保持清醒、安静、谦卑和诚实；临场时思路清楚，谈吐自然，回答合宜，不被焦虑或骄傲牵引。

求你赐我们智慧，使我们能真实地表达能力与经验，也能分辨这份工作是否适合良心、生活责任和属灵需要。若这机会合乎你的旨意，愿相关的人能公平地看见合适之处；我们不求控制任何人的决定，也不求夺取他人的机会或损害他人的益处。

求你供应今日所需，帮助我们以正直方式寻找工作，耐心等候，勤恳预备，并在结果未明时仍信赖你。也求你帮助我们宽恕别人、保持和睦，不因压力说出不当的话或作出不诚实的事。

我们感谢你赐下生命、理智、学习的机会，以及弟兄姊妹和身边人的关怀。无论结果如何，求你帮助我们保持属灵清醒，把这件事交在你手中，继续尊重你的名，寻求你的王国和正义。

耶和华，我们只愿向你祷告，凡事照你的旨意而行；愿我们借着独一的中保，怀着洁净的良心亲近你。

奉耶稣基督的名祷告，阿们。

---

## 菲律宾 Iglesia ni Cristo

Amang banal, Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan Mo.

Lumapit kami sa Iyo na may pagpapakumbaba.  
Kinikilala naming Ikaw ang tunay na Diyos,  
ang Maylalang, ang nagbibigay-buhay,  
at ang tanging dapat naming sambahin.

Ama, patawarin Mo po kami sa aming mga pagkukulang,  
sa aming mga kasalanan,  
at sa anumang hindi naging kalugud-lugod sa Iyong harapan.  
Linisin Mo po ang aming puso at kalooban,  
at tulungan Mo kaming makasunod sa Iyong mga salita.

Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan Mo.  
Dumating nawa ang kaharian Mo.  
Sundin nawa ang loob Mo,  
dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan Mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin Mo kami sa aming mga utang,  
gaya naman namin na nagpatawad sa mga may utang sa amin.  
At huwag Mo kaming ihatid sa tukso,  
kundi iligtas Mo kami sa masama.

Ama, inilalapit po namin sa Iyo ang nalalapit na pakikipanayam para sa trabaho.  
Hinihiling po namin na maging maayos ang lahat ng paghahanda at pagharap dito.  
Pagkalooban Mo po kami ng maliwanag na pag-iisip, payapang loob,  
maingat na pananalita, at kakayahang sumagot nang may katapatan,  
paggalang, at kahinahunan.

Kung ito po ay ayon sa Iyong kalooban,  
buksan Mo ang mabuting pagkakataon,  
at ipagkaloob na ang mga taong makakausap ay makakita ng sipag,  
kakayahan, kabutihang-asal, at tunay na hangaring maglingkod nang tapat.  
Nawa’y matagpuan ang gawaing nararapat, malinis, at kapaki-pakinabang,  
na hindi maglalayo sa amin sa pagsunod sa Iyong mga utos.

Hindi po namin hinihiling ang tagumpay na makapipinsala sa kapwa,  
hindi upang agawan ang iba ng kabuhayan,  
at hindi upang manaig sa pamamagitan ng pandaraya o kapalaluan.  
Ang hinihiling po namin ay patnubay, karunungan, at kaloob Mong mabuti,  
ayon sa Iyong katuwiran at kalooban.

Ingatan Mo po ang aming katawan, isip, at puso.  
Ilayo Mo po kami sa takot, pagkalito, pagmamadali,  
at sa anumang salita o kilos na hindi magiging marapat sa Iyong harapan.  
Patnubayan Mo po ang aming mga pagpapasiya,  
upang manatili kaming mapagpakumbaba, matapat, at masunurin.

Idinadalangin po namin ang Iglesia, ang mga kapatid,  
at ang mga namumuno sa paglilingkod,  
na patuloy Mong patnubayan sa pagsunod sa Iyong kalooban.  
Idinadalangin din po namin ang aming sambahayan,  
na pagpalain Mo ng pagkakaisa, pagtitiis, at pagtitiwala sa Iyo.

Hindi po ang aming sariling kalooban ang masunod,  
kundi ang kalooban Mo.  
Turuan Mo kaming tanggapin ang Iyong pasiya,  
magtiwala sa Iyong awa,  
at manatiling tapat maging anuman ang maging bunga.

Ama, sa Iyo lamang kami dumudulog at sumasamba.  
Sa Iyo lamang namin inihahain ang pasasalamat, papuri, at kahilingan.  
Patuloy Mo po kaming akayin sa matuwid na landas,  
iligtas sa masama,  
at panatilihin sa pananampalataya at pagsunod.

Ang lahat ng ito ay aming hinihiling at idinadalangin  
sa pangalan ng aming Panginoong Jesucristo.

Amen.

---

## 静修主义 Hesychasm

Εἰς τὸ ὄνομα τοῦ Πατρὸς καὶ τοῦ Υἱοῦ καὶ τοῦ Ἁγίου Πνεύματος. Ἀμήν.

Δόξα σοι, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον τὴν συνέντευξιν τῆς ἐργασίας· δὸς νηφαλιότητα νοῦ, πραότητα καρδίας, καὶ λόγον σώφρονα.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, εἰ θέλημά σου ἅγιον ἐστίν, ἄνοιξον ὁδὸν δικαίαν, ἵνα εὑρεθῇ θέσις πρόσφορος καὶ ἄνθρωποι εὔγνωμονες, οὐκ ἀφαιρουμένη εὐλογίαν ἑτέρου, οὐδὲ βλάπτουσα τινά.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε, φύλαξόν με ἐν ταπεινώσει καὶ νήψει· μὴ κατὰ τὸ θέλημά μου, ἀλλὰ κατὰ τὸ σὸν ἅγιον θέλημα· ἀπάλλαξόν με ἀπὸ πλάνης, κενοδοξίας, καὶ ταραχῆς.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

---

## Lutheran

In nomine Patris et Filii et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Adiutorium nostrum in nomine Domini,  
qui fecit caelum et terram.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum misericordiam tuam;  
secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.

Kyrie eleison.  
Christe eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Credo in Deum Patrem omnipotentem, creatorem caeli et terrae.  
Et in Iesum Christum, Filium eius unicum, Dominum nostrum,  
qui conceptus est de Spiritu Sancto,  
natus ex Maria virgine,  
passus sub Pontio Pilato,  
crucifixus, mortuus, et sepultus,  
descendit ad inferos,  
tertia die resurrexit a mortuis,  
ascendit ad caelos,  
sedet ad dexteram Dei Patris omnipotentis,  
inde venturus est iudicare vivos et mortuos.  
Credo in Spiritum Sanctum,  
sanctam ecclesiam catholicam,  
sanctorum communionem,  
remissionem peccatorum,  
carnis resurrectionem,  
et vitam aeternam. Amen.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo.  
Amen.

Domine Deus, Pater caelestis,  
per Iesum Christum Filium tuum, Dominum nostrum,  
respice in misericordia super hanc petitionem pro colloquio laboris.  
Non in meritis nostris confidimus,  
sed in sola misericordia tua et in promissione evangelii tui.

Da mentem claram, cor quietum, sermonem moderatum et liberum;  
aperi, si voluntas tua est, viam honestam ad opus dignum,  
ubi dona a te data recte adhibeantur,  
et ubi favor iustus atque prudentia inveniantur.  
Concede ut responsa sint vera, humilia, sapientia plena;  
remove timorem inutilem, confusionem et superbiam;  
dirige iudicia interrogantium et respondentis in aequitate.

Non petimus ut alii spolientur, deprimantur, aut iniuste praeveniantur;  
sed ut fiat voluntas tua, et panis quotidianus sine iniuria proximi detur.  
Si haec via bona est, confirma eam;  
si alia melior est, conduce nos ad eam in pace.

In manus tuas, Domine, commendamus hoc negotium et omnem sollicitudinem cordis;  
redemisti nos, Domine Deus veritatis.  
Per Iesum Christum, Dominum nostrum. Amen.

Benedicamus Domino.  
Deo gratias.

Benedicat nos omnipotens et misericors Dominus,  
Pater et Filius et Spiritus Sanctus. Amen.

---

## 埃塞俄比亚 Tewahedo

Bä-səmə ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus, ʾAhadu ʾAmlak. ʾAmen.

Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäwälädä ʾəm-qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäṣäwwärä bəʾəntitänä, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäqäbärä wä-tänśəʾa ʾəmən-mutan, täsahalänä.

ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.

Ṣälotä haymanot:  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾAmlak, ʾAb, ʾamlakä kullu,  
zägäbärä sämayat wä-mədər, zäyətarʾay wä-zäʾiyətarʾay.  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾEgziʾ, Iyyäsus Krəstos, Wäldä ʾAmlak,  
Wäldä ʾAb waḥid, zətawälädä ʾəm-ʾAb qädmä kullu zämän.

Dawit:  
Täsaḥaläni ʾEgziʾo bəkämä ʿabiy məḥrätəkä,  
wä-bəkämä bəzuh rəḥrəhəkä ḥəddäg ʿamäṣaʾəya.  
ʾAṣḥəḥäni ʾəm-ʿamäṣaʾəya,  
wä-ʾəm-ḥaṭiʾatəya ʾanṣəḥäni.

ʾAntä ʾEgziʾo, ʾamlakä ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus,  
bə-məḥrätəkä täsähal, wä-səmaʿ ṣälotänä.  
Bəʾəntä məngädä səraḥ, wä-bəʾəntä säʾalä qalat,  
habänä ləbbä ṣəruy, ḥasabä rətuʿ, wä-qalä sälam.  
ʾAḍḥən ləbbä ʾəm-fərəhat, ʾaṣnaʿ nəfsä bə-ṭənt,  
wä-ʾabsəḥ ʾafä bä-qal zä-yətaʾammän wä-zä-yəstaḥəbb.  
ʾEgziʾo, fätäḥ ʾəntä yähäyyəs məngädä ṭəbb,  
wä-ʾamləkä ḥassabä ṣadəq ḫäbä zä-yəsmaʿun.  
ʾI-nəśʿal zəntu bä-ḥəsäd, wä-ʾi-bä-məḥṣänatä ʾahadu;  
ʾi-nəsärrəq wä-ʾi-näḍərr ḫäbä bäʾəsä ʾəḥu;  
ʾala bä-fəqadəkä, bä-ṣədq, bä-səlam, wä-bä-məḥrät.

Bäṣälotä qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan məlʾəkt,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan wä-ṣadəqan,  
ʾEgziʾo, səmaʿ ṣälotänä,  
wä-ʾabṣaḥ länä səlamäka wä-məḥrätəkä.

Abunä zäbä-sämayat,  
yitqäddäs səməkä;  
təmṣaʾ mängəśtəkä;  
yəkun fəqadəkä bä-kämä bä-sämay, kämä bä-mədər.  
Sisanä zä-zäntä ʿəlätä habänä yom;  
ḥədäg länä aṣəḥatänä,  
kämä nəḥna nəḥädäg lä-zä-aṣḥaḥunä;  
ʾi taʾabbanä ḫäbä mənsut,  
ʾala adḥənänä wä-ʾaḍḥənänä ʾəm-kullu ʾəkuy.  
ʾIsmä ziʾakä yəʾəti mängəśt,  
wä-ḥayl, wä-səbḥat,  
läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

Səbḥat läʾAb, səbḥat läWäld,  
səbḥat läMänfäs Qəddus,  
ʾəntä kämä bəqədmə ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəʾəti ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəkun läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

Bä-sərrʿätä Beta Krəstiyan, zəntu yəkun ṣälotä rəḥrəh,  
ʾi-qəddase, ʾi-ḥədägä ḥaṭiʾat, ʾi-masḥä qidusan, ʾi-sərrʿätä gənzät, ʾi-mawṣəʾä ʾaganənt;  
məsṭiratä ʾEgziʾabəḥer yəkun bəʾədə kahənatä qidusan.  
ʾEgziʾo, bä-fəqadəkä wä-bä-məḥrätəkä, sälam lä-kullu. ʾAmen.

---

## الكنيسة المارونية

B-shmo d-Abo w-d-Bro w-d-Ruho d-Qudsho, Had Aloho shariro. Amin.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Hayelthono,  
Qadishat lo Moyutho,  
ethraham ‘alayn.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Abun d-bashmayo,  
netqadash shmokh.  
Tite malkuthokh.  
Nehwe sebyonokh,  
aykano d-bashmayo oph bar‘o.  
Haw lan lahmo d-sunqonan yawmono.  
Washboq lan hawbayn wahtohayn,  
aykano doph hnan shbaqn l-hayyobayn.  
Wlo ta‘lan l-nesyuno,  
elo fasso lan men bisho.  
Metul d-dilokh hi malkutho w-haylo w-teshbuhto  
l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Shlom lekh Maryam,  
mlayat taybutho,  
Moran ‘amekh.  
Mbarakhto at b-neshe,  
w-mbarakh hu piro d-karsekh,  
Maran Yeshua.  
O qadishto Maryam,  
Yoldath Aloho,  
saloy hlofayn hnaye,  
hosho w-bsho‘at mawthan. Amin.

Moran Yeshua Mshiha,  
Bro d-Aloho hayo,  
qabel sluthan b-rahmayk.

愿求职面试一切顺利；临场心思清明，谈吐自若，言语合宜；得遇赏识，觅得正当良缘与合适岗位。此求不夺他人机会，不损他人福分，不以强迫他人意志为意向，惟愿在真理、和平与公义中成就。

B-shfa‘otho d-Yoldath Aloho Maryam,  
w-d-Mor Maron,  
w-d-Mor Efram,  
w-d-Mor Ya‘qub,  
w-d-Mor Sharbel,  
w-d-kulhon qadisho,  
Moryo etraham ‘alayn.

Nhoor, Moryo, mad‘an b-nuhrokh,  
w-fthah saphwathan b-shaynokh.  
Haw lan meltho rakhikhto w-shariro,  
lebo nisho,  
ruho shayno,  
w-tar‘e d-taybutho,  
ayk sebyonokh qadisho.

Dkar, Moryo, l-‘abdayk w-l-amhotokh,  
kulhon hayye d-sabreen b-rahmayk,  
w-kulhon d-ba‘eyn pulhono keno w-lahmo d-sunqono.

Dkar, Moryo, l-‘anide mhaymne,  
w-a‘med enon b-nuhro d-afayk,  
b-rahmayk saggiye.

Moryo, nhoor lan b-nuhrokh,  
nattar lan b-slibokh,  
shadar ‘alayn rahmayk,  
w-ahlan b-shaynokh.  
Nehwe sebyonokh,  
w-la sebyonan;  
b-rahmayk netqabel,  
w-b-shaynokh neshtalem.

Lakh shubho,  
l-Abokh iqoro,  
w-l-Ruho d-Qudsho segedto,  
hosho w-bkul zban  
w-l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

---

## 摩门教（LDS）

亲爱的天父，

我们感谢你赐下生命、机会、学习与工作的能力，也感谢你借着你的儿子耶稣基督赐给我们盼望，并愿意借圣灵引导寻求智慧的人。

我们承认耶稣基督是我们的救主和中保，恳求圣灵在求职面试之时同在，使心思清明、情绪平稳、言语合宜、态度诚恳，能够清楚表达所预备的内容，并以谦卑、正直和自信面对每一个问题。

求你开启合宜的道路，使面试过程一切顺利；若这份工作符合你的旨意，愿能得遇赏识，觅得良好的职业机会与合适的工作缘分。也求你帮助我们不以骄傲或焦虑行事，不求夺取他人的机会或福分，只愿在正义、公平与勤勉中接受你所预备的祝福。

愿你的旨意成就；若结果与所愿不同，也求你赐下平安、辨识力与继续前行的力量，使我们能信靠你的时间和安排，并在一切事上纪念救主、遵守诫命、跟随圣灵的提示。

我们这样祈求，是奉耶稣基督的名，阿们。

---

## മലങ്കര ഓർത്തഡോക്സ് സുറിയാനി സഭ

B-shem Abo w-Bro w-Ruho d-Qudsho, Hado Aloho Shariro.  
Shubho leh, w-‘alayn raḥme w-ḥanono neshtaf‘un l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Abun d-bashmayo,  
nethqadash shmokh,  
tithe malkuthokh,  
nehwe sebyonokh,  
aykano d-bashmayo af b-ar‘o.  
Hab lan lahmo d-sunqonan yawmono.  
Washbuq lan ḥawbayn wa-ḥṭohayn,  
aykano d-af ḥnan shbaqan l-ḥayobayn.  
W-lo ta‘lan l-nesyuno,  
ella paṣṣan men bisho.  
Metol d-dilokh hi malkutho w-ḥaylo w-teshbuḥto  
l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Moran etraḥem ‘alayn.  
Moran ḥus w-raḥem ‘alayn.  
Moran ‘ani w-raḥem ‘alayn.  
Shubho lokh Moran.  
Shubho lokh Moran.  
Shubho lokh sabran l-‘olam.

Mizmor 50/51:  
Raḥem ‘alay Aloho ayk ṭaybuthokh;  
w-ayk sugo d-raḥmayk ‘ṭi ḥṭohay.  
Asgo mashigani men ‘awli,  
w-men ḥṭithi dakani.  
Meṭul d-‘awli ana yoda‘,  
w-ḥṭithi luqbalay hi b-kholzban.

Mizmor 90/91:  
D-yotheb b-sethro d-‘Elyono,  
b-ṭelolo d-Aloho nethnaga.  
Emar l-Moryo: Beth gawsī w-beth tawklanī,  
Alohi d-‘alaw tawkleth.

കർത്താവായ ദൈവമേ, നിന്റെ കരുണയാൽ ഈ തൊഴിൽ അഭിമുഖത്തിന്റെ സമയത്ത് മനസ്സിന് തെളിച്ചവും ഹൃദയത്തിന് സമാധാനവും നാവിന് മിതത്വവും ധൈര്യവും തരണമേ. ചോദ്യങ്ങൾ കേൾക്കുമ്പോൾ വിവേകവും ഉത്തരം പറയുമ്പോൾ സൗമ്യതയും സത്യസന്ധതയും തരണമേ. ന്യായമായ പരിഗണനയും യോഗ്യമായ അംഗീകാരവും ലഭിക്കുവാൻ കൃപ ചെയ്യണമേ; നിന്റെ വിശുദ്ധ ഇഷ്ടത്തിൽ അനുയോജ്യമായ വാതിലും നല്ല അവസരവും തുറക്കണമേ. മറ്റുള്ളവരുടെ നന്മ അപഹരിക്കാതെ, ആരെയും നഷ്ടപ്പെടുത്താതെ, നീതിയിലും സമാധാനത്തിലും ഈ കാര്യത്തെ നയിക്കണമേ.

Moryo Aloho, b-raḥmayk qabel ṣlutho hode,  
la b-zedqo d-dilan, ella b-raḥme d-dilokh.  
Nṭar, ḥayel, shayen, w-nahhar ‘abdayk;  
w-hawi sebyonokh, la sebyonan,  
b-shubḥo d-Abo w-d-Bro w-d-Ruho d-Qudsho.

Dukhrono d-Yoldath Aloho Maryam,  
w-d-qadishe kulhon,  
nehwe ‘amman l-‘olam. Amin.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.  
Haleluya, Haleluya, Haleluya, shubho lokh Aloho.  
Amin.

## 东正教 圣礼礼仪派

为求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，谈吐自若，得遇赏识，并觅得合宜良缘；但不夺他人机会，不损他人益处，惟愿按主圣善旨意成就。

Εὐλογημένη ἡ βασιλεία τοῦ Πατρὸς καὶ τοῦ Υἱοῦ καὶ τοῦ Ἁγίου Πνεύματος, νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων.  
Ἀμήν.

Βασιλεῦ οὐράνιε, Παράκλητε, τὸ Πνεῦμα τῆς ἀληθείας, ὁ πανταχοῦ παρὼν καὶ τὰ πάντα πληρῶν, ὁ θησαυρὸς τῶν ἀγαθῶν καὶ ζωῆς χορηγός, ἐλθὲ καὶ σκήνωσον ἐν ἡμῖν, καὶ καθάρισον ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ πάσης κηλῖδος, καὶ σῶσον, Ἀγαθέ, τὰς ψυχὰς ἡμῶν.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

Παναγία Τριάς, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς· Κύριε, ἱλάσθητι ταῖς ἁμαρτίαις ἡμῶν· Δέσποτα, συγχώρησον τὰς ἀνομίας ἡμῖν· Ἅγιε, ἐπίσκεψαι καὶ ἴασαι τὰς ἀσθενείας ἡμῶν, ἕνεκεν τοῦ ὀνόματός σου.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς· ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου· ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου· γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου, ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς· τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον· καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν, ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφίεμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν· καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν, ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Ἐλέησόν με, ὁ Θεός, κατὰ τὸ μέγα ἔλεός σου, καὶ κατὰ τὸ πλῆθος τῶν οἰκτιρμῶν σου ἐξάλειψον τὸ ἀνόμημά μου.  
Ἐπὶ πλεῖον πλῦνόν με ἀπὸ τῆς ἀνομίας μου, καὶ ἀπὸ τῆς ἁμαρτίας μου καθάρισόν με.  
Ὅτι τὴν ἀνομίαν μου ἐγὼ γινώσκω, καὶ ἡ ἁμαρτία μου ἐνώπιόν μού ἐστι διὰ παντός.

Ἐν εἰρήνῃ τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῆς ἄνωθεν εἰρήνης καὶ τῆς σωτηρίας τῶν ψυχῶν ἡμῶν, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῆς εὐοδώσεως τοῦ προκειμένου ἔργου καὶ τῆς συνεντεύξεως, καὶ ὑπὲρ νοὸς νηφαλίου, καρδίας εἰρηνικῆς, λόγου σαφοῦς καὶ πραέος, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ γενέσθαι πᾶν κατὰ τὸ ἅγιον θέλημα τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἄνευ φθόνου, ἄνευ ἀδικίας, καὶ ἄνευ ἀφαιρέσεως τοῦ ἀγαθοῦ τῶν πλησίον, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ εὑρεῖν εὔνοιαν, διάκρισιν καὶ ἀγαθὴν ἀνταπόκρισιν παρὰ τοῖς ἀνθρώποις, καὶ τόπον ἁρμόδιον πρὸς ἔργον τίμιον καὶ ὠφέλιμον, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ ῥυσθῆναι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ ταραχῆς, φόβου, ἀθυμίας, κενοδοξίας καὶ παντὸς λόγου ταραχώδους, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ἀντιλαβοῦ, σῶσον, ἐλέησον καὶ διαφύλαξον ἡμᾶς, ὁ Θεός, τῇ σῇ χάριτι.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Τῆς Παναγίας, ἀχράντου, ὑπερευλογημένης, ἐνδόξου Δεσποίνης ἡμῶν Θεοτόκου καὶ ἀειπαρθένου Μαρίας, μετὰ πάντων τῶν ἁγίων μνημονεύσαντες, ἑαυτοὺς καὶ ἀλλήλους καὶ πᾶσαν τὴν ζωὴν ἡμῶν Χριστῷ τῷ Θεῷ παραθώμεθα.  
Σοί, Κύριε.

Ὁ κατοικῶν ἐν βοηθείᾳ τοῦ Ὑψίστου, ἐν σκέπῃ τοῦ Θεοῦ τοῦ οὐρανοῦ αὐλισθήσεται.  
Ἐρεῖ τῷ Κυρίῳ· Ἀντιλήπτωρ μου εἶ καὶ καταφυγή μου, ὁ Θεός μου, καὶ ἐλπιῶ ἐπ’ αὐτόν.  
Ὅτι αὐτὸς ῥύσεταί σε ἐκ παγίδος θηρευτῶν καὶ ἀπὸ λόγου ταραχώδους.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ὁ φωτίζων πάντα ἄνθρωπον ἐρχόμενον εἰς τὸν κόσμον, δὸς νηφαλιότητα τῷ νοΐ, εἰρήνην τῇ καρδίᾳ, σωφροσύνην τῷ λογισμῷ, καὶ χάριν λόγου ἀληθοῦς καὶ ἀταράχου. Εὐόδωσον τὸ προκείμενον ἔργον, εἰ συμφέρει τῇ σωτηρίᾳ, καὶ ὁδήγησον εἰς ὁδὸν ἀγαθὴν, ἵνα ἐν παντὶ δοξάζηται τὸ πανάγιον ὄνομά σου.

Ὑπεραγία Θεοτόκε, σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Πάντες οἱ ἅγιοι, πρεσβεύσατε ὑπὲρ ἡμῶν.

Δόξα σοι, Χριστὲ ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἡ ἐλπὶς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Δι’ εὐχῶν τῶν ἁγίων Πατέρων ἡμῶν, Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἐλέησον καὶ σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἀμήν.

---

## Ritus Hispano-Mozarabicus

V. Dominus sit semper vobiscum.  
R. Et cum spiritu tuo.

Gloria et honor Patri et Filio et Spiritui Sancto,  
in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Psalmus:  
Qui habitat in adiutorio Altissimi,  
in protectione Dei caeli commorabitur.  
Dicet Domino: Susceptor meus es tu et refugium meum;  
Deus meus, sperabo in eum.  
Quoniam ipse liberavit me de laqueo venantium,  
et a verbo aspero.  
Scapulis suis obumbrabit tibi,  
et sub pennis eius sperabis.

Lauda:  
Verbum meum et meditatio cordis mei  
sit placita in conspectu tuo, Domine,  
adiutor meus et redemptor meus.

Oratio admonitionis:  
Oremus, fratres carissimi, Dominum Deum omnipotentem,  
pro opere iusto quaerendo,  
pro congressu interrogationis et probationis,  
pro serenitate mentis, libertate sermonis,  
rectitudine cordis et honesta aestimatione;  
ut Spiritus Sanctus illuminet memoriam, temperet affectum,  
aperiat os ad verba simplicia et vera,  
et dirigat vias in opportunitatem bonam,  
non per invidiam, non per fraudem,  
non auferendo bona aliena neque minuendo sortem proximi,  
sed secundum misericordiam et voluntatem Dei.

R. Praesta, aeterne omnipotens Deus.

Alia:  
Deus, qui corda fidelium illustratione Sancti Spiritus doces,  
respice propitius super hanc necessitatem laboris;  
aufer confusionem, metum immoderatum et perturbationem cordis;  
da mentem claram, linguam modestam, vultum quietum,  
responsa prudentia condita et fiducia humilitate temperata.  
Fac inveniri gratiam coram eis qui discernunt,  
si hoc saluti et bono communi congruit;  
et concede laboris locum honestum, pacificum et utilem,  
ubi dona tua fideliter exerceantur,  
et vita recta sustentetur.

Post nomina:  
Memor esto, Domine, omnium quaerentium panem quotidianum  
per laborem iustum et dignum;  
memor esto eorum qui portas laboris aperire possunt,  
ut iudicent sine acceptione personarum,  
cum aequitate, sapientia et benignitate.  
Memor esto etiam famulorum famularumque tuarum defunctorum,  
et dona eis locum refrigerii, lucis et pacis.

R. Amen.

Ad pacem:  
Pacem tuam, Domine Iesu Christe,  
quam dedisti discipulis tuis, conserva in nobis;  
mitiga anxietatem, dissolve superbiam, comprime verba vana,  
et corda nostra in caritate tua confirma.  
Sit in hoc congressu pax, veritas et mutua reverentia;  
sit sermo sine dolo, auditus sine contemptu,  
discernimentum sine iniustitia.

R. Amen.

Trisagium:  
Sanctus Deus, Sanctus Fortis, Sanctus Immortalis,  
miserere nobis.

Sanctus:  
Sanctus, Sanctus, Sanctus Dominus Deus Sabaoth.  
Pleni sunt caeli et terra gloria tua.  
Hosanna in excelsis.  
Benedictus qui venit in nomine Domini.  
Hosanna in excelsis.

Pater noster:  
Pater noster, qui es in caelis:  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Completuria:  
Libera nos, Domine, ab omni malo,  
praeterito, praesenti et futuro;  
intercedente sancta et gloriosa Dei Genitrice Maria,  
cum beatis apostolis, sancto Isidoro,  
et omnibus sanctis tuis,  
da propitius pacem in diebus nostris.  
Non nobis, Domine, non nobis, sed nomini tuo da gloriam;  
quod petitur, tua voluntate purificetur,  
tua misericordia ordinetur,  
tua Ecclesiae pace custodiatur,  
ut haec precatio sit humilis et privata,  
sine praesumptione mysteriorum sacrorum,  
sine commercio mercedis, sine dominatione voluntatum,  
sed in fide catholica, in spe sincera, in caritate perfecta.

R. Amen.

V. In nomine Domini nostri Iesu Christi perficiatur oratio nostra cum pace.  
R. Amen.

Gloria et honor Patri et Filio et Spiritui Sancto,  
in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

---

## старообрядцы

Во имя Отца и Сына и Святаго Духа. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй мя грешнаго.

Царю Небесныи, Утешителю, Душе истинныи, иже везде сыи и вся исполняя, сокровище благих и жизни подателю, прииди и вселися в ны, и очисти ны от всякия скверны, и спаси, Блаже, душа наша.

Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Пресвятая Троице, помилуй нас. Господи, очисти грехи наша. Владыко, прости беззакония наша. Святыи, посети и исцели немощи наша, имене Твоего ради.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Отче наш, иже еси на небесех, да святится имя Твое, да приидет Царствие Твое, да будет воля Твоя, яко на небеси и на земли. Хлеб наш насущныи даждь нам днесь, и остави нам долги наша, якоже и мы оставляем должником нашим, и не введи нас во искушение, но избави нас от лукаваго.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Верую во единаго Бога Отца, Вседержителя, Творца небу и земли, видимым же всем и невидимым. И во единаго Господа Исуса Христа, Сына Божия, Единороднаго, иже от Отца рожденнаго прежде всех век. Света от Света, Бога истинна от Бога истинна, рожденна, а не сотворенна, единосущна Отцу, Имже вся быша. Нас ради человек и нашего ради спасения сшедшаго с небес, и воплотившагося от Духа Свята и Марии Девы, и вочеловечшася. Распятаго же за ны при Понтийстем Пилате, и страдавша, и погребенна. И воскресшаго в третии день по Писанием. И возшедшаго на небеса, и седяща одесную Отца. И паки грядущаго со славою судити живым и мертвым, Его же Царствию несть конца. И в Духа Святаго, Господа истиннаго и животворящаго, иже от Отца исходящаго, иже со Отцем и Сыном спокланяема и сславима, глаголавшаго пророки. Во едину святую соборную и апостольскую Церковь. Исповедую едино крещение во оставление грехов. Чаю воскресения мертвым, и жизни будущаго века. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, призри милостивно на прошение о предстоящем собеседовании и о начале дела сего: просвети ум, умири сердце, укрепи память, даруй слово кротко и разумно, да будет ответ ясен, речь свободна, лице спокойно, мысль трезвенна, и да обрящется благоволение у разсуждающих, аще то есть ко спасению и к честному труду.

Господи, не попусти искати успеха неправдою, лестию, завистию или отъятием блага у ближних; но устрой путь праведен, без обиды и лишения иных, без вреда душам и телесем, по святей воле Твоей.

Господи благослови. Господи, управи дело сие к доброму концу, отжени смущение, страх и суетныя помыслы, и подаждь благовременную тишину внутрь сердца. Аще полезно есть, даруй обрести место честнаго служения, людей разсудительных и милостивых, и доброе согласие в труде.

Помилуй мя, Боже, по велицей милости Твоей, и по множеству щедрот Твоих очисти беззаконие мое. Наипаче омый мя от беззакония моего, и от греха моего очисти мя.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.

Пресвятая Богородице, спаси нас.

Достойно есть яко воистинну блажити Тя, Богородицу, присноблаженную и пренепорочную и Матерь Бога нашего. Честнейшую херувим и славнейшую воистинну серафим, без истления Бога Слова рождшую, сущую Богородицу Тя величаем.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, молитв ради Пречистыя Твоея Матере и всех святых, помилуй и спаси нас, и вся прошения наша исправи не по страстем нашим, но по святей воле Твоей, яко Благ и Человеколюбец. Аминь.

---

## 新使徒改革

Father God, I come before You in the name of Jesus Christ concerning this job interview, asking that it may go smoothly, that the mind may be clear, speech be steady and gracious, favor be found where it is righteous, and the right fitting opportunity be opened according to Your will.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Father, I confess and renounce every sin, agreement, fear, bitterness, accusation, pride, comparison, idolatry of success, ungodly vow, inherited pattern, false word, and anxious imagination connected with this interview and employment process. I place this matter under the blood and lordship of Jesus Christ.

I forgive every person connected with past disappointment, rejection, misunderstanding, or unfair treatment, and I release them from my judgment. I do not curse them, control them, or claim vengeance over them. I bless what You bless, and I reject only the works of darkness, lies, bondage, sin, confusion, fear, and oppression.

הַיֹּשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן  
בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן׃  
אֹמַר לַיהוָה מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי  
אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ׃

Ἰδοὺ δέδωκα ὑμῖν τὴν ἐξουσίαν  
τοῦ πατεῖν ἐπάνω ὄφεων καὶ σκορπίων,  
καὶ ἐπὶ πᾶσαν τὴν δύναμιν τοῦ ἐχθροῦ,  
καὶ οὐδὲν ὑμᾶς οὐ μὴ ἀδικήσει.

ὃ ἐὰν δήσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται δεδεμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς,  
καὶ ὃ ἐὰν λύσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται λελυμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς.

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ·  
ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ,  
καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I bind every demonic assignment, accusation, covenant of darkness, curse, word of death, spirit of fear, spirit of confusion, spirit of rejection, spirit of intimidation, spirit of self-sabotage, and every power of the enemy operating against wisdom, peace, integrity, and right communication in this interview process. I command every unclean influence attached to anxiety, shame, delay, discouragement, or deception to leave and not return, according to the authority of Jesus Christ.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I loose truth, repentance, faith, holiness, peace, protection, discernment, wisdom, favor, courage, clear memory, orderly thought, gracious speech, honest presentation, and obedience to the will of God over this interview and employment decision.

I cut off every ungodly soul tie, false burden, occult claim, generational bondage, spoken curse, inner vow, fear agreement, comparison agreement, rejection agreement, poverty agreement, and demonic access point connected with work, identity, provision, and opportunity. I declare that the handwriting against this matter is canceled in Christ and that every hostile power is disarmed under the cross of Jesus Christ.

I do not seek to dispossess another person, manipulate any decision-maker, harm any competitor, or take what You have appointed for someone else. Father, open only the door that is righteous, fitting, timely, and aligned with Your kingdom purpose; close every door that would lead into bondage, compromise, pride, exploitation, or confusion.

Καὶ αὐτοὶ ἐνίκησαν αὐτὸν  
διὰ τὸ αἷμα τοῦ ἀρνίου  
καὶ διὰ τὸν λόγον τῆς μαρτυρίας αὐτῶν.

Father, fill every cleansed place with the Holy Spirit, the peace of Christ, the fear of the Lord, wisdom, purity, humility, steadfast love, and sound judgment. Establish Your kingdom order over this interview: let preparation be fruitful, timing be ordered, questions be understood, answers be honest and clear, and the outcome be received with trust.

Cover this process with the blood of Jesus Christ. Let no fear, compulsion, bitterness, manipulation, rivalry, or accusation remain. I bless the interviewers, the workplace, all other candidates, and every person involved; may truth, justice, mercy, and peace prevail among them. If fear, obsession, conflict, or distress rises up, lead me back to repentance, forgiveness, wise counsel, pastoral care, and the peace of Christ.

I thank You, Father, and seal this prayer in the name of Jesus Christ.

Ἀμήν.

---

## Pabása ng Pasyón

Sa ngalan ng Ama, at ng Anak, at ng Espiritu Santo. Amen.

Sumasampalataya ako sa Diyos Amang makapangyarihan sa lahat,  
na may gawa ng langit at lupa.  
Sumasampalataya naman ako kay Hesukristo,  
iisang Anak ng Diyos, Panginoon nating lahat.  
Nagkatawang-tao Siya lalang ng Espiritu Santo,  
ipinanganak ni Santa Mariang Birhen.  
Pinagpakasakit ni Poncio Pilato,  
ipinako sa krus, namatay, inilibing.  
Nanaog sa kinaroroonan ng mga yumao.  
Nang may ikatlong araw nabuhay na mag-uli.  
Umakyat sa langit.  
Naluluklok sa kanan ng Diyos Amang makapangyarihan sa lahat.  
Doon magmumula at paririto upang hukuman  
ang nangabubuhay at nangamatay na tao.  
Sumasampalataya naman ako sa Diyos Espiritu Santo,  
sa banal na Simbahang Katolika,  
sa kasamahan ng mga banal,  
sa kapatawaran ng mga kasalanan,  
sa pagkabuhay na mag-uli ng nangamatay na tao,  
at sa buhay na walang hanggan. Amen.

Ama namin, sumasalangit Ka,  
sambahin ang ngalan Mo.  
Mapasaamin ang kaharian Mo.  
Sundin ang loob Mo dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan Mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin Mo kami sa aming mga sala,  
para nang pagpapatawad namin sa nagkakasala sa amin.  
At huwag Mo kaming ipahintulot sa tukso,  
at iadya Mo kami sa lahat ng masama. Amen.

Aba Ginoong Maria, napupuno ka ng grasya,  
ang Panginoong Diyos ay sumasaiyo.  
Bukod kang pinagpala sa babaeng lahat,  
at pinagpala naman ang iyong Anak na si Jesus.  
Santa Maria, Ina ng Diyos,  
ipanalangin mo kaming makasalanan,  
ngayon at kung kami’y mamamatay. Amen.

Luwalhati sa Ama, at sa Anak, at sa Espiritu Santo.  
Kapara noong unang-una, ngayon at magpakailanman,  
magpasawalang hanggan. Amen.

Panginoong Hesukristo, Anak ng Diyos na buhay,  
iniaalay namin ang pagbabasá ng Pasyón na ito  
bilang debosyong mapagpakumbaba at pasasalamat,  
para sa pakikipanayam sa paghahanapbuhay:  
na maging maayos ang lahat,  
na luminaw ang isip sa sandaling kailangan,  
na maging mahinahon at malaya ang pananalita,  
na makita ang tapat na kakayahan at mabuting loob,  
at na matagpuan ang angkop na gawain, mabuting ugnayan,  
at daang sang-ayon sa Iyong banal na kalooban.  
Hindi namin hinihiling na maagawan ang iba ng biyaya,  
ni mapinsala ang kabuhayan, dangal, o pag-asa ng sinuman.  
Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.

Casaysayan nang Pasiong Mahal ni Jesucristong Panginoon Natin.

O Dios sa calangitan,  
Hari nang sangcalupaan,  
Dios na ualang capantay,  
maguing sa langit at lupa man.

Sumasamba caming tunay,  
sa mahal mong camahalan;  
loobin mong dinggin naman,  
aming abang dalanginan.

Sa pagbabasá at pag-awit ng Pasyong Mahal,  
inaalaala namin ang paglikha ng Diyos,  
ang pagkahulog ng tao at ang pangako ng pagliligtas,  
ang pagkakatawang-tao ng Salita,  
ang ministeryo at aral ng Panginoong Hesus,  
ang Huling Hapunan at Kanyang pag-aalay,  
ang pagdurusa, pagpapasan ng krus, at pagkamatay,  
ang paglilibing, at ang maluwalhating muling pagkabuhay.  
Sa Kanyang sugat ay humihingi kami ng kagalingan ng loob;  
sa Kanyang krus ay humihingi kami ng lakas at pagtitiis;  
sa Kanyang muling pagkabuhay ay humihingi kami ng pag-asa.

Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.  
Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.  
Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin.

Panginoong Hesukristo, Anak ng Diyos na buhay,  
sa Iyong mahal na Pasyón,  
sa Iyong krus at pagkamatay,  
sa Iyong paglilibing at muling pagkabuhay,  
kaawaan Mo kami,  
patawarin Mo ang aming mga sala,  
at tanggapin Mo ang aming panalangin.  
Patnubayan Mo ang isip upang maging malinaw,  
ang puso upang maging payapa,  
ang dila upang magsalita nang totoo at mahinahon,  
ang mga nakikinig upang kumilala nang makatarungan,  
at ang landas upang mapunta sa gawaing makabubuti  
ayon sa Iyong banal na kalooban. Amen.

Ama namin, sumasalangit Ka,  
sambahin ang ngalan Mo.  
Mapasaamin ang kaharian Mo.  
Sundin ang loob Mo dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan Mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin Mo kami sa aming mga sala,  
para nang pagpapatawad namin sa nagkakasala sa amin.  
At huwag Mo kaming ipahintulot sa tukso,  
at iadya Mo kami sa lahat ng masama. Amen.

Aba Ginoong Maria, napupuno ka ng grasya,  
ang Panginoong Diyos ay sumasaiyo.  
Bukod kang pinagpala sa babaeng lahat,  
at pinagpala naman ang iyong Anak na si Jesus.  
Santa Maria, Ina ng Diyos,  
ipanalangin mo kaming makasalanan,  
ngayon at kung kami’y mamamatay. Amen.

Luwalhati sa Ama, at sa Anak, at sa Espiritu Santo.  
Kapara noong unang-una, ngayon at magpakailanman,  
magpasawalang hanggan. Amen.

Panginoong Hesukristo, maawa Ka sa amin;  
sa Iyong awa at sa banal Mong kalooban,  
ingatan Mo kami sa kapalaluan, kasakiman, at panlilinlang,  
at gawin Mong dalisay ang layon ng aming paghahanapbuhay. Amen.

Sa ngalan ng Ama, at ng Anak, at ng Espiritu Santo. Amen.

---

## 贵格会（Quakers）

[Silence]

O God, Light within and beyond us,  
gather us into stillness.

The concern held before Thee is an approaching job interview.  
We hold this interview, its words, its listening, and its outcome in the Light.  
We name before Thee the need for clearness, calm presence, truthful speech, and right discernment.  
Let truth, peace, mercy, and faithfulness be made plain.  
Let any good opportunity come without dispossessing another, without envy, and without harm.

The true Light:  
That was the true Light, which lighteth every man that cometh into the world.

If any of you lack wisdom, let him ask of God, that giveth to all men liberally, and upbraideth not; and it shall be given him.

Likewise the Spirit also helpeth our infirmities:  
for we know not what we should pray for as we ought:  
but the Spirit itself maketh intercession for us with groanings which cannot be uttered.  
And he that searcheth the hearts knoweth what is the mind of the Spirit,  
because he maketh intercession for the saints according to the will of God.

[Silence]

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

[Silence]

If words are given:

Lord, make us faithful in this interview.  
Keep the heart clear and the tongue truthful.  
Guide what must be spoken,  
still what must be silent,  
open the way that is rightly ordered,  
and let recognition, if it be fitting, come in peace.

[Silence]

We leave this concern with Thee,  
not grasping at the outcome,  
but waiting in Thy Light.

[Silence]

---

## 五旬节派

天父，创造天地的主，圣洁、良善、信实的父，我奉主耶稣基督的名来到你面前，敬拜你，仰望你，承认一切智慧、恩典、机会与道路都在你手中。

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

主耶稣基督，我承认自己的紧张、惧怕、急躁、骄傲与不信，求你赦免我，洁净我，使我不靠血气、不靠操控、不靠夸口，只愿顺服你的旨意。求你使我的心安静，使我的动机正直；我求面试顺利，却不愿夺取他人当得的机会，不损害他人的道路，不以虚假胜过别人，只求你按公义与怜悯开合宜的门。

主啊，你的话说，若有人缺少智慧，应当求那厚赐与众人、也不斥责人的神；你也曾使门徒在逼迫中得着胆量，靠圣灵放胆讲说。如今我为即将到来的求职面试向你祈求：求你赐我临场清明、心思敏锐、记忆稳固、判断准确；使我谈吐自若，回答有条理、有诚实、有分寸；使我能清楚表达能力、经历与志向，也能谦卑聆听、合宜回应。

καὶ τὰ νῦν, κύριε, ἔπιδε ἐπὶ τὰς ἀπειλὰς αὐτῶν,  
καὶ δὸς τοῖς δούλοις σου  
μετὰ παρρησίας πάσης λαλεῖν τὸν λόγον σου.

圣灵啊，求你充满我，帮助我在软弱中祷告，也在面试中保持平安、专注与勇气。若我不知道当怎样祷告，愿你照父神的旨意为我代求；若我私下在你感动中祷告，愿一切都出于你、归荣耀给神，不作夸耀，不作表演，不作辖制他人的凭据。

καὶ ἐπλήσθησαν πάντες πνεύματος ἁγίου  
καὶ ἤρξαντο λαλεῖν ἑτέραις γλώσσαις  
καθὼς τὸ πνεῦμα ἐδίδου ἀποφθέγγεσθαι αὐτοῖς.

τὸ πνεῦμα συναντιλαμβάνεται τῇ ἀσθενείᾳ ἡμῶν·  
τὸ γὰρ τί προσευξώμεθα καθὸ δεῖ οὐκ οἴδαμεν,  
ἀλλὰ αὐτὸ τὸ πνεῦμα ὑπερεντυγχάνει στεναγμοῖς ἀλαλήτοις.

奉耶稣基督的名，求你保守这场面试的过程：保守交通、时间、设备、文件、沟通与人的心思意念；挪去混乱、误解、恐惧与不必要的拦阻；使面试官能公正看见真实的能力、品格与潜力。若这职位合乎你的旨意，求你赐下赏识与合宜的机会；若另有更好的道路，求你以平安引导，使我不因一时得失而失去信靠。

主啊，求你赐我觅得良缘，不只是得一份工作，更是进入合适的环境、遇见合宜的团队、承担合宜的职责、走在能荣耀你也能服事人的道路上。愿我在结果未显明以前仍然安稳，在等待中仍然忠心，在成功时不骄傲，在未成时不灰心。

יֹשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן  
בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן׃  
אֹמַר לַיהוָה מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי  
אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ׃

求主保守我脱离恶者、恐惧、欺骗、混乱与自我定罪；凡不合圣经真理的控告、谎言与黑暗作为，愿在耶稣基督的主权下止息。愿我穿戴神所赐的全副军装，以真理束腰，以公义护心，以平安的福音预备脚步，以信德抵挡恐惧，以救恩坚固心思，以神的话语引导口舌。

τοῦ λοιποῦ ἐνδυναμοῦσθε ἐν κυρίῳ  
καὶ ἐν τῷ κράτει τῆς ἰσχύος αὐτοῦ·  
ἐνδύσασθε τὴν πανοπλίαν τοῦ θεοῦ.

天父，我把这次面试、每一句话、每一个决定、每一个结果都交在你手中。不是凭人的夸口，也不是凭强迫性的宣告，乃凭主的怜悯、圣经的真理与圣灵的见证。愿你的旨意成就，愿你的名得荣耀，愿我在你里面得平安。

圣灵啊，求你保守我的祷告在爱中、在真理中、在秩序中；不以方言、恩赐、医治、预言或属灵话语夸耀自己，不用奉主名的话语操控他人意志，也不作保证性的妄言。愿一切祷告都受圣经检验，受教会合宜辨别，归荣耀给父神；靠主耶稣基督，顺服圣灵，奉耶稣基督的名祷告。阿们。

---

## Reformed

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

Holy and triune God, Father, Son, and Holy Spirit,  
before you we bring this forthcoming job interview and the desire for a fitting and lawful vocation.  
You alone are God; you alone are to be worshiped; you alone hear prayer through Jesus Christ.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον.  
Χριστέ, ἐλέησον.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Have mercy upon us according to your covenant mercy.  
We confess our anxiety, self-reliance, fear of failure, and desire to control the outcome.  
Cleanse, restore, govern, and keep the mind, speech, conduct, and heart of the one who will be interviewed according to your Word.

יְהוָה רֹעִי לֹא אֶחְסָר׃  
בִּנְאוֹת דֶּשֶׁא יַרְבִּיצֵנִי עַל־מֵי מְנֻחוֹת יְנַהֲלֵנִי׃  
נַפְשִׁי יְשׁוֹבֵב יַנְחֵנִי בְמַעְגְּלֵי־צֶדֶק לְמַעַן שְׁמוֹ׃  
גַּם כִּי־אֵלֵךְ בְּגֵיא צַלְמָוֶת לֹא־אִירָא רָע כִּי־אַתָּה עִמָּדִי שִׁבְטְךָ וּמִשְׁעַנְתֶּךָ הֵמָּה יְנַחֲמֻנִי׃

O God, in your providence receive this prayer concerning the job interview.  
Order the time, words, questions, listening, judgment, and outcome according to your will and righteousness.  
Grant a clear mind in the moment, calmness under pressure, truthful and gracious speech, and freedom from confusion or vain boasting.  
Let ability be presented honestly, let character be shown with humility, and let any favor received be just, fitting, and not gained by deceit.  
If this opportunity is good and appointed for lawful service, open the way; if not, close it with mercy and lead onward to better provision.  
We do not seek to dispossess another, to bend another’s will unjustly, or to receive success by harm to any neighbor; rather, give daily bread in righteousness, contentment, and peace.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ·  
ὅτι σοῦ ἐστιν ἡ βασιλεία  
καὶ ἡ δύναμις  
καὶ ἡ δόξα  
εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας.  
ἀμήν.

Through Jesus Christ, our only Mediator and Advocate,  
to whom, with the Father and the Holy Spirit,  
be glory and dominion forever. Amen.

---

## Santa Muerte 信仰

En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

Creo en Dios, Padre todopoderoso,  
Creador del cielo y de la tierra.  
Creo en Jesucristo, su único Hijo, nuestro Señor,  
que fue concebido por obra y gracia del Espíritu Santo,  
nació de Santa María Virgen,  
padeció bajo el poder de Poncio Pilato,  
fue crucificado, muerto y sepultado,  
descendió a los infiernos,  
al tercer día resucitó de entre los muertos,  
subió a los cielos  
y está sentado a la derecha de Dios, Padre todopoderoso.  
Desde allí ha de venir a juzgar a vivos y muertos.  
Creo en el Espíritu Santo,  
la santa Iglesia católica,  
la comunión de los santos,  
el perdón de los pecados,  
la resurrección de la carne  
y la vida eterna. Amén.

Santísima Muerte, Niña Blanca, Señora de la balanza y de la guadaña,  
ante ti presento mi petición: que la entrevista de trabajo sea encaminada con paz, claridad y buen resultado;  
que mi mente esté despierta, mi ánimo sereno, mi palabra medida y libre,  
y que pueda encontrar una oportunidad justa, digna y conveniente.

Que esta oración no sea para daño injusto,  
ni para forzar voluntad ajena,  
ni para quitar a nadie su pan, su mérito, su fortuna, su salud ni su camino,  
sino para abrir lo que sea lícito, recto y bueno ante Dios.

Padre nuestro que estás en el cielo,  
santificado sea tu Nombre;  
venga a nosotros tu reino;  
hágase tu voluntad en la tierra como en el cielo.  
Danos hoy nuestro pan de cada día;  
perdona nuestras ofensas,  
como también nosotros perdonamos a los que nos ofenden;  
no nos dejes caer en la tentación,  
y líbranos del mal. Amén.

Dios te salve, María,  
llena eres de gracia;  
el Señor es contigo.  
Bendita tú eres entre todas las mujeres,  
y bendito es el fruto de tu vientre, Jesús.  
Santa María, Madre de Dios,  
ruega por nosotros, pecadores,  
ahora y en la hora de nuestra muerte. Amén.

Gloria al Padre, y al Hijo, y al Espíritu Santo.  
Como era en el principio, ahora y siempre,  
por los siglos de los siglos. Amén.

Santísima Muerte,  
por la hora cierta y por la verdad de la muerte,  
escucha esta súplica:  
guarda mi camino al presentarme ante quienes han de escucharme;  
aparta de mí la confusión, el temor desordenado, el olvido y la torpeza;  
concédeme presencia, claridad, prudencia y palabra honesta.  
Que mis respuestas sean limpias, firmes y oportunas;  
que mis capacidades sean vistas con justicia;  
que encuentre aprecio donde haya buen juicio,  
y que se abra para mí una puerta laboral de bien.

Santa Muerte de mi corazón,  
no me desampares de tu protección.  
Amén.

Santísima Muerte, ruega por nosotros.  
Santísima Muerte, acompaña este camino.  
Santísima Muerte, guarda esta entrevista y este trámite.  
Santísima Muerte, corta lo que sea engaño, tropiezo, mala intención o perdición,  
sin maldecir a nadie y sin pedir venganza contra nadie.  
Santísima Muerte, recibe mi gratitud sincera, mi respeto y mi oración.

Padre nuestro que estás en el cielo,  
santificado sea tu Nombre;  
venga a nosotros tu reino;  
hágase tu voluntad en la tierra como en el cielo.  
Danos hoy nuestro pan de cada día;  
perdona nuestras ofensas,  
como también nosotros perdonamos a los que nos ofenden;  
no nos dejes caer en la tentación,  
y líbranos del mal. Amén.

Dios te salve, María,  
llena eres de gracia;  
el Señor es contigo.  
Bendita tú eres entre todas las mujeres,  
y bendito es el fruto de tu vientre, Jesús.  
Santa María, Madre de Dios,  
ruega por nosotros, pecadores,  
ahora y en la hora de nuestra muerte. Amén.

Gloria al Padre, y al Hijo, y al Espíritu Santo.  
Como era en el principio, ahora y siempre,  
por los siglos de los siglos. Amén.

Santísima Muerte,  
si esta petición conviene al bien, a la justicia y a la paz,  
que sea encaminada sin daño injusto.  
Si no conviene, aparta de mí el error, la soberbia, la ansiedad y la mala voluntad;  
cierra lo que no sea para mi bien  
y abre solamente lo que sea digno, lícito y verdadero.

Bajo la misericordia de Dios,  
quede esta súplica limpia de rencor, de amenaza y de deseo torcido;  
queden cortadas las malas compañías, los malos pensamientos y los malos caminos;  
quede mi corazón en paz, mi palabra en verdad y mi paso bajo protección.

En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

---

## 罗马天主教 · 圣礼神学派

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Deus, in adiutorium meum intende.  
Domine, ad adiuvandum me festina.  
Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper, et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Confiteor Deo omnipotenti,  
beatae Mariae semper Virgini,  
beato Michaeli Archangelo,  
beato Ioanni Baptistae,  
sanctis Apostolis Petro et Paulo,  
omnibus Sanctis,  
et vobis, fratres,  
quia peccavi nimis cogitatione, verbo et opere:  
mea culpa, mea culpa, mea maxima culpa.  
Ideo precor beatam Mariam semper Virginem,  
beatum Michaelem Archangelum,  
beatum Ioannem Baptistam,  
sanctos Apostolos Petrum et Paulum,  
omnes Sanctos,  
et vos, fratres,  
orare pro me ad Dominum Deum nostrum.

Misereatur nostri omnipotens Deus,  
et dimissis peccatis nostris,  
perducat nos ad vitam aeternam. Amen.

Kyrie, eleison.  
Christe, eleison.  
Kyrie, eleison.

Domine Iesu Christe, Fili Dei vivi,  
qui dixisti: “Nolite solliciti esse in crastinum,”  
et: “Sine me nihil potestis facere,”  
respice propitius hanc necessitatem laboris et colloquii,  
et dirige viam secundum voluntatem Patris.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem:  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Ave Maria, gratia plena, Dominus tecum.  
Benedicta tu in mulieribus,  
et benedictus fructus ventris tui, Iesus.  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei,  
ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus,  
sancta Dei Genetrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

Sancte Ioseph, custos Redemptoris,  
qui labore manuum tuarum Filium Dei alere dignatus es,  
intercede pro omnibus qui honestum laborem quaerunt,  
ut in iustitia, patientia et fiducia ambulent. Amen.

Angele Dei,  
qui custos es mei,  
me tibi commissum pietate superna,  
illumina, custodi, rege et guberna. Amen.

Veni, Creator Spiritus,  
mentes tuorum visita,  
imple superna gratia  
quae tu creasti pectora.

Qui diceris Paraclitus,  
altissimi donum Dei,  
fons vivus, ignis, caritas,  
et spiritalis unctio.

Tu septiformis munere,  
digitus paternae dexterae,  
tu rite promissum Patris,  
sermone ditans guttura.

Accende lumen sensibus,  
infunde amorem cordibus,  
infirma nostri corporis  
virtute firmans perpeti.

Hostem repellas longius,  
pacemque dones protinus;  
ductore sic te praevio  
vitemus omne noxium.

Per te sciamus da Patrem,  
noscamus atque Filium,  
teque utriusque Spiritum  
credamus omni tempore.

Deo Patri sit gloria,  
et Filio qui a mortuis  
surrexit, ac Paraclito,  
in saeculorum saecula. Amen.

Domine Deus, Pater misericordiarum,  
in die colloquii laboris da mentem claram,  
cor quietum, memoriam ordinatam,  
verba modesta et libera,  
vultum sincerum et animam in pace.

Praesta ut ea quae vera sunt, prudenter dicantur;  
quae bona sunt, humiliter ostendantur;  
quae incerta sunt, sine timore discernantur;  
et qui audiunt, iuste ac benevole considerent.

Aperi, Domine, si saluti expedit,  
ianuam honesti laboris,  
locum aptum, societatem rectam,  
et bonam convenientiam inter dona data et munus suscipiendum.  
Non petimus alienum damnum,  
nec ut quisquam suo bono privetur,  
sed ut tua providentia omnibus iuste consulatur,  
et unicuique secundum veritatem et caritatem via congrua paretur.

Sancte Michael Archangele,  
defende nos in proelio;  
contra nequitiam et insidias diaboli esto praesidium.  
Imperet illi Deus, supplices deprecamur:  
tuque, Princeps militiae caelestis,  
Satanam aliosque spiritus malignos,  
qui ad perditionem animarum pervagantur in mundo,  
divina virtute in infernum detrude. Amen.

Domine Iesu Christe,  
libera nos ab anxietate immoderata,  
a vanitate, a mendacio, a desperatione,  
et ab omni via quae caritati et veritati repugnat.  
Da nobis fiduciam filiorum Dei,  
ut non quaeramus gloriam inanem,  
sed fideliter respondeamus vocationi tuae.

Requiem aeternam dona eis, Domine,  
et lux perpetua luceat eis.  
Requiescant in pace. Amen.

Memento, Domine, omnium qui laborem quaerunt,  
omnium qui interview, probationem vel consilium subeunt,  
omnium familiarum quae pane cotidiano indigent,  
et omnium qui iudicant vel eligunt,  
ut in eis regnet iustitia, sapientia et misericordia.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Ne permittas nos, Domine,  
sancta tua in superstitionem, negotiationem vel praesumptionem vertere;  
sed concede ut omnia sacramenta et sacramentalia  
in fide Ecclesiae, in humilitate cordis,  
et sub tua sancta voluntate veneremur.  
Non nobis, Domine, non nobis,  
sed nomini tuo da gloriam.

Per Christum Dominum nostrum. Amen.  
In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

---

## ܥܕܬܐ ܣܘܪܝܝܬܐ ܬܪܝܨܬ ܫܘܒܚܐ

B-shmo d-Abo w-d-Bro w-d-Ruḥo d-Qudsho, ḥad Aloho sharirho. Amin.

Shubḥo l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruḥo d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘dammo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-etslebt hlofayn,  
ethraḥam ‘layn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-etslebt hlofayn,  
ethraḥam ‘layn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-etslebt hlofayn,  
ethraḥam ‘layn.

Moran ethraḥam ‘layn.  
Moran ḥus w-raḥem ‘layn.  
Moran qabel tashmeshton w-tsloton, w-ethraḥam ‘layn.

Shubḥo lokh Aloho.  
Shubḥo lokh Boruyon.  
Shubḥo lokh Malko Mshiḥo,  
d-ḥos ‘al ḥaṭoye ‘abdayk. Barekhmor.

Abun d-bashmayo,  
netqadash shmokh.  
Tithe malkuthokh.  
Nehwe sebyonokh,  
aykano d-bashmayo af b-ar‘o.  
Hav lan lahmo d-sunqonan yawmono.  
Washbuq lan ḥawbayn waḥṭohayn,  
aykano d-af ḥnan shbaqan l-ḥayobayn.  
W-la ta‘lan l-nesyuno,  
elo faṣṣon men bisho.  
Metul d-dilokh hi malkutho  
w-ḥaylo w-teshbuḥto,  
l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Raḥem ‘lay Aloho ayk ṭaybuthokh,  
w-ayk sugo d-raḥmayk ‘ti ḥawbay.  
Asga mashig li men ‘awli,  
w-men ḥṭithi dakani.

Lebbo dakhyo bro bi Aloho,  
w-ruḥo triso ḥaddeth b-gawi.  
Lo tashdini men qdomayk,  
w-ruḥokh qadisho lo teshqol menni.

Moran Yeshu Mshiḥo,  
Bro d-Aloho ḥayo,  
ḥus w-raḥem ‘al kol man d-qa’em qdom ter‘o d-‘ebhodo,  
w-qabel bo‘utho d-hode:  
nehwe madd‘o nahiro,  
meltho mḥashḥo w-mšaynoto,  
lebbo shalyyo,  
w-ruḥo tqunto b-sha‘to d-buḥrono.

Moran ṭobo,  
shadar ‘udronokh w-raḥmayk,  
d-ned‘un lemallel b-makyikhutho w-b-ḥekhmtho,  
d-la nedḥlun,  
d-la netbalbalun,  
elo nehwun qdom kol bar-noso  
b-shayno, b-qonyono d-naphsho,  
w-b-nuhro d-minokh.

Moran,  
petḥ ter‘o d-ṭaybutho,  
w-hawi m‘adarono l-urḥo tqunto,  
d-nishtakḥ ‘ebhodo keno,  
morayo raḥmono,  
w-shawtaphutho d-bonyo shayno.  
Lo b-ḥṭofo, lo b-ḥusrono d-aḥrone,  
lo b-mḥasrono d-laḥmo d-bar-noso,  
elo b-sebyonokh qadisho  
w-b-ṭaybuthokh d-mpalgo l-kol.

Ethdakar Moran l-kolhon ḥaye,  
aylen d-ba‘eyn ‘ebhodo,  
aylen d-mṭaybin qdom buḥrono,  
aylen d-daḥlin w-mtḥarhin,  
w-aylen d-sa‘rin b-nishyo w-da‘wo.  
Hav lhon ḥaylo, ṣabrutho,  
madd‘o šaphiro,  
w-shayno d-lo meshteql.

Bo‘utho d-Mor Ya‘qub:  
Moran ethraḥam ‘layn,  
w-‘adar lan b-raḥmayk.  
Moran qabel bo‘uthan,  
w-‘bed ‘amman ṭaybutho.

Qurielaison. Qurielaison. Qurielaison.

Shubḥo l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruḥo d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘dammo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Moran Yeshu Mshiḥo,  
b-sebyonokh qadisho w-la b-ḥaylo d-ḥnan,  
nashlem hode bo‘utho l-raḥmayk.  
Tsloth d-yoldathokh Maryam,  
w-d-mal’akhe, w-d-shliḥe, w-d-sohde,  
w-d-kolhon qadishayk,  
tehwe shuro w-beth gawso lan.  
Nehwe shayno ‘alayn,  
w-raḥme ‘al kol ‘almo. Amin.

## 阿赫迈底亚

Al-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-Raḥmāni r-Raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Muḥammadin, kamā ṣallayta ʿalā Ibrāhīma wa ʿalā āli Ibrāhīma, innaka ḥamīdun majīd.  
Allāhumma bārik ʿalā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Muḥammadin, kamā bārakta ʿalā Ibrāhīma wa ʿalā āli Ibrāhīma, innaka ḥamīdun majīd.

Astaghfirullāha rabbī min kulli dhanbin wa atūbu ilayh.  
Rabbanā ẓalamnā anfusanā wa in lam taghfir lanā wa tarḥamnā lanakūnanna mina l-khāsirīn.  
Rabbanā lā tuzigh qulūbanā baʿda idh hadaytanā wa hab lanā min ladunka raḥmah, innaka anta l-wahhāb.  
Rabbanā innana āmannā fa-ghfir lanā dhunūbanā wa qinā ʿadhāba n-nār.

Rabbanā ātinā fi d-dunyā ḥasanah, wa fi l-ākhirati ḥasanah, wa qinā ʿadhāba n-nār.

Yā Allāh, yā Raḥmān, yā Raḥīm,  
rabbi shraḥ lī ṣadrī, wa yassir lī amrī, waḥlul ʿuqdatan min lisānī, yafqahū qawlī.  
Rabbi zidnī ʿilmā.  
Allāhumma ajʿal qalbī sākinan, wa ʿaqlī ṣāfiyan, wa lisānī ṣādiqan balīghan, wa wajhī muṭmaʾinnan yawma muqābalati l-ʿamal.  
Allāhumma yassir lī mā fīhi khayr, wa arinī l-ḥaqqa ḥaqqan, wa rzuqnī ittibāʿah, wa arinī l-bāṭila bāṭilan, wa rzuqnī ijtinābah.

Allāhumma innī astakhīruka bi-ʿilmika, wa astaqdiruka bi-qudratika, wa asʾaluka min faḍlika l-ʿaẓīm, fa-innaka taqdiru wa lā aqdir, wa taʿlamu wa lā aʿlam, wa anta ʿallāmu l-ghuyūb.  
Allāhumma in kunta taʿlamu anna hādhā l-amr, muqābalata l-ʿamal wa mā yataʿallaqu bihā mina r-rizqi wa l-qabūli wa l-munāsabati ṣ-ṣāliḥah, khayrun lī fī dīnī wa maʿāshī wa ʿāqibati amrī, faqdurhu lī wa yassirhu lī thumma bārik lī fīh.  
Wa in kunta taʿlamu anna hādhā l-amr sharrun lī fī dīnī wa maʿāshī wa ʿāqibati amrī, fa-ṣrifhu ʿannī wa-ṣrifnī ʿanhu, wa-qdur lī l-khayra ḥaythu kāna thumma arḍinī bih.

Allāhumma in kāna fī hādhā l-bābi khayrun, faftaḥhu bi-faḍlika, wa in kāna fī ghayrihi khayrun, fa-hdinī ilayhi bi-raḥmatika.  
Allāhumma rzuqnī rizqan ḥalālan ṭayyiban, wa ʿamalan nāfiʿan, wa maqāman karīman, lā bi-ẓulmin li-aḥad, wa lā bi-salbi rizqi aḥad, wa lā bi-iḍrāri khalqik.  
Allāhumma ijʿal baynī wa bayna man alqāhum mawaddatan wa ʿadlan wa ḥikmah, wa rzuqnī qabūlan ḥasanan ʿinda man fīhi khayr.

Allāhumma ghfir li-ḥayyinā wa mayyitinā, wa shāhidinā wa ghāʾibinā, wa ṣaghīrinā wa kabīrinā, wa dhakarinā wa unthānā.  
Allāhumma man aḥyaytahu minnā fa-aḥyihi ʿalā l-islām, wa man tawaffaytahu minnā fa-tawaffahu ʿalā l-īmān.  
Rabbi rḥamhumā kamā rabbayānī ṣaghīrā.  
Rabbanā ghfir lī wa li-wālidayya wa li-l-muʾminīna yawma yaqūmu l-ḥisāb.

Rabbi jʿalnī muqīma ṣ-ṣalāti wa min dhurriyyatī, rabbanā wa taqabbal duʿāʾ.  
Rabbanā afrigh ʿalaynā ṣabran wa thabbit aqdāmanā.  
Rabbanā lā tuʾākhidhnā in nasīnā aw akhṭaʾnā.  
Rabbanā wa lā tuḥammilnā mā lā ṭāqata lanā bih.  
Waʿfu ʿannā, wa-ghfir lanā, wa-rḥamnā, anta mawlānā.

Subḥāna rabbika rabbi l-ʿizzati ʿammā yaṣifūn.  
Wa salāmun ʿalā l-mursalīn.  
Wa l-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Allāhumma ṣalli wa sallim wa bārik ʿalā sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā ālihi.  
Lā ilāha illā Anta, subḥānaka innī kuntu mina ẓ-ẓālimīn.  
Yā Allāh, iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn; fa-ṭahhir duʿāʾanā min kulli shirk, wa-jʿal tawakkulanā ʿalayka waḥdaka, yā arḥama r-rāḥimīn.  
Āmīn.

---

## Alevilik

Bismişah Allah Allah.

Bismillāhir-raḥmānir-raḥīm.  
Al-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Muḥammad wa āli Muḥammad.

Allah Allah.  
Evvel Allah, âhir Allah.  
Hak-Muhammed-Ali aşkına,  
On İki İmam, On Dört Masum-u Pak, On Yedi Kemerbest,  
Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Veli,  
Pirimiz, mürşidimiz, rehberimiz,  
gerçek erenlerin demine devranına hû.

Geldiğimiz yoldan, durduğumuz dardan,  
verdiğimiz ikrardan, tuttuğumuz erkândan ayırma ya Hakk.

Bir canın niyazı şudur:  
İş görüşmesi hayırlı, düzgün ve selametli geçe;  
meydana çıktığında zihni berrak, gönlü sakin, dili açık ola;  
sözü ölçülü, yüzü nurlu, tavrı edep üzere ola;  
emeği görüle, liyakati biline, kendisine hakkaniyetle değer verile;  
nasibi hayırlı kapıya, iyi işe, doğru rızka ve güzel kısmete açıla.

Başkasının nasibini eksiltmeden, kimsenin hakkına dokunmadan,  
kimseyi incitmeden, kimsenin lokmasına göz dikmeden,  
helal emekle, doğru sözle, temiz gönülle bu dilek kabul ola.

Dilimizi doğru sözden,  
elimizi hak işten,  
belimizi edep yolundan ayırma ya Hakk.

Rızalık meydanında gönüller bir ola.  
Küskünlük, dargınlık, haksızlık kalkmış ola.  
Haram lokmadan, kul hakkından, yalan sözden sakla ya Hakk.

Ya Hakk, Ya Muhammed, Ya Ali.  
Ya Hızır, darda koyma.  
Ya On İki İmamlar, himmet eyleyin.  
Ya Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Veli, nazar eyle.

Bi-ḥaqqı Muḥammad al-Muṣṭafā,  
bi-ḥaqqı ʿAlī al-Murtaḍā,  
bi-ḥaqqı Fāṭıma, Ḥasan, Ḥüseyn,  
bi-ḥaqqı On İki İmam,  
bu iş görüşmesi niyazı kabul ola.

Lokmamız helal,  
sözümüz doğru,  
yolumuz açık,  
gönlümüz rızalıkta ola.

Allah Allah.  
Gerçeğe hû.  
Müminlere rahmet,  
münkirlere hidayet,  
hakka yürüyen canlara rahmet,  
hazır-gaip cümle canlara birlik ola.

Eline sahip ola, haksızlığa uzanmayasın.  
Beline sahip ola, edep yolundan ayrılmayasın.  
Diline sahip ola, yalan ve kırıcı söz söylemeyesin.  
Cem huzuruna, yol edebine, pirlerin rızasına saygı ola;  
mahrem sır mahremde kala, gönül kibirden arına, niyaz gösterişten uzak ola.  
Hak-Muhammed-Ali yolunda rıza, birlik ve muhabbet daim ola.

Hû, Hû, Hû.  
Gerçek erenler demine,  
Hakk-Muhammed-Ali aşkına,  
Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Veli hürmetine,  
Allah eyvallah.  
Hû.

---

## علوية (نصيرية)

نَوَيْتُ الدُّعَاءَ إِلَى اللهِ تَعَالَى فِي شَأْنِ تَيْسِيرِ الْمُقَابَلَةِ وَطَلَبِ الْعَمَلِ، بِقَلْبٍ صَادِقٍ وَنِيَّةٍ سَلِيمَةٍ.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ.

أَشْهَدُ أَنْ لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ، وَأَشْهَدُ أَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا رَسُولُ اللهِ.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ  
الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ  
الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ  
مَالِكِ يَوْمِ الدِّينِ  
إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ  
اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ  
صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ  
غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ  
قُلْ هُوَ اللهُ أَحَدٌ  
اللهُ الصَّمَدُ  
لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ  
وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ.

إِنَّ اللهَ وَمَلَائِكَتَهُ يُصَلُّونَ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ،  
يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا صَلُّوا عَلَيْهِ وَسَلِّمُوا تَسْلِيمًا.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

يَا اللهُ، يَا رَحْمٰنُ، يَا رَحِيمُ، يَا حَيُّ، يَا قَيُّومُ،  
أَسْأَلُكَ بِاسْمِكَ وَرَحْمَتِكَ، وَبِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ،  
أَنْ تُيَسِّرَ أَمْرَ الْمُقَابَلَةِ، وَتَفْتَحَ بَابَ الْخَيْرِ وَالرِّزْقِ الْحَلَالِ،  
وَأَنْ تَجْعَلَ فِي الْقَلْبِ سَكِينَةً، وَفِي الْعَقْلِ صَفَاءً، وَفِي اللِّسَانِ بَيَانًا،  
وَأَنْ تُبْعِدَ الْحَيْرَةَ وَالْخَوْفَ، وَتُقَرِّبَ الْفَهْمَ وَالثِّقَةَ وَحُسْنَ الْجَوَابِ.

اللَّهُمَّ اجْعَلِ الْكَلَامَ مُهَذَّبًا، وَالْحُضُورَ مُطْمَئِنًّا، وَالْقَبُولَ فِيمَا تُحِبُّ وَتَرْضَى،  
وَارْزُقْ لُقْيَا مَنْ يَعْرِفُ الْفَضْلَ وَيُقَدِّرُ الْأَهْلِيَّةَ،  
وَاجْعَلْ هٰذَا السَّعْيَ سَبَبًا لِعَمَلٍ صَالِحٍ، وَرِزْقٍ طَيِّبٍ، وَصُحْبَةٍ حَسَنَةٍ، وَمُنَاسَبَةٍ مُبَارَكَةٍ.

اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّا لَا نَطْلُبُ رِزْقًا بِسَلْبِ رِزْقِ أَحَدٍ،  
وَلَا نَجَاحًا بِظُلْمِ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا رِفْعَةً بِإِضْرَارِ أَحَدٍ،  
وَلٰكِنْ نَسْأَلُكَ مِنْ فَضْلِكَ الْوَاسِعِ، وَقَضَائِكَ الْحَسَنِ، وَهُدَاكَ الْمُسْتَقِيمِ.

اللَّهُمَّ احْفَظْ حُرْمَةَ أَهْلِ الْبَيْتِ،  
وَاجْعَلْ هٰذَا الدُّعَاءَ خَالِصًا لِوَجْهِكَ،  
وَلَا تَجْعَلْ فِيهِ ظُلْمًا وَلَا قَطِيعَةً وَلَا أَذًى.

رَبَّنَا تَقَبَّلْ مِنَّا، إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ.  
وَتُبْ عَلَيْنَا، إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ.

أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ رَبِّي وَأَتُوبُ إِلَيْهِ.

اللَّهُمَّ طَهِّرْ نِيَّتَنَا، وَاسْتُرْ زَلَّتَنَا، وَاجْعَلْنَا مِنْ أَهْلِ الصِّدْقِ وَالْحِلْمِ وَالْوَفَاءِ،  
وَصَلِّ اللَّهُمَّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

---

## സീറോ മലബാർ സഭ

പിതാവിന്റെയും പുത്രന്റെയും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിന്റെയും നാമത്തിൽ. ആമ്മേൻ.

പിതാവിനും പുത്രനും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിനും സ്തുതി.  
ആദിമുതൽ എന്നേക്കും. ആമ്മേൻ.

കർത്താവായ ഈശോമിശിഹായേ, ജ്ഞാനത്തിന്റെയും സമാധാനത്തിന്റെയും നാഥാ,  
വരാനിരിക്കുന്ന തൊഴിൽ അഭിമുഖത്തെയും അതിന്റെ എല്ലാ സാഹചര്യങ്ങളെയും  
അങ്ങയുടെ തിരുമനസ്സിനും കരുണയ്ക്കും സമർപ്പിക്കുന്നു.  
മനസ്സിൽ തെളിമയും ഹൃദയത്തിൽ ധൈര്യവും നാവിൽ സൗമ്യതയും തരണമേ.

ദൈവമേ, പാപിയായ എന്നോടു കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.  
കർത്താവേ, കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.  
മിശിഹായേ, കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.  
കർത്താവേ, കരുണയുണ്ടാകണമേ.

“കർത്താവ് എന്റെ ഇടയനാകുന്നു; എനിക്കൊന്നും കുറവുണ്ടാകയില്ല” എന്ന വിശ്വാസത്തിൽ  
ഈ പ്രത്യേക സന്ദർഭത്തിൽ ഞങ്ങൾ അങ്ങയിൽ ആശ്രയിക്കുന്നു.  
ഭയം കലങ്ങാതെ, അഹങ്കാരം വരാതെ, സത്യവും വിനയവും ചേർന്ന് സംസാരിക്കുവാൻ അനുഗ്രഹിക്കണമേ.

കർത്താവായ ഈശോമിശിഹായേ,  
അഭിമുഖസമയത്ത് ഓർമ്മ തെളിമയോടെ നിലനിൽക്കണമേ;  
ചോദ്യങ്ങൾ ശരിയായി കേൾക്കുവാനും, ഉചിതമായി ഗ്രഹിക്കുവാനും,  
ശാന്തതയോടും വ്യക്തതയോടും കൂടെ മറുപടി പറയുവാനും കൃപ തരണമേ.  
അനുയോജ്യമായ അവസരവും നീതിയുള്ള വിലയിരുത്തലും ലഭിക്കട്ടെ.  
പ്രയത്നം, കഴിവ്, സത്യസന്ധത എന്നിവ നല്ല മനസ്സുള്ളവരുടെ മുമ്പിൽ പ്രകാശിക്കട്ടെ.  
മറ്റൊരാളുടെ നന്മ അപഹരിക്കാതെയും മറ്റൊരാളുടെ അവകാശം കുറയാതെയും,  
അങ്ങയുടെ നീതിയിലും കരുണയിലും യോജിച്ച വഴിയിലേക്ക് നയിക്കണമേ.  
ഈ തൊഴിൽബന്ധം നല്ലതും സമാധാനപരവുമായ അനുയോജ്യമായ വഴിയാകുമെങ്കിൽ തുറക്കണമേ;  
അല്ലെങ്കിൽ അതിലും മെച്ചമായ അങ്ങയുടെ വഴിയിലേക്ക് നടത്തണമേ.

നന്മ നിറഞ്ഞ മറിയമേ, സ്വസ്തി,  
കർത്താവ് അങ്ങയോടുകൂടെ,  
സ്ത്രീകളിൽ അങ്ങ് അനുഗ്രഹിക്കപ്പെട്ടവളാകുന്നു,  
അങ്ങയുടെ ഉദരഫലമായ ഈശോ അനുഗ്രഹിക്കപ്പെട്ടവനാകുന്നു.  
പരിശുദ്ധ മറിയമേ, തമ്പുരാന്റെ അമ്മേ,  
പാപികളായ ഞങ്ങൾക്കുവേണ്ടി  
ഇപ്പോഴും ഞങ്ങളുടെ മരണസമയത്തും  
തമ്പുരാനോടപേക്ഷിക്കണമേ. ആമ്മേൻ.

മാർത്തോമ്മാ ശ്ലീഹായേ, വിശ്വാസത്തിന്റെ സാക്ഷിയേ,  
നല്ല ധൈര്യത്തോടും നേരുള്ള ഹൃദയത്തോടും കൂടെ നടക്കുവാൻ  
ഞങ്ങൾക്കുവേണ്ടി കർത്താവിനോടപേക്ഷിക്കണമേ.

സ്വർഗ്ഗസ്ഥനായ ഞങ്ങളുടെ പിതാവേ,  
അങ്ങയുടെ നാമം പൂജിതമാകണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ രാജ്യം വരണമേ.  
അങ്ങയുടെ തിരുമനസ്സ് സ്വർഗ്ഗത്തിലെപ്പോലെ ഭൂമിയിലും ആകണമേ.  
ഞങ്ങൾക്ക് ആവശ്യമുള്ള ആഹാരം ഇന്ന് ഞങ്ങൾക്ക് തരണമേ.  
ഞങ്ങളുടെ കടക്കാരോട് ഞങ്ങൾ ക്ഷമിക്കുന്നതുപോലെ  
ഞങ്ങളുടെ കടങ്ങൾ ഞങ്ങളോടും ക്ഷമിക്കണമേ.  
ഞങ്ങളെ പ്രലോഭനത്തിൽ ഉൾപ്പെടുത്തരുതേ.  
ദുഷ്ടനിൽ നിന്നു ഞങ്ങളെ രക്ഷിക്കണമേ. ആമ്മേൻ.

Qaddīšā Alāhā,  
Qaddīšā ḥayltānā,  
Qaddīšā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

പിതാവിനും പുത്രനും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിനും സ്തുതി.  
ആദിമുതൽ എന്നേക്കും. ആമ്മേൻ.

കർത്താവായ ഈശോമിശിഹായേ,  
ഈ ഒരുക്കവും പരിശ്രമവും പ്രതീക്ഷയും ഫലവും  
അങ്ങയുടെ പരിശുദ്ധ സ്ലീവായോടും ഉയിർപ്പോടും ചേർത്ത് സമർപ്പിക്കുന്നു.  
ഇത് ഇടപാടോ നിർബന്ധമോ അല്ല;  
അങ്ങയുടെ കരുണയിലും പരിശുദ്ധ തിരുമനസ്സിലും വിശ്വാസത്തോടെ ചെയ്യുന്ന സമർപ്പണമാകുന്നു.  
അങ്ങേക്കു സ്തുതിയും ബഹുമാനവും കൃതജ്ഞതയും  
ഇപ്പോഴും എല്ലായ്പ്പോഴും എന്നേക്കും. ആമ്മേൻ.

പിതാവിന്റെയും പുത്രന്റെയും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിന്റെയും നാമത്തിൽ. ആമ്മേൻ.

---

## 苏菲 Bektashi

Bism-i Şâh, Allâh Allâh.

Niyyet eyledim rızâ-yı Ḥaqq için; iş görüşmesinin hayırla, açıklıkla ve selâmetle geçmesi niyetiyle. Gönül aynası pâk, zihin berrak, söz ölçülü ve rahat ola; takdir eden gözlerle karşılaşıla, nasip olan hayırlı kapı açıla.

Bismi llāhi r-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Al-ḥamdu li-llāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Bismi llāhi r-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Qul huwa llāhu aḥad.  
Allāhu ṣ-ṣamad.  
Lam yalid wa lam yūlad.  
Wa lam yakun lahu kufuwan aḥad.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Sayyidinā Muḥammad.  
Allāhumma bārik ʿalā Sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Sayyidinā Muḥammad.

Lā ilāha illā llāh.  
Muḥammadun rasūlu llāh.  
ʿAlīyun walīyu llāh.

Allāh Allāh Allāh.  
Hū Hū Hū.  
Lā ilāha illā Anta subḥānaka innī kuntu mina ẓ-ẓālimīn.

Bi-ḥurmeti Muḥammed Muṣṭafā.  
Bi-ḥurmeti ʿAlī al-Murtażā.  
Bi-ḥurmeti Fāṭımatü’z-Zehrā.  
Bi-ḥurmeti Ḥasan u Ḥüseyn.  
Bi-ḥurmeti On İki İmām.  
Bi-ḥurmeti Pîr Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Velî.

Bism-i Şâh, Allâh Allâh.  
Niyetimiz Ḥaqq katında kabul ola.  
İş görüşmesi hayra döne; kapılar keremle açıla, yollar erkân ola.  
Hayırlar feth ola, şerler def ola.  
Dil çözük, kalp sakin, akıl uyanık, nefes doğru ola.  
Sözümüz ölçülü, cevabımız açık, hâlimiz edepli ola.  
Gören göz insafla göre, duyan kulak hakkaniyetle duya.  
Kısmetimiz olan hayırlı iş, helâl lokmaya ve güzel hizmete vesile ola.  
Başkasının nasibi eksilmeden, kimsenin rızkı daralmadan, herkesin hakkı korunarak hayır murad ola.  
Dertlere dermân, gönüllere îmân, yollara erkân ola.  
Eline, beline, diline doğruluk ola.  
Meydanımız nurlu, lokmamız helâl, sözümüz gerçek ola.  
Dil bizden, nefes Pîr Hünkâr Hacı Bektaş Velî’den ola.  
Gerçeğe Hû.

Bismi llāhi r-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Al-ḥamdu li-llāhi rabbi l-ʿālamīn.  
Ar-raḥmāni r-raḥīm.  
Māliki yawmi d-dīn.  
Iyyāka naʿbudu wa iyyāka nastaʿīn.  
Ihdinā ṣ-ṣirāṭa l-mustaqīm.  
Ṣirāṭa lladhīna anʿamta ʿalayhim, ghayri l-maghḍūbi ʿalayhim wa lā ḍ-ḍāllīn.  
Āmīn.

Allāhumma ṣalli ʿalā Sayyidinā Muḥammadin wa ʿalā āli Sayyidinā Muḥammad.  
Yā Ḥaqq, gönlümüzü kibirden, dilimizi yalandan, niyetimizi haksızlıktan arıt.  
Eline, beline, diline sahip olmayı bize nasip eyle.  
Allāh Allāh, Hū Hū.  
Gerçeğe Hû.

---

## الداؤودية البهرة

[الطَّهَارَةُ وَالنِّيَّةُ]

اللّٰهُمَّ طَهِّرْ قَلْبِي وَنِيَّتِي، وَاجْعَلْ دُعَائِي خَالِصًا لِوَجْهِكَ الْكَرِيمِ.  
نَوَيْتُ أَنْ أَدْعُوَ اللهَ تَعَالَى لِتَيْسِيرِ مُقَابَلَةِ الْعَمَلِ، وَصَفَاءِ الذِّهْنِ، وَحُسْنِ الْبَيَانِ، وَنَيْلِ الْقَبُولِ وَالرِّزْقِ الطَّيِّبِ، خَالِصًا لِلّٰهِ تَعَالَى.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ٱلْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَالَمِينَ  
ٱلرَّحْمَٰنِ ٱلرَّحِيمِ  
مَٰلِكِ يَوْمِ ٱلدِّينِ  
إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ  
ٱهْدِنَا ٱلصِّرَٰطَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ  
صِرَٰطَ ٱلَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ  
غَيْرِ ٱلْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا ٱلضَّآلِّينَ

اللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

يَا اللهُ، يَا رَحْمٰنُ، يَا رَحِيمُ، يَا كَرِيمُ،  
بِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَبِوَلَايَةِ أَوْلِيَائِكَ الصَّالِحِينَ،  
أَسْأَلُكَ تَيْسِيرَ هٰذَا الأَمْرِ، وَفَتْحَ بَابِ الصِّدْقِ وَالْخَيْرِ.

وَقُلْ رَبِّ أَدْخِلْنِي مُدْخَلَ صِدْقٍ وَأَخْرِجْنِي مُخْرَجَ صِدْقٍ وَاجْعَلْ لِّي مِنْ لَدُنْكَ سُلْطَانًا نَصِيرًا.  
وَقُلْ رَبِّ زِدْنِي عِلْمًا.

اللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلْ لِي فِي الْمُقَابَلَةِ سَكِينَةً وَفَهْمًا،  
وَثَبَاتًا وَحُسْنَ جَوَابٍ،  
وَطَلَاقَةَ لِسَانٍ بِغَيْرِ كِبْرٍ،  
وَوُضُوحَ قَلْبٍ بِغَيْرِ خَوْفٍ،  
وَاجْعَلْنِي أَلْقَى التَّقْدِيرَ الْحَسَنَ وَالنَّظَرَ الْمُنْصِفَ.

اللّٰهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هٰذَا الْعَمَلُ خَيْرًا لِي فِي دِينِي وَدُنْيَايَ وَآخِرَتِي،  
فَيَسِّرْهُ لِي وَبَارِكْ لِي فِيهِ،  
وَإِنْ كَانَ غَيْرَ ذٰلِكَ، فَاصْرِفْهُ عَنِّي بِرَحْمَتِكَ،  
وَافْتَحْ لِي بَابًا أَطْيَبَ وَأَقْرَبَ إِلَى رِضَاكَ.

اللّٰهُمَّ إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ رِزْقًا طَيِّبًا، وَعِلْمًا نَافِعًا، وَعَمَلًا مُتَقَبَّلًا،  
وَلَا أَسْأَلُكَ بِسَلْبِ رِزْقِ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا بِظُلْمِ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا بِضَرَرِ أَحَدٍ،  
بَلْ أَسْأَلُكَ فَضْلًا حَلَالًا طَيِّبًا مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.
