## 祆教 / 琐罗亚斯德教

### —— 1. Khshnaothra ——

Khshnaothra Ahurahe Mazdāo.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 2. Niyyat / Dibache ——

Pa nām i yazdān, Ohrmazd Khodāe awazūnī.

愿求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，谈吐自若，得遇赏识，觅得良缘；所求皆在 Asha 之内，依 humata、hukhta、hvarshta 而成，不夺他人福报，不损他人寿数，不以强迫、操控或伤害成就己愿。

Humata hukhta hvarshta andar Asha.

### —— 3. Kem Na Mazda ——

Kêm-nâ mazdâ mavaitê pâyûm dadå,  
hyat mâ dregvå dîdareshatâ aênanghê,  
anyêm thwahmât âthrascâ mananghascâ,  
ýayå shyaothanâish ashem thraoshtâ ahurâ,  
tãm môi dãstvãm daênayâi frâvaocâ.

Kê verethrem-jâ thwâ pôi sêñghâ ýôi heñtî,  
cithrâ môi dãm ahûmbish ratûm cizhdî,  
at hôi vohû seraoshô jañtû mananghâ,  
mazdâ ahmâi ýahmâi vashî kahmâicît.

Pâta-nô tbishyañtat pairi mazdåsca ârmaitishca speñtasca,  
nase daêvî druxsh, nase daêvô-cithre, nase daêvô-frakarshte, nase daêvô-fradâiti,  
apa druxsh nase, apa druxsh dvâra, apa druxsh vînase, apâxedhre apa-nasyehe,  
mâ mereñcainîsh gaêthå astvaitîsh ashahe,  
nemascâ ýâ ârmaitish îzhâcâ.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 4. Patet / Ahura Mazda Khodāe ——

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, Ahereman awā-dashãn, dur avāz dāshtār, zad shekasteh bād.

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum,  
az harvastīn dushmata duzhukhta duzhvarshta,  
mem pa getī manīd, oem goft, oem kard, oem jast, oem būn būd ested.

Az ān gunāh, manashnī gavashnī kunashnī, tanī ravānī getī minōānī,  
okhe awākhsh pashemān, pa se gavashnī pa patet hom.

### —— 5. Jasa me Avanghe Mazda / Fravarane ——

Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda.

Mazdayasnō ahmī, Mazdayasnō Zarathushtrish fravarānē āstūtascā fravaretascā.  
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  
Āstuyē daēnām vanguhīm Māzdayasnīm,  
fraspāyaokhedhrām, nidhāsnaithishem, khvaētvadathām ashaonīm,  
yā hāitināmchā būshyeintināmchā mazishtāchā vahishtāchā sraēshtāchā,  
yā āhūirish Zarathushtrish.  
Ahurāi Mazdāi vīspā vohū chinahmī.  
Aēshā astī daēnayāo Māzdayasnōish āstūitish.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 6. Yathā / Ashem / Yenghē ——

Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

Yenghē hātām āat yesnē paiti vanghō,  
Mazdāo Ahurō vaēthā ashāt hachā,  
yāonghāmchā tāschā tāschā yazamaidē.

### —— 7. 正行：Warharan / Sraosha ——

Sraoshahe ashyehe, takhmahe, tanu-manthrahe, darshi-draosh ahuiryehe,  
khshnaothra yasnaicha vahmaicha khshnaothraicha frasastayaecha.

Yasnemcha vahmemcha aojascha zavarecha āfrīnāmi,  
Verethraghnahe Ahuradhātahe vanaintyāoscha uparatātō.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 8. Ahmai Raeshcha / Doa Tan-Dorosti ——

Ahmāi raēshcha khvarenanghacha,  
Ahmāi tanvō drvatātem,  
Ahmāi tanvō vazdvārē,  
Ahmāi tanvō verethrem,  
Ahmāi ishtim pourush-khathrem,  
Ahmāi asnāmchit frazantim,  
Ahmāi darekham darekho-jītim,  
Ahmāi vahishtem ahum ashaonām,  
raochanghem vispō-khathrem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

Tandarosti, dorosti, zor, niru, khoreh, awazuni,  
ravāni shād, tan dorost, geti minōānī andar Asha.

Ahmāi raēshcha; Hazanghrem; Jasa me Avanghe Mazda; Kerfeh Mozd.

### —— 9. 回结净护 ——

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum,  
az harvastīn dushmata duzhukhta duzhvarshta,  
okhe awākhsh pashemān, pa se gavashnī pa patet hom.

Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

---

## 混沌魔法（Chaos Magick）

I banish from this working all obsession, confusion, and reflected desire.

Neither-neither.  
I am not this.  
I am not that.  
No belief is true.  
Everything is permitted.

KIA.  
ZOS.  
KIA.  
ZOS.

This is my will:  
The job interview unfolds smoothly; in the moment the mind is clear, the speech is free, the presence is steady, and the right appreciation meets the right opportunity.

This working dispossesses none, diminishes none, and seeks no success by the loss, harm, or deprivation of another.

The sign is made:  
THE CLEAR INTERVIEW SIGN.

The desire is bound into the sign.  
The sign is empty of words.  
The sign is full of will.

IAŌ.  
SABAŌ.  
ABRASAX.  
ZAZAS ZAZAS NASATANADA ZAZAS.  
IAŌ SABAŌ ABRASAX.

By gnosis, by silence, by the death of thought:  
THE CLEAR INTERVIEW SIGN is launched.

It is done.  
It is forgotten.  
It is no longer mine.

HA.  
HA.  
HA.

The working is closed.  
The mask is removed.  
The record remains: one neutral mark, then silence.

I banish again all clinging, all rehearsal, all hunger for result.  
The sign is released to ash, blankness, or sleep.  
The feet return to earth; the breath returns to the body; the name of the day returns to the day.

HA.  
HA.  
HA.

Closed.

## 现代术士派（Cochranian、Sabbatic Craft）

In the name of the Old One,  
Master of the Crooked Path,  
Keeper of the hidden fire,  
I hallow this compass.

By stang, by stone, by thorn, by flame,  
by bone, by blood, by breath, by name,  
let this ring be whole,  
let no false word enter,  
let no oath be broken,  
let no secret be profaned.

Old One, hear the word set within this compass.  
The work is for the appointed meeting of employment:  
may the interview proceed in good order;  
may the mind be clear at the threshold;  
may the tongue speak steadily and freely;  
may honest merit be seen, rightly weighed, and kindly received;  
may a fitting place of work be found,  
without theft of another’s portion,  
without dispossessing another of rightful bread,  
without binding or bending any will.

No stolen oath is spoken here.  
No hidden word is claimed here.  
Only the open charm is set,  
only the rightful prayer is made.

Road before, road behind,  
gate before, gate behind;  
let the way be opened,  
let the appointed work be met,  
let the interview pass in right order  
under clear wit, steady breath, and truthful speech.

Fire in the head, light in the bone,  
the crooked road beneath the feet;  
let confusion fall as chaff,  
let fear be bridled,  
let fitting words rise cleanly,  
let the true sign be known.

Hand to hand, hearth to hearth,  
word to word, and eye to eye;  
let fair regard be given,  
let worthy skill be recognized,  
let the right door open,  
and the wrong door close without harm.

By stang, by stone, by thorn, by flame,  
by bone, by blood, by breath, by name,  
the word is spoken,  
the work is sealed,  
the compass is whole.

Old One, receive thanks.  
If any word has strayed beyond its rightful road,  
let it be withdrawn into silence.  
If any desire has pressed too hard upon another’s will,  
let it be loosed and made harmless.  
Let all names uncalled remain untroubled.  
Let every boundary be restored.

Let the road be shut where it must be shut.  
Let the road be open where it must be open.  
Peace to the ring,  
peace to the dead,  
peace to the living.

So mote it be.

---

## 共济会

Most holy and glorious Lord God,  
the Great Architect of the Universe,  
the Giver of all good gifts and graces:

Thou hast promised that where two or three are gathered together in Thy Name,  
Thou wilt be in the midst of them and bless them.

In Thy Name, and in reverence before Thy presence,  
we place this petition concerning the appointed interview,  
that it may proceed in order, concord, and uprightness.

Grant that every thought, word, and act  
may be ordered by Wisdom,  
supported by Strength,  
and adorned with Beauty.

May the mind be clear at the hour of questioning;  
may speech be calm, truthful, and fitting;  
may anxiety be set aside, and due confidence arise.  
May honest merit be seen, good character be recognized,  
and a suitable vocation be found in peace.

We seek no gain by falsehood, coercion, vanity,  
or by dispossessing another of rightful good;  
but only that the path most just, useful, and honorable  
may be opened according to Thy wise providence.

הִנֵּה מַה־טּוֹב וּמַה־נָּעִים  
שֶׁבֶת אַחִים גַּם־יָחַד׃

Let Brotherly Love, Relief, and Truth  
govern our hearts toward all persons met in this undertaking.  
Let no anger, unlawful gain, false witness,  
or betrayal of trust enter this work.

Direct the labor of this interview  
so that it may be conducted with fairness, clarity, and mutual respect;  
and if this opportunity be rightly fitted,  
let favor, understanding, and good accord attend it.

Keep us faithful to every lawful obligation,  
silent where silence is due,  
truthful where speech is required,  
and charitable toward all mankind.

May the Supreme Grand Master  
preside over this intention,  
until all work is closed in peace.

So mote it be.

---

## 赫密士主义当代社团

[净化与定向]  
Silentio, pietate, mente clara hic sto.  
Non ad nocendum, non ad cogendum, non ad fallendum, non ad auferendum oro.  
Sit haec precatio secundum Unum, Mentem, Verbum, et ordinem divinum.

[向一者与Nous发愿]  
Ad Unum et ad Nous me converto.  
Cedat confusio; redeat recta mens; sermo meus sit sobrius, verax, modestus.  
Non quaero alienam sortem rapere, non honorem alterius minuere, non libertatem cuiusquam violare.

[赫密士感恩祷正行：Asclepius 41]  
Tibi gratias agimus, summe et excellentissime,  
cuius numine solo gubernamur;  
et gratias agimus tibi, qui nos tanto lumine cognitionis inlustrasti.

Sanctum est nomen tuum et honorabile,  
nomen unum, quo solus Deus benedicendus est religione paterna,  
quoniam omnibus paternam pietatem, religionem, amorem  
et quaecumque sunt dulcioris affectus praestare dignatus es.

[陈明所愿]  
In colloquio laboris, adsit claritas mentis, praesentia animi, et libertas sermonis.  
Verba sint apta, responsa tranquilla, iudicium lucidum, memoria ordinata.  
Fiat aestimatio iusta; appareat digna opportunitas; inveniam congruentem locum et bonam coniunctionem, sine iniuria, sine fraude, sine coactione.

[感恩]  
Non impero sacro; supplex tantum aperio cor, audio, et corrigor.  
Gratias ago pro lumine quod docet, pro ordine qui temperat, pro pace quae mentem componit.

[回向与静默]  
Quod bonum, clarum, pium et utile ex hac prece nascitur,  
redeat ad bonum commune, ad iustitiam, ad concordiam, ad divinum ordinem.  
Purificetur intentio; solvatur anxietas; maneat gratitudo.  
Si timor, adhaesio, aut perturbatio surgat, in silentium redeo et simpliciter gratias ago.

Sigē. Nous. Logos. Hen.

---

## Reclaiming（Starhawk）

Ground of being, Earth below and within,  
I center in breath, body, and presence.

By my will, by my breath, by my truth,  
this circle is cast here,  
a boundary of clarity, consent, and love.

East, powers of Air:  
breath, song, thought, and dawn,  
be present in this circle.

South, powers of Fire:  
will, courage, heat, and transformation,  
be present in this circle.

West, powers of Water:  
feeling, dream, grief, and healing,  
be present in this circle.

North, powers of Earth:  
body, root, stone, and bread,  
be present in this circle.

Goddess, immanent one,  
She who is within and around all beings,  
be present in this circle.

Air I am,  
Fire I am,  
Water, Earth, and Spirit I am.

For the job interview soon to be met,  
for clear presence in the moment,  
for speech that flows freely and truly,  
for calm mind, steady heart, and right livelihood,  
for recognition where there is genuine fit,  
and for an opportunity that harms none and dispossesses none,  
I raise this prayer.

She changes everything She touches,  
and everything She touches changes.

Let coercion fall away.  
Let fear be named and released.  
Let power-over be undone.  
Let power-with arise.  
Let this interview be aligned with consent,  
justice, healing, and the freedom of all beings concerned.

Let the gathered will around this event  
rise as a cone of power,  
not to dominate,  
but to

## 东方圣殿骑士团（OTO）

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

I set forth my will in this prayer:  
May the job interview proceed smoothly; may the mind be clear in the moment, the speech poised and natural, the worth of the work be rightly seen, and a fitting opportunity be found under True Will.

I believe in one secret and ineffable LORD; and in one Star in the Company of Stars of whose fire we are created, and to which we shall return; and in one Father of Life, Mystery of Mystery, in His name CHAOS, the sole viceregent of the Sun upon the Earth; and in one Air the nourisher of all that breathes.

A ka dua  
Tuf ur biu  
Bi a'a chefu  
Dudu ner af an nuteru.

Unity uttermost showed!  
I adore the might of Thy breath,  
Supreme and terrible God,  
Who makest the gods and death  
To tremble before Thee:  
I, I adore thee!

Hail unto Thee who art Ra in Thy rising, even unto Thee who art Ra in Thy strength, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Uprising of the Sun.  
Let this interview be aligned with True Will.

May attention be steady, memory ordered, voice measured, and presence bright.  
May appreciation arise without compulsion, and may the right relation between work, skill, and opportunity be revealed.  
May this success seek no dispossession of another, no narrowing of another’s path, and no harm to any will rightly ordered.

There is no part of me that is not of the gods.

APO PANTOS KAKODAIMONOS.  
IO PAN, IO PAN PAN.  
IO ISCHUROS, IO ATHANATOS, IO ABROTOS, IO IAO.  
HAGIOS, HAGIOS, HAGIOS IAO.

Love is the law, love under will.

## 玛丁主义（Martinism）

[静默与十字圣号]

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Seigneur, Dieu éternel, source de toute lumière, de toute justice et de toute miséricorde,  
que notre pensée, notre parole et notre acte soient redressés devant Toi.  
Seigneur Jésus-Christ, Réparateur, que ta paix descende sur cette intention droite :  
que le colloquium laboris se déroule dans l’ordre, la clarté et la paix;  
que l’esprit demeure lucide, que la parole soit simple, vraie et libre;  
que l’entretien rencontre un jugement équitable, une estime juste,  
et, si cela convient à la Providence, une voie professionnelle bonne et proportionnée.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Et secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum, dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.  
Ne proicias me a facie tua,  
et Spiritum sanctum tuum ne auferas a me.  
Redde mihi laetitiam salutaris tui,  
et spiritu principali confirma me.

Asperges me, Domine, hyssopo, et mundabor;  
lavabis me, et super nivem dealbabor.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In principio erat Verbum,  
et Verbum erat apud Deum,  
et Deus erat Verbum.  
Hoc erat in principio apud Deum.  
Omnia per ipsum facta sunt:  
et sine ipso factum est nihil, quod factum est.  
In ipso vita erat,  
et vita erat lux hominum:  
et lux in tenebris lucet,  
et tenebrae eam non comprehenderunt.

Domine Deus, Providentia sancta,  
non quaerimus aliena bona auferre,  
non voluntatem alterius ligare,  
non iniustum lucrum adipisci;  
sed petimus viam rectam, laborem honestum,  
mentem claram, cor pacatum, sermonem temperatum,  
et occursum cum iis qui veritatem, industriam et bonam voluntatem agnoscere possint.

Seigneur Jésus-Christ, Réparateur,  
rétablis en nous l’ordre intérieur;  
que l’inquiétude retourne au silence,  
que la vanité soit purifiée,  
que la crainte soit changée en confiance humble,  
et que la lumière du Verbe éclaire l’heure de l’entretien.  
Fiat voluntas tua.

Pax Domini sit in corde, in ore et in opere.  
Que toute issue soit remise à la justice, à la miséricorde et à la Providence de Dieu.  
Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto:  
sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

---

## Spiritism · Kardecism（凯德克派）

Dieu tout-puissant, souverainement juste et bon,  
que ta volonté soit faite et non la nôtre.  
Si la demande que nous formons est utile à l’âme,  
conforme à ta loi, et propre à servir le bien,  
daigne l’accueillir avec miséricorde.

Notre Père qui êtes aux cieux,  
que votre nom soit sanctifié;  
que votre règne arrive;  
que votre volonté soit faite sur la terre comme au ciel.  
Donnez-nous aujourd’hui notre pain de chaque jour;  
pardonnez-nous nos offenses,  
comme nous pardonnons à ceux qui nous ont offensés;  
ne nous laissez pas succomber à la tentation,  
mais délivrez-nous du mal.  
Ainsi soit-il.

Bons Esprits qui êtes les ministres de Dieu,  
assistez-nous dans l’épreuve présente.  
Anges gardiens, Esprits protecteurs,  
éclairez la pensée, soutenez le courage,  
écartez les pensées mauvaises, l’orgueil, la crainte et la confusion,  
et inspirez ce qui est juste, simple, charitable et conforme à la loi de Dieu.

Seigneur,  
dans l’entretien qui approche, accorde la lucidité nécessaire,  
la mémoire fidèle, la parole calme et naturelle,  
le discernement pour répondre avec sincérité,  
et l’humilité pour recevoir l’issue que ta sagesse permettra.  
Que les bons Esprits aident à voir clairement la voie convenable,  
à rencontrer une appréciation juste,  
et à trouver une occasion de travail honnête, utile et bien accordée.

Mon Dieu, inspirez la meilleure résolution dans cette circonstance.  
Bons Esprits qui protégez,  
aidez à discerner ce qui est conforme à la charité,  
à la justice et à l’humilité.  
Que cette réussite, si elle est accordée,  
ne soit obtenue ni par la tromperie, ni par l’injustice,  
ni au détriment légitime d’autrui;  
qu’elle ne dépouille personne de son bien, de sa paix ou de sa juste place.

Seigneur,  
nous te prions aussi pour toutes les personnes concernées par cette rencontre:  
que leur jugement soit équitable,  
que leurs intentions soient droites,  
et que chacun soit guidé vers ce qui convient le mieux au progrès de son âme.

Ne permets pas que cette prière serve l’orgueil,  
l’intérêt égoïste, la curiosité frivole,  
ni la domination d’aucune créature visible ou invisible.  
Qu’elle soit seulement un acte de foi,  
de confiance, de repentir, de courage moral  
et de soumission à ta volonté.

Donne la force de corriger les défauts,  
de parler avec vérité sans vanité,  
d’accepter sans amertume ce qui sera décidé,  
et de continuer le devoir avec patience, gratitude et bienveillance.

Que tout retourne à Dieu,  
source de justice, de bonté et de lumière.  
Ainsi soit-il.

---

## 玫瑰十字 Lectorium Rosicrucianum

[静默归心]  
Σιωπή.

[承认真实意向]  
在此承认自身的意向：愿求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，谈吐自若，得遇赏识，觅得良缘；愿此事不为强制，不为贪求，不为支配，不为伤害；不夺他人机缘，不损他人福分，不以自我意志压迫任何人的自由判断。  
愿一切偏离真实光明之念，在静默中止息。

[光明呼求]  
Φῶς τοῦ Λόγου, λάμψον ἐν τῇ καρδίᾳ·  
νοῦν καθαρὸν δός, λόγον σώφρονα, εἰρήνην ἐν τῇ ὥρᾳ τῆς συναντήσεως.  
Μὴ τὸ ἐμὸν θέλημα κρατείτω, ἀλλὰ τὸ ἀγαθὸν καὶ ἀληθές φανερούσθω.

[经文正行]  
Ἐν ἀρχῇ ἦν ὁ Λόγος,  
καὶ ὁ Λόγος ἦν πρὸς τὸν Θεόν,  
καὶ Θεὸς ἦν ὁ Λόγος.  
οὗτος ἦν ἐν ἀρχῇ πρὸς τὸν Θεόν.  
πάντα δι’ αὐτοῦ ἐγένετο,  
καὶ χωρὶς αὐτοῦ ἐγένετο οὐδὲ ἕν.  
ὃ γέγονεν ἐν αὐτῷ ζωὴ ἦν,  
καὶ ἡ

---

## 神智学协会

In the name of the One Life, and for the good of the whole human family, this prayer is held concerning the forthcoming job interview: may the occasion proceed smoothly, the mind remain clear, speech be calm and natural, true ability be rightly recognized, and a fitting opportunity be found within right human relations and the Plan of Love and Light.

From the point of Light within the Mind of God  
Let light stream forth into the minds of men.  
Let Light descend on Earth.

May clear perception, steady thought, and wise discernment illumine this event, so that words may be truthful, measured, and timely.

From the point of Love within the Heart of God  
Let love stream forth into the hearts of men.  
May Christ return to Earth.

May goodwill govern the meeting of persons; may appreciation arise without compulsion; may no will be coerced, no place be taken unjustly, and no one be deprived of rightful good.

From the centre where the Will of God is known  
Let purpose guide the little wills of men—  
The purpose which the Masters know and serve.

May the purpose of this interview be aligned with honest work, right livelihood, service, and the unfolding of a proper path.

From the centre which we call the race of men  
Let the Plan of Love and Light work out  
And may it seal the door where evil dwells.

May anxiety, confusion, harmful influence, and self-seeking obstruction be closed away, without hatred, retaliation, or harm to any being.

Let Light and Love and Power restore the Plan on Earth.

May this personal need be held within Light, Love and Power; may success, if rightly granted, serve not only private gain but the wider good; may all outcomes be accepted without coercion, and may the good of the whole human family and of all beings be served.

---

## 瑟勒玛（Thelema）

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

Under the Law of Thelema, in the matter of the coming interview, let this word be set in harmony with True Will.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.

ΣΟΙ, Ὦ ΦΑΛΛΕ, ἸΣΧΥΡΟΣ, ΕΥΧΑΡΙΣΤΟΣ, ΙΑΩ.

ΘΗΡΙΟΝ.

ΝΥΙΤ.

ΒΑΒΑΛΟΝ.

ΑΔΙΤ.

ΙΩ ΠΑΝ.

ΠΡΟ ΜΟΥ ΙΥΓΓΕΣ,  
ΟΠΙΣΩ ΜΟΥ ΤΕΛΕΤΑΡΧΑΙ,  
ΕΠΙ ΔΕΞΙΑ ΣΥΝΟΧΕΣ,  
ΕΠΑΡΙΣΤΕΡΑ ΔΑΙΜΟΝΕΣ,  
ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Hail unto Thee who art Ra in Thy rising, even unto Thee who art Ra in Thy strength, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Uprising of the Sun. Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm. Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Night!

Unity uttermost showed!  
I adore the might of Thy breath,  
Supreme and terrible God,  
Who makest the gods and death  
To tremble before Thee:—  
I, I adore thee!

Appear on the throne of Ra!  
Open the ways of the Khu!  
Lighten the ways of the Ka!  
The ways of the Khabs run through  
To stir me or still me!  
Aum! let it fill me!

May the interview proceed in clarity, poise, and ordered speech; may thought be lucid, tongue be free, presence be steady, and merit be rightly seen. May a fitting opportunity arise in accordance with True Will, without restriction of another star, without dispossessing another, and without seeking gain by the diminution of any other will.

Let this matter be ordered according to True Will, in liberty, balance, and love under will.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.  
ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Love is the law, love under will.

## Spiritualism / NSAC

Infinite Intelligence, God of love, law, and life,  
I come in reverence, in sincerity, and in personal responsibility,  
holding this forthcoming job interview before Thee.

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

I affirm:  
We believe in Infinite Intelligence.  
We believe that the phenomena of Nature, both physical and spiritual,  
are the expression of Infinite Intelligence.  
We affirm that true religion is living in obedience to Nature's Laws.  
We affirm that the existence and personal identity of the individual  
continue after the change called death.  
We affirm that communication with the so-called dead is a fact,  
scientifically proven by the phenomena of Spiritualism.  
We affirm the highest morality contained in the Golden Rule:  
Therefore all things whatsoever ye would that men should do to you,  
do ye even so to them.  
We affirm moral responsibility, and that each soul makes its own happiness  
or unhappiness as it obeys or disobeys Nature's physical and spiritual laws.  
We affirm that the doorway to reformation is never closed  
against any soul here or hereafter.  
We affirm that the precepts of Prophecy and Healing are Divine attributes  
proven through Mediumship.

Infinite Intelligence,  
within Divine Law, truth, compassion, and the welfare of all concerned,  
let this interview be held in light.

愿求职面试一切顺利，临场清明，谈吐自若，得遇赏识，觅得良缘。

Let duty, courage, order, and right timing be present.  
Let the mind be clear, the breath steady, and the speech honest and natural.  
Let preparation bear good fruit, and let every answer be guided by truth, courtesy, and sound judgment.  
Let the interviewer and the applicant meet under the Golden Rule,  
with mutual respect, fair consideration, and freedom from deception or fear.  
May suitable opportunity open according to merit, fitness, and Divine Law.  
I seek no success by dispossessing another, diminishing another’s rightful good,  
or bending any person’s will; let only what is just, honest, and beneficial come to pass.

Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart,  
be acceptable in thy sight, O LORD, my strength, and my redeemer.

May no word spoken here replace conscience, preparation, responsibility, or truth.  
May no spirit, person, or influence be compelled.  
May all be governed by Infinite Intelligence, Divine Love, and Natural Law.

If fear, confusion, or the desire to force an answer should arise,  
bring me back to quiet prayer, to the Lord’s Prayer, to silence, and to personal responsibility.  
Let me seek no compulsory sign and no fearful message,  
but only calmness, right action, and obedience to truth.  
Where practical, legal, financial, medical, or emotional counsel is needed,  
guide me to proper human help, wise judgment, and honest care.

Amen.

---

## 威卡 Dianic

By earth and moon, by breath and flame,  
this place is made sacred.

I cast this circle as a boundary of truth,  
a circle of protection,  
a circle of blessing,  
a circle of the Goddess.

O Diana,  
Bright Lady of the Moon,  
Mother of the wild places,  
Keeper of women’s mysteries,  
be present in this circle.

I stand before you in sincerity.  
I name the matter of this rite:  
may the coming job interview unfold smoothly;  
may the mind be clear in the moment,  
the speech be calm and natural,  
the bearing be steady and true;  
may worthy gifts be seen and fairly recognized,  
and may the right opportunity be found in freedom.

Let this prayer touch only what may be touched in freedom.  
Let it bind no unwilling heart.  
Let it cross no oath-bound door.  
Let it harm none.

O Diana,  
look upon this path of seeking work,  
and upon the meeting, the words, the choices, and the outcome.

Where there is fear, let there be clear boundary.  
Where there is confusion, let there be inner knowing.  
Where there is haste, let there be centered breath.  
Where there is self-doubt, let there be quiet strength.  
Where there is opportunity, let it open rightly.  
Where there is recognition, let it be freely given.  
Where there is a fitting place, let the way become clear.

All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.

I place within this circle  
my attention, my breath, my honest preparation,  
and this prayer offered without bargain.

By the waxing, full, and waning Moon,  
by the dark and returning Moon,  
may what is true be strengthened,  
may what is harmful be dissolved,  
may what belongs to me return to me,  
may what is not mine depart in peace.

For a smooth interview, clear presence, natural speech,  
fair appreciation, and a fitting opportunity,  
I ask blessing, clarity, and right unfolding.

I seek no place by dispossessing another.  
I seek no success by diminishing another’s life, luck, dignity, or freedom.  
May all rightful paths remain open to all.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

O Diana,  
Bright Lady of the Moon,  
I thank you for your presence.  
Cleanse this circle of grasping, fear, and compulsion.  
Let only free blessing remain.  
Let every will be unbound,  
every choice remain its own,  
and every outcome unfold in truth.

Remain if you will,  
depart if you must,  
with blessing between us.

The circle is open,  
but unbroken.  
Merry meet,  
merry part,  
and merry meet again.

---

## 威卡 Alexandrian

I stand within the Circle, in perfect love and perfect trust.  
Let all within this rite be bounded by the Rede:  
An it harm none, do what ye will.

By Air, by Fire, by Water, by Earth,  
this Circle is cast and sealed.  
Between the worlds, and in the presence of the Mighty Ones,  
let this rite be held for a clear, graceful, and fortunate job interview.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

O Goddess,  
Great Mother, Lady of the Moon,  
Listen to the words of the Great Mother.  
Receive this prayer for calm mind, clear presence, and gracious speech.

O God,  
Lord of the Greenwood, Horned One,  
guardian of life, death, and return,  
Receive this prayer for courage, steadiness, and right opportunity.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For the coming interview,  
for clarity in the moment, ease in speech, and a composed heart,  
for being rightly seen, fairly heard, and met with worthy appreciation,  
for finding a fitting path, a good match, and honorable work,  
within right will, right boundary, and harm to none,  
let the prayer be shaped in truth.

I seek not to dispossess another,  
nor to take by force what is not rightly mine;  
may the way open only where it is just, fitting, and free.

So mote it be.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

The Circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.

Blessed be.

If any word has overreached, let it fall away.  
If any desire would bind another will, let it be released.  
By Earth beneath, by breath within, I am grounded and at peace.  
An it harm none, do what ye will.  
So mote it be.

---

## 巴斯克 Sorginak 复兴

Ni naiz nire hitzaren zaindaria.  
Hitz hau nire ahoan, arnasa nire bularrean, lurra nire oinen azpian.

Agur, Mari Anbotoko Dama.  
Agur, Lurraren bihotzeko andrea.  
Entzun nire hitza, entzun nire arnasa.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Iluna behera, argia gora.

Nire eskaria hau da:  
Lan-elkarrizketa ongi joan dadila;  
unean gogoa argi gera dadila;  
nire hitzak bare, zuzen eta neurriz atera daitezela;  
entzuten nauenak nire balioa garbi ikus dezala;  
eta nire bideari dagokion lan-lotura ona aurki dadila.

Gertakari honen inguruan,  
lotura gaiztoa askatu dadila,  
bidea garbi ager dadila,  
hitza zuzen gera dadila,  
beldurra haizeak eraman dezala,  
zalantza urak garbi dezala,  
indarra suak piztu dezala.

Ez dut inoren zoria kendu nahi.  
Ez dut inoren bidea itxi nahi.  
Ez dut inor behartu nahi.  
Niretzat egokia den atea ireki dadila,  
eta besteentzat egokia dena bere tokian gera dadila.

Eguzki amandrea, argitu bidea.  
Ilargi amandrea, gorde isila.  
Lurra, hartu mina.  
Haizea, eraman beldurra.  
Ura, garbitu aztarna.  
Sua, piztu indarra.

Ez dut kalterik nahi.  
Ez dut inor behartu nahi.  
Ez dut gezurrik zin egiten.  
Ez dut sorgin izena gaizki erabiltzen.

Mari Anbotoko Dama,  
nire hitza entzuna izan dadila,  
nire muga gordea izan dadila,  
nire bidea argitua izan dadila.

Kalterik gabe, gezurrik gabe, behartzerik gabe.  
Bihotza garbi, ahoa garbi, bidea garbi.  
Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Hala bedi.

---

## 威卡 Gardnerian

In this place, in this hour, I stand between the worlds,  
with clean hands, clear speech, and a will held in Perfect Love and Perfect Trust.

I conjure thee, O Circle of Power,  
that thou beest a boundary between the world of men and the realms of the Mighty Ones,  
a guardian and a meeting-place for the working of this event:  
a job interview blessed with calm presence, clear mind, graceful speech, fair recognition, and the finding of a right and fitting opportunity.

Lady of the Moon,  
Great Mother, Bright One, Queen of the secret place,  
hear the words spoken within this circle.

Whenever ye have need of anything,  
once in the month, and better it be when the moon is full,  
then shall ye assemble in some desert place,  
or in a forest all together join  
to adore the potent spirit of your queen.

Horned One,  
Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life and death,  
stand apart in thy own power and witness this working.

Before the Lady I speak the need:  
May the interview unfold smoothly; may the mind be lucid, the breath steady, the words natural and well-measured.  
May merit be seen without distortion, may honest effort be recognized, and may the path open toward work that is lawful, fitting, and mutually beneficial.

Before the Lord I speak the boundary:  
Let this prayer bind no will, cloud no judgment, and compel no person.  
Let success come only by truth, readiness, good timing, and right accord.  
Let it dispossess no other, diminish no other’s livelihood, and take no blessing unjustly from another’s hands.

Let this prayer be for clear presence, fair recognition, and right livelihood,  
harming none, binding none against the true will,  
and turning aside all falsehood, fear, and ill-wrought force.

Eko, Eko, Azarak,  
Eko, Eko, Zomelak.

By earth, let this opportunity take lawful root.  
By air, let thought be clear and speech be skillful.  
By fire, let courage be kindled without arrogance.  
By water, let feeling flow in peace and composure.

Lady of the Moon, receive this prayer.  
Horned One, witness this prayer.  
Mighty Ones of the circle, keep it within right measure.

As the cup and the bread are blessed in fellowship,  
so may the work be whole:  
for this interview, for right success,  
according to freedom, consent, truth, and the Rede.

May all excess be grounded into the good earth.  
May all fear be washed away in clean water.  
May all speech be purified by living air.  
May all will be tempered by sacred fire.  
What is not mine to hold, I release; what is rightly mine to learn, I receive.

Lady of the Moon, I thank thee.  
Horned One, I thank thee.  
Mighty Ones of the circle, I thank thee.  
Let no hidden oath be trespassed, no secret thing be taken, no will be constrained.  
Let this be only a plain and open devotion, held in Perfect Love and Perfect Trust.

The circle is open, yet unbroken.  
Merry meet, and merry part, and merry meet again.

---

## Dievturība（拉脱维亚）

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
stāv pie mana ceļa,  
stāv pie mana darba,  
stāv pie šīs sarunas un šī godīgā nodoma.

Dievs, dod man kalnā kāpt,  
Ne no kalna lejiņā;  
Dievs, dod man otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt.

Par šo darba sarunu es saku taisnu vārdu:  
lai mana doma ir skaidra,  
lai mana valoda ir brīva un mierīga,  
lai mans prāts ir klātesošs,  
lai mans darbs ir godīgs,  
lai mans ceļš ir taisns,  
lai es tieku redzēts pēc tikuma, prasmēm un patiesas gribas,  
lai atnāk laba saderība starp darbu un cilvēku,  
lai mana roka nedara pāri nevienam,  
lai mana veiksme neatņem cita daļu un nemazina cita mūžu.

Dod, Dieviņi, otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt;  
Otram devu, sev palika,  
Savu mūžu dzīvojot.

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
pieņem šo vārdu bez spaidiem un bez ļauna nodoma,  
pieņem šo dainu par skaidru prātu, drošu soli un taisnu darbu.  
Lai vārds paliek tīrs,  
lai dziesma paliek godīga,  
lai tikums vada manu ceļu.

Lai top.

---

## 威卡 Eclectic

In perfect love and perfect trust,  
I stand within the circle between the worlds,  
for this event: a job interview,  
seeking clear presence, steady speech, fair recognition,  
and the opening of a fitting and rightful opportunity.

By earth and sea and sky,  
let this circle be cast and sealed.  
What enters here shall enter in truth;  
what leaves here shall leave in peace.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the job interview.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the job interview.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the job interview.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite for the job interview.

Great Mother,  
Listen to the words of the Great Mother,  
who of old was called Artemis, Astarte, Dione, Melusine,  
Aphrodite, Cerridwen, Diana, Arionrhod, Brigid, and by many other names.  
All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.  
Be present to this prayer for the job interview.

Horned One,  
Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life, death, and return,  
be present to this prayer for the job interview.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

Therefore I speak only within willing, rightful, and harmless bounds:  
May the mind be clear in the moment.  
May speech flow calmly, honestly, and well.  
May answers arise with steadiness and good sense.  
May true skill, sincerity, and readiness be seen.  
May fair appreciation be met without coercion.  
May the right door open, if it is rightful and fitting.  
May no one be dispossessed, diminished, or deprived of what is truly theirs.  
Let no will be bound.  
Let no heart be compelled.  
Let no life be diminished.  
Let what is not mine return to its own place.  
Let what is mine stand clear in truth.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For the job interview,  
may the crooked be made clear,  
may the harmful be made harmless,  
may the hidden be known in right measure,  
may the needed path open without coercion.

If any word of this rite has exceeded rightful boundary,  
I withdraw it now.  
If any force has been called beyond consent,  
I release it now.  
If any bond has been made against true will,  
I unmake it now.  
Peace to all beings touched by this prayer.

Great Mother, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Horned One, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

The circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.  
So mote it be.

---

## Finnish Suomenusko

Alku aina, alku aina,  
sana synty, virsi nousi.

Minä sanan lausun,  
hiljaisesta mielestä,  
selvästä sydämestä,  
oikean avun asiassa.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
kuule sanat suustani,  
ota virsi viereltäni.

Mieleni minun tekevi,  
aivoni ajattelevi,  
lähteäni laulamahan,  
saa’ani sanelemahan.

Sanat suustani sulavat,  
puhe’et putoelevat,  
kielelleni kerkiävät,  
hampahilleni hajoovat.

Synty syvä, synty vanha,  
tule tietä myöten tähän,  
näytä juuri, näytä alku,  
näytä oikea omasi.

Ei pahaksi, ei panoksi,  
ei kateeksi, ei kiroukseksi,  
ei toisen onnen ottamiseksi,  
ei kenenkään osan vähentämiseksi,  
vaan oikeaksi avuksi  
työnhaun ja haastattelun asiassa.

Tie edessä avautukoon,  
kynnys lempeästi laskekoon,  
askel olkoon vakaa,  
mieli kirkas, muisti selvä.

Kun kysymys tulee vastaan,  
tulkoon vastaus ajallansa;  
kun sana nousee suuhun,  
nouskoon se suoraan ja sopuisaan.

Puhe olkoon tyyni kuin järvi,  
terävä kuin talven tähti,  
pehmeä kuin kevään tuuli,  
vakaa kuin vanha honka.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
anna apu oikeahan,  
anna rauha rintaan,  
anna suoja matkalle,  
anna sana oikeahan.

Antakoon kuulija arvon,  
näkeköön tekijän taidon,  
tuntekoon työn soveliaaksi,  
löytyköön hyvä kohtaaminen,  
löytyköön oikea paikka,  
löytyköön suotuisa onni.

Mikä on väärin lausuttu,  
se takaisin peräytyköön.  
Mikä on pahoin pantu,  
se omaan sijaansa palatkoon.  
Mikä on oikein sanottu,  
se paikalleen asettukoon.

Mene väki sijallesi,  
mene voima kohdallesi,  
mene sana synnyllesi,  
mene rauha rinnalleni.

Näin sanon, näin sidon,  
sanan suuhun, työn teloille,  
rauhan maahan, valon päälle,  
hyvän osaksi.

Jos sana väärin kääntyi,  
minä sen nyt peruutan.  
Jos voima väärin nousi,  
minä sen nyt nimeän väärinkäytöksi.  
Ei kirousta, ei pakkoa,  
ei pahaa kenenkään päälle.

Palatkaa, väet, omille sijoillenne,  
palatkaa, voimat, oikeille kohdillenne.  
Anteeksi pyydän sanalta,  
anteeksi pyydän väeltä,  
anteeksi pyydän Ukolta yliseltä.

Rauha maahan, rauha mieleen,  
valo tielle, selvyys kieleen.  
Lopussa sana lepää,  
lopussa voima tyyntyy.

---

## 匈牙利 Ősmagyar Vallás

Istenem, Magyarok Istene,  
hallgasd meg e tiszta kérést.

Őseim, apáim és anyáim,  
kik előttem jártatok,  
álljatok mögém tiszta emlékezettel,  
ne ártással, ne haraggal,  
hanem áldással.

Áldjon meg az Isten,  
őrizzen meg az Isten,  
fordítsa jóra az állásinterjú dolgát.

Adjon Isten világosságot az elmébe,  
nyugalmat a szívbe,  
jó mértéket a szóba,  
erős tartást a cselekedetbe.  
Legyen a gondolat tiszta,  
a felelet pontos,  
a beszéd természetes és szabad.

Adjon Isten jó utat e találkozás dolgában.  
Legyen előtte nyitott kapu,  
mögötte békesség,  
mellette jó szándék,  
felette tiszta ég.  
Aki hallgatja, értse meg a jóra való készséget;  
aki mérlegeli, lássa meg a becsületes erőt;  
ami igazán illő munka és jó hely,  
az találjon egymásra rendben és békességben.

Nem kérek más kárából szerencsét,  
nem kérek más kenyerének elvételéből bőséget,  
nem kérek más útjának megrövidítéséből előmenetelt.  
Ami nekem rendelt, jöjjön tisztán;  
ami nem nekem rendelt, menjen békével.

Ami zavaró szó,  
ami kapkodó félelem,  
ami rossz szándék vagy téves gondolat  
e nap köré tapadna,  
az oldódjék el,  
menjen vissza a semmibe,  
ne bántson senkit,  
ne térjen ártással.

Hála az Istennek a lélegzetért,  
hála az ősöknek az emlékezetért,  
hála a kenyérért, a vízért,  
a tűz melegéért és az otthon küszöbéért.

Nem kérek ártást,  
nem mondok hamis esküt,  
nem gyalázom az ősöket,  
nem töröm meg a kenyeret haraggal,  
nem szennyezem a tüzet rossz szóval.  
Tiszta szívvel kérek,  
tiszta úton járok,  
és amit kapok, békességgel fogadom.

Áldás legyen az úton,  
áldás legyen a szóban,  
áldás legyen a döntésben,  
áldás legyen azon, ami igaz és tiszta.

Úgy legyen.  
Áldás, békesség.

---

## Heathenry / Ásatrú

Friðr sé hér.  
Helga ek þenna stað til fríðar ok sannra orða.

Ek kalla á Óðin,  
Alföðr, Hroptatýr, farmagnuðr máls ok manvits,  
heyr orð mín.

Heill dagr, heilir dags synir,  
heil nótt ok nipt!  
Óreiðum augum lítið okkr þinig,  
ok gefið sitjendum sigr.

Ek ber fram góðan hug, skýr orð ok minni heiðarlegt.  
Ek bið um heill í þessu máli:  
at atvinnuviðtal fari vel,  
at hugr sé skýrr á stundu,  
at orð gangi frjáls ok rétt af tungu,  
at verðleikar verði séðir með góðum augum,  
ok at rétt vegamót til góðs starfs finnist.

Málrúnar skaltu kunna,  
ef þú vilt at manngi þér  
heiptum gjaldi harm.

Gef mér mál ok manvit,  
stöðugan hug, frjálsa önd,  
heilar hugsanir, heil orð, heil verk.  
Lát mér mæla satt, hlýtt ok traust,  
eigi með hroka, eigi með blekkingu,  
heldr innan frithar.

Ek bið eigi at taka heill annarra,  
eigi at spilla vegi annars manns,  
eigi at binda vilja þeirra er heyra.  
Lát hindranir víkja án níðs,  
lát rétt mat, rétt orð ok rétt tækifæri koma fram.

Óðinn, tak við þessum orðum sem heiðri,  
eigi sem kaupi, eigi sem eiði.  
Gef sigr í þessu atburði,  
ef það er rétt, heilt ok innan frithar.

Ek geri eigi níð.  
Ek bind eigi vilja annars.  
Ek sver eigi ósannan eið.  
Orð mín standi innan frithar.  
Einn er þessi kviður, einn er sá er kallaðr er.  
Með virðingu, minni ok hófi er þetta mælt.

Svá sé.  
Friðr með oss.

---

## 凯尔特德鲁伊（OBOD / ADF / AODA）

[净化与定界]  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Boed y dŵr hwn yn glanhau’r meddwl,  
boed yr anadl hon yn tawelu’r galon,  
boed y cylch hwn yn cael ei osod mewn heddwch.

[向土地与三界致敬]  
Anrhydedd i’r ddaear dan fy nhraed,  
i’r dyfroedd sy’n llifo,  
i’r gwynt sy’n symud,  
ac i’r tân sy’n goleuo.  
Anrhydedd i’r Byd Uchod, y Byd Canol, a’r Byd Isod.  
Anrhydedd i ysbrydion y lle, mewn parch ac mewn hedd.

[陈明目的]  
Heddiw y mae’r weddi hon dros gyfweliad gwaith:  
boed i’r ffordd agor yn gyfiawn,  
boed i’r meddwl fod yn glir ar y foment,  
boed i’r geiriau ddod yn rhwydd ac yn onest,  
boed i werth gwirioneddol gael ei weld a’i gydnabod,  
a boed i’r cyfle priodol ddod fel cymar da i’r galw a’r gallu.  
Ni cheisiaf niweidio neb, na thorri ewyllys neb,  
na chymryd bendith oddi wrth eraill,  
na difetha cydbwysedd tir, cymuned, na chreaduriaid.

[分别致敬土地灵、祖灵、神明或 Awen]  
Ysbrydion caredig y lle, derbyniwch fy mharch.  
Ancestors, honoured dead, rhai a fu o’n blaenau,  
gwelwch y weddi hon mewn doethineb a heddwch.  
Awen, ffynnon ysbrydoliaeth, disgyn yn dyner:  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[正行：Gweddi'r Derwydd / The Druid's Prayer]  
Dyro, Dduw, dy nawdd;  
Ac yn nawdd, nerth;  
Ac yn nerth, deall;  
Ac yn neall, gwybod;  
Ac yngwybod, gwybod y cyfiawn;  
Ac yngwybod y cyfiawn, ei garu;  
Ac o garu, caru pob hanfod;  
Ac ymhob hanfod, caru Duw;  
Duw a phob daioni.

[供献与请求]  
Gyda dŵr glân, bara neu afal, a diolchgarwch,  
rwy’n gwneud offrwm syml i’r ddaear a’r rhai caredig.  
Nid bargen yw hyn, ond parch;  
nid gorfodaeth yw hyn, ond gweddi.

Boed nawdd dros y daith i’r cyfweliad.  
Boed nerth yn y corff ac yn y llais.  
Boed deall yn clirio’r meddwl rhag ofn a dryswch.  
Boed gwybod y cyfiawn yn arwain pob ateb.  
Boed caru pob hanfod yn cadw’r galon yn deg,  
fel y siaredir â gwirionedd, urddas, a thawel hyder.  
Os yw’r gwaith hwn yn addas, boed iddo agor yn lân;  
os nad yw, boed i’r drws cywirach ymddangos heb golled na chwerwder.  
Ni cheisiaf amddifadu neb o’i le, ei fywoliaeth, na’i fendith;  
boed llwyddiant yn codi mewn cyfiawnder ac mewn hedd.

[静默承接]  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Boed y gair yn glir.  
Boed y galon yn gadarn.  
Boed y ffordd yn deg.

[感谢诸灵]  
Diolch i’r ddaear sy’n fy nal.  
Diolch i’r dyfroedd, y gwyntoedd, a’r tân.  
Diolch i ysbrydion y lle.  
Diolch i’r hynafiaid anrhydeddus.  
Diolch i Awen, ffynnon pob ysbrydoliaeth.

[关闭与回归]  
Mae’r weddi wedi ei llefaru.  
Boed iddi weithio mewn ffordd gyfiawn, garedig, a rhydd.  
Boed pob peth yn dychwelyd i’w le mewn heddwch.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

---

## Maausk（爱沙尼亚）

Tere, püha hiis.  
Tere, püha maa.  
Tere, Maaema.

Seisan siin  
puhta meelega ja rahuliku sõnaga,  
oma tee ja ettevõtmise õnne paludes.

Tere, esivanemad.  
Tere, isade-isade hinged.  
Tere, emade-emade hinged.  
Mäletan teid nimega ja nimeta,  
lähedalt ja kaugelt,  
vere, kodu ja maa kaudu.

Maaema,  
hoia seda teed.  
Püha hiis,  
hoia seda ettevõtmist.  
Esivanemad,  
andke selge meel,  
andke õiged sõnad,  
andke kindel süda.

Tulgu hea tee ja õige aeg.  
Tulgu töövestlusel rahulik meel,  
selge mõte,  
vaba ja aus sõna,  
sirge selg ja tasane hing.  
Tulgu kuuljad, kes märkavad oskust ja head tahet.  
Tulgu sobiv töö, sobiv koht ja hea kokkusaamine,  
kui see on kooskõlas maa, vee, tule ja tuulega.

Ma ei palu teise leiba ära võtta,  
ma ei palu teise õnne vähendada,  
ma ei palu teise eluiga lühendada.  
Tulgu oma õige osa õigel ajal,  
ausalt ja rahuga.

Taara avita.  
Taara avita.  
Taara avita.

Katkegu kuri sõna,  
vaibugu halb tahe,  
lahkugu võõras vari.  
Olgu meel puhas,  
olgu keel selge,  
olgu süda tugev,  
olgu samm kindel.

Maa all rahu.  
Maa peal rahu.  
Taeva all rahu.  
Kodus rahu.  
Südames rahu.

Mis on antud, olgu puhas.  
Mis on öeldud, olgu aus.  
Mis on palutud, olgu kooskõlas maa, vee, tule ja tuulega.

Kui sõna on eksinud,  
siis puhastugu see vaikuses.  
Kui mõte on läinud liiale,  
siis pöördugu see tagasi rahusse.  
Kui tegu on olnud kohatu,  
siis saagu see parandatud puhta meelega.

Tänu, püha hiis.  
Tänu, püha maa.  
Tänu, Maaema.  
Tänu, esivanemad.

Taara avita.  
Nõnda olgu.

---

## Hellenismos / YSEE

[Καθαρμός]  
Χέρνιψ· καθαρῶς προσέρχομαι.  
Ἔστω τὸ σῶμα καθαρόν, ὁ νοῦς σώφρων, ἡ γλῶσσα ἀληθής.

[Ἐπίκλησις]  
Κλῦθί μου, ὦ Ἑρμῆ, Διὸς καὶ Μαίας υἱέ, ἄγγελε ἀθανάτων, πομπαῖε, λόγων καὶ ὁδῶν προστάτα.  
Ἵλαθι καὶ δέξαι τήνδε εὐχήν.

[Ὕμνος]  
Ὁμηρικὸς Ὕμνος ΙΗ΄ εἰς Ἑρμῆν.  
Χαῖρε, Ἑρμῆ, διάκτορε, δωτὴρ ἐάων.

[Προσφορά]  
Ὦ Ἑρμῆ, δέξαι θυμίαμα καθαρὸν καὶ σπονδὴν ὕδατος ἢ οἴνου καθαροῦ·  
σπονδὴν καὶ θυμίαμα ἐν εὐσεβείᾳ προσφέρω, οὐκ ἐμπορίᾳ, οὐδὲ ἀνάγκῃ.

[Εὐχή]  
Χαῖρε, Ἑρμῆ.  
Δὸς εὔοδον τὴν τῆς ἐργασίας συντυχίαν·  
δὸς νοῦν σαφῆ, μνήμην ἑδραίαν, λόγον εὔρυθμον, παρρησίαν σώφρονα, καὶ χάριν ἐν ὄψει τῶν κρινόντων.  
Ἄγε πρὸς ἀγαθὴν εὐκαιρίαν καὶ πρὸς ἔργον ἁρμόζον, ἔνθα ἀρετὴ, τέχνη καὶ δίκη τιμῶνται.  
Μὴ ἀφαιρεθῇ ἄλλων ἀγαθόν, μὴ βλαβῇ τις, μὴ γένηται ἀδικία·  
ἀλλὰ γενέσθω τὸ συμφέρον κατὰ κόσμον, κατὰ δίκην, καὶ μὴ παρὰ θέμιν.

[Χάρις]  
Χάριν σοι ἔχω, ὦ Ἑρμῆ.  
Φύλασσε ἐν εὐσεβείᾳ, σωφροσύνῃ καὶ δίκῃ.  
Καθαρὸν τὸ τέλος, καθαρὰ ἡ διάνοια, καθαρὸς ὁ λόγος·  
δέξαι τὴν τιμὴν καὶ τὴν εὐχὴν ἄβλαβον.  
Χαῖρε, Ἑρμῆ, καὶ αὖθις χαῖρε.

---

## Kemetism

ỉw=ỉ r ḏd mdw m mꜣꜥt.  
ỉb=ỉ wꜥb, r=ỉ mꜣꜥ, ḏrt=ỉ wꜥbt.  
n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḥḏ ḥtpw nṯrw.  
n ỉnk šd mꜣꜥt.  

dwꜣ Rꜥ.  
dwꜣ Rꜥ m wbn=f m ꜣḫt.  
ỉꜣw n=k, Rꜥ, nb pt, nb ꜣḫt, nb wbn.  
di=k mꜣꜥt r st=s, di=k ḥtp r ỉb=ỉ.  

ḥtp dỉ nsw Rꜥ nb ꜣḫt.  
dỉ=f prt-ḫrw:  
t ḥnqt, kꜣw ꜣpdw, šs mnḫt,  
snṯr mrḥt, ḫt nb(t) nfr(t) wꜥb(t),  
n kꜣ=ỉ.  

ỉb=ỉ n mwt=ỉ,  
ỉb=ỉ n ḫprw=ỉ,  
m ḏd r=ỉ m mꜣꜥty,  
m ỉr ḫft r=ỉ m-bꜣḥ nṯr ꜥꜣ.  
ỉb=ỉ n mwt=ỉ,  
m ḫsf r=ỉ m ḏꜣḏꜣt.  

n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḏd grg.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n nṯr.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n ꜣḫ.  
n ỉnk ḥtm rn.  
n ỉnk sḫm r ḏrt ḫft mꜣꜥt.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ špss n ky.  
n ỉnk ḫsf ꜥnḫ n ky.  

m hrw pn n mdw m-bꜣḥ srw,  
di=k sšꜣ ỉb=ỉ, wꜣḥ r=ỉ, ḏd mdw m ḥtp.  
di=k mꜣꜥ ḫrw n r=ỉ, ḥswt m ḥr=sn.  
di=k wꜣt nfrt, st nfrt, šzp nfr m mꜣꜥt.  
di=k gm=ỉ sp nfr, ḥmt nfrt, ḏsr nfr m šms mꜣꜥt.  

di=k wꜣḏ ỉb, snb ẖt, ḥtp pr, mꜣꜥ ḫrw.  
di=k wḏꜣ, snb, ꜥnḫ m mꜣꜥt.  

ḥtp dỉ nsw Rꜥ nb ꜣḫt.  
dỉ=f ḥtp n nṯrw, ḥtp n ꜣḫw,  
prt-ḫrw t ḥnqt, snṯr mrḥt,  
ḫt nb(t) nfr(t) wꜥb(t),  
m rn nfr, m ỉb wꜥb, m mdw mꜣꜥ.  

dwꜣ Rꜥ.  
mꜣꜥt rꜥ nb.  
ḥtp n nṯrw, ḥtp n ꜣḫw,  
ḥtp n kꜣ=ỉ,  
mꜣꜥ ḫrw.
